[줄 2] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - In ships designed with a rake of keel the waterline on which this length is measured is taken parallel to the design waterline.
[줄 3] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Molded dimensions are often referred to; these are taken to the inside of plating on a metal ship.
[줄 4] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Base Line : A horizontal line drawn at the top of the keel plate.
[줄 5] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - All vertical molded dimensions are measured relative to this line.
[줄 6] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - Molded Beam : Measured at the midship section, this is the maximum molded breadth of the ship.
[줄 7] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - Molded Draft : Measured from the base line to the summer load line at the midship section.
[줄 8] [95.2%] (20/21) ✅ 유지 - Molded Depth : Measured from the base line to the heel of the upper deck beam at the ship's side amidships.
[줄 9] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - Extreme Beam : The maximum beam taken over all extremities.
[줄 10] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Extreme Draft : Taken from the lowest point of keel to the summer load line.
[줄 11] [100.0%] (5/5) ✅ 유지 - Draft marks represent extreme drafts.
[줄 12] [94.1%] (16/17) ✅ 유지 - Extreme Depth : Depth of vessel at ship's side from upper deck to lowest point of keel.
[줄 13] [92.6%] (25/27) ✅ 유지 - Half Breadth : Since a ship's hull is symmetrical about the longitudinal centre line, often only the half beam or half breadth at any section is given.
[줄 14] [88.9%] (16/18) ✅ 유지 - The vertical distance measured at the ship's side between the summer load line and the freeboard deck.
[줄 15] [94.3%] (33/35) ✅ 유지 - The freeboard deck is normally the uppermost complete deck exposed to weather and sea that has permanent means of closing all openings, and below which all openings in the ship's side have watertight closings.
[줄 16] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Sheer : A rise in the height of the deck in the longitudinal direction.
[줄 17] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Measured as the height of deck at side at any point above the height of deck at side amidships.
[줄 18] [100.0%] (7/7) ✅ 유지 - Curvature of decks in the transverse direction.
[줄 19] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Measured as the height of deck at center above the height of deck at side.
[줄 20] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Straight line camber is used on many large ships to simplify construction.
[줄 21] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Rise of Floor : The rise of the bottom shell plating line above the base line.
[줄 22] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - This rise is measured at the line of molded beam.
[줄 23] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - Large cargo ships often have no rise of floor.
[줄 24] [95.8%] (23/24) ✅ 유지 - Half Siding of Keel : The horizontal flat portion of the bottom shell measured to port or starboard of the ship's longitudinal center line.
[줄 25] [88.9%] (8/9) ✅ 유지 - This is a useful dimension to know when drydocking.
[줄 26] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - Tumblehome : The inward curvature of the side shell above the summer load line.

[줄 28] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - The outward curvature of the side shell above the waterline.
[줄 29] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - It promotes dryness and is therefore associated with the fore end of ship.
[줄 30] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Stem Rake : Inclination of the stem line from the vertical.
[줄 31] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Keel Rake : Inclination of the keel line from the horizontal.

[줄 37] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Nondestructive testing For obvious reasons some form of nondestructive test is required to enable the soundness of ship welds to be assessed.
[줄 38] [89.5%] (17/19) ✅ 유지 - The various available nondestructive testing methods may be summarized as follows: Visual examination Dye penetrant Magnetic particle Radiographic Ultrasonic.
[줄 39] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - Of these five methods, the dye penetrant and magnetic particle tests have few applications in ship hull construction, being used for examining surface cracks in stern frames and other castings.
[줄 40] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - Visual, radiographic, and ultrasonic examinations are considered in more detail, as they are in common use.
[줄 41] [92.6%] (25/27) ✅ 유지 - Magnetic particle testing is carried out by magnetizing the casting and spreading a fluid of magnetic particles e.g iron fillings suspended in paraffin on the surface.
[줄 42] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Any discontinuity such as a surface crack will show up as the particles will concentrate at this point where there is an alteration in the magnetic field.
[줄 43] [96.0%] (24/25) ✅ 유지 - A dye penetrant will also show up a surface flaw if it remains after the casting has been washed following the application of the dye.
[줄 44] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - To aid the detection of a surface crack the dye penetrant used is often luminous and is revealed under an ultraviolet light.
[줄 45] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Visual inspection of welds is routine procedure, and surface defects are soon noticed by the experienced inspector and surveyor.
[줄 46] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - Incorrect bead shape, high spatter, undercutting, bad stop and start points, incorrect alignment, and surface cracks are all faults that may be observed at the surface.
[줄 47] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Subsurface and internal defects are not observed, but the cost of visual inspection is low, and it can be very effective where examination is made before, during, and after welding.
[줄 48] [96.0%] (24/25) ✅ 유지 - The principle of radiographic inspection is simply to subject a material to radiation from one side, and record the radiation emitted from the opposite side.
[줄 49] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Any obstacle in the path of the radiation will affect the radiation density emitted and may be recorded.
[줄 50] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - As radiation will expose photographic plate, for all practical weld test purposes this is used to record the consistency of the weld metal.
[줄 51] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - The photographic plate records changes in radiation density emitted; for example, a void will show up as a darker shadow on the radiograph.
[줄 52] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - Either X-ray or gamma-ray devices may be used to provide the source of radiation.
[줄 53] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - X-ray equipment consists of a high-voltage power source, which is used to provide potential between a cathode and target anode in a glass vacuum tube.
[줄 54] [96.2%] (25/26) ✅ 유지 - Only a small percentage of this energy is converted to X-rays, so that large amounts of heat have to be conducted away from the target.
[줄 55] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - From the target the X-rays are projected out of the tube onto the weld surface.
[줄 56] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Where gamma-ray devices are used ray emission is produced by decay of a radioactive nucleus, the rate of emission being reduced with time.
[줄 57] [88.9%] (16/18) ✅ 유지 - The radiation given off may be magnetically separated into three parts, a -rays, b -rays and g -rays

[줄 61] [92.3%] (24/26) ✅ 유지 - the g -rays being similar to X-rays and of most importance since they are very penetrating, but this also means that heavy shielding is required.
[줄 62] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Since natural radioactive sources are in short supply, great use is made of artificial radioactive sources, namely isotopes.
[줄 63] [95.0%] (19/20) ✅ 유지 - To interpret the weld radiograph a large amount of experience is required, and a sound knowledge of the welding process.
[줄 64] [95.2%] (20/21) ✅ 유지 - Radiographs usually carry the image of an 'image quality indicator', which shows the minimum change of thickness revealed by the technique.
[줄 65] [93.9%] (31/33) ✅ 유지 - This image quality indicator may have graded steps of metal, each step being identified on the radiograph so that the minimum step thickness discernible is noted and the sensitivity of the radiograph assessed.
[줄 66] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - This indicator is placed adjacent to the weld prior to taking the radiograph.
[줄 67] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - Ultrasonic energy is commonly used as a tool for locating defects in welds, and has several advantages over radiography, particularly as no health hazard is involved.
[줄 68] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - The technique is particularly useful for locating fine cracks that are often missed by radiography, particularly where they lie perpendicular to the emission source.
[줄 69] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - The principle of ultrasonic inspection depends on the fact that pulses of ultrasonic energy are reflected from any surface that they encounter.
[줄 70] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Ultrasonic waves traveling through a plate may be reflected from the surface of the metal and also from the surfaces of any flaws that exist in the metal.
[줄 71] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Virtually total reflection occurs at an air–metal interface, and therefore to get the ultrasonic wave into the metal a liquid is placed between the source and metal.
[줄 72] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - The pattern of reflection is revealed on a cathode ray tube, which may be calibrated using a standard reference block.
[줄 73] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - An experienced operator is able to recognize flaws from the cathode ray tube display, and to some extent recognition of defect types is possible.
[줄 74] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Apart from weld inspection, ultrasonic techniques are valuable for assessing the thickness of structural members.
[줄 75] [92.6%] (25/27) ✅ 유지 - Classi fi cation society weld tests Classification societies specify a number of destructive tests that are intended to be used for initial electrode and weld material approval.
[줄 76] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - These tests are carried out to ascertain whether the electrode or wire-flux combination submitted is suitable for shipbuilding purposes in the category specified by the manufacturer.
[줄 77] [93.8%] (30/32) ✅ 유지 - Tests are made for conventional electrodes, deep penetration electrodes, wire-gas and wire-flux combinations, consumables for electro-slag and electro-gas welding, and consumables for one-sided welding with temporary backing.
[줄 78] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Tensile, bend, and impact tests are carried out on the deposited weld metal and welded plate specimens.
[줄 79] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Other tests are made for the composition of the weld metal deposited and possible cracking.
[줄 80] [94.9%] (37/39) ✅ 유지 - All works where electrodes, wire-flux and wire-gas combinations, consumables for electro-slag and electro-gas welding, and consumables for one-sided welding with temporary backing are produced, and have been initially approved, are subject to annual inspection.

[줄 155] [83.3%] (5/6) ✅ 유지 - FEU is forty-foot equivalent unit.
[줄 156] [83.8%] (31/37) ✅ 유지 - An indication of the size by capacity of oil tankers, bulk carriers, and container ships is often given by the following types: Oil tankers ULCC is a tanker usually between 300,000 and 550,000 tonnes deadweight.
[줄 157] [57.1%] (8/14) ❌ 제거 - VLCC is a tanker usually between 200,000 tonnes and 300,000 tonnes deadweight.
[줄 158] [81.0%] (17/21) ✅ 유지 - Suezmax indicates the largest oil tanker that can transit the current Suez Canal fully laden, being about 150,000 tonnes deadweight.
[줄 159] [91.7%] (22/24) ✅ 유지 - Aframax the standard designation of smaller crude oil tankers, being the largest tanker size in the AFRA Freight Rate Assessment Scale Large One Category.
[줄 160] [85.7%] (6/7) ✅ 유지 - AFRA stands for 'American Freight Rate Association'.
[줄 161] [54.5%] (6/11) ❌ 제거 - Variously reported as being 80,000 to 115,000 tones deadweight.
[줄 162] [88.6%] (31/35) ✅ 유지 - Panamax is the maximum size of oil tanker, with beam restriction of 32.2 meters and length restriction of 275 meters, that can transit the Panama Canal prior to completion of the planned new locks.
[줄 163] [50.0%] (5/10) ❌ 제거 - Typical size is about 55,000–70,000 tonnes deadweight.
[줄 164] [50.0%] (7/14) ❌ 제거 - Handysize/Handymax are typical product tankers of about 35,000–45,000 tonnes deadweight.
[줄 165] [95.0%] (19/20) ✅ 유지 - Bulk carriers Capesize ships that are too large to transit the current Panama Canal and therefore voyage around Cape Horn.
[줄 166] [75.0%] (9/12) ✅ 유지 - All bulk carriers above 80,000 tonnes deadweight fall into this category.
[줄 167] [76.0%] (19/25) ✅ 유지 - Most are up to 170,000 tonnes deadweight but a small number are larger for specific trade routes, the biggest being 365,000 tonnes deadweight.
[줄 168] [75.0%] (3/4) ✅ 유지 - PanamaxAs for oil tankers.
[줄 169] [50.0%] (6/12) ❌ 제거 - Handymax ships are between around 35,000 and 60,000 tonnes deadweight.
[줄 170] [73.9%] (17/23) ✅ 유지 - Ships between 10,000 and 35,000 tonnes deadweight have formed the majority of the fleet for many years and are designated 'Handysize'.
[줄 171] [95.8%] (23/24) ✅ 유지 - In recent years the size of these ships has been increasing and the term 'Handymax' has been applied to designate the larger bulk carriers.
[줄 172] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - The site includes virtual shipyard tours explaining the process used.

[줄 177] [71.4%] (5/7) ✅ 유지 - Further reading 134 Some useful websites 134
[줄 178] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - In order to produce a ship, it is necessary to develop the initial structural and arrangement design into information usable by production.
[줄 179] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - While the initial design is focused on the operation of the ship once completed, production requires information in a form that relates to the manufacturing, assembly, and construction processes.
[줄 180] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Historically, this was done by creating a full-size model of the structure, in the mold loft, from which dimensions could be lifted and templates could be made.
[줄 181] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - The relatively simple outfitting of early ships was carried out on the completed ship structure with pipes and other connectors run where space was available.
[줄 182] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Larger, more complex ships, faster construction times and cost have made this process obsolete, and it has largely been replaced by computer modeling.
[줄 183] [92.6%] (25/27) ✅ 유지 - This chapter briefly outlines the original functions of the ship drawing office and subsequent full or 10:1 scale lofting of the hull and its structural components.
[줄 184] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - It then concentrates on current use by shipyards of computer-aided design for these purposes and the extensive use of computer-aided manufacturing in shipbuilding.
[줄 185] [96.2%] (25/26) ✅ 유지 - In the past, the shipyard design office defined the principal ship dimensions, the scantlings for all major structure, specified major equipment, and satisfied all salutatory requirements.
[줄 186] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - The drawing office developed the design by creating drawings that identified piece parts and critical dimensions.
[줄 187] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - The mold loft then defined the detailed, accurate geometry to manufacture hull piece parts for the ship structure and other trades defied the geometry for their own products, for example pipes and ventilation trunking.
[줄 188] [100.0%] (3/3) ✅ 유지 - All rights reserved.
[줄 189] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - The planning of production, the flow of material through the manufacturing stages, and the sequence of unit erection in the dock or slipway were determined by the production management.
[줄 190] [60.0%] (3/5) ✅ 유지 - Ship drawing of fi ce
[줄 191] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - The ship drawing office was traditionally responsible for producing detailed working structural, general arrangement, and outfit drawings for a new ship.
[줄 192] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - It was also common practice for the drawing office to contain a material ordering department that would identify the necessary material requirements from the drawings and progress them.
[줄 193] [94.9%] (37/39) ✅ 유지 - Structural drawings prepared by the drawing office would be in accordance with Lloyd's or other classification society rules and subject to their approval; also, owner's additional requirements and standard shipyard practices would be incorporated in the drawings.
[줄 194] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - General arrangements of all the accommodation and cargo spaces and stores would also be prepared, incorporating statutory requirements as well as any shipowner's requirements and standards.
[줄 195] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Outfit plans including piping arrangements, ventilation and air-conditioning, rigging arrangements, furniture plans, etc were also prepared.
[줄 196] [92.9%] (13/14) ✅ 유지 - Two plans of particular significance were the ship's 'lines plan' and 'shell expansion'.
[줄 197] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Lines plan A preliminary version of this was, in effect, prepared at the time of the conceptual design to give the required capacity, displacement, and propulsive characteristics.
[줄 198] [92.3%] (24/26) ✅ 유지 - It was subsequently refined during the preliminary design stage and following any tank testing or other method of assessing the hull's propulsive and seakeeping characteristics.
[줄 199] [92.0%] (23/25) ✅ 유지 - The lines plan is a drawing, to a suitable scale, typically 1:100, of the molded lines of the vessel in plan, profile, and section.
[줄 200] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - Transverse sections of the vessel at equally spaced stations between the after and forward perpendiculars are drawn to form what is known as the body plan.
[줄 201] [95.0%] (19/20) ✅ 유지 - Usually, 10 equally spaced sections are selected with half ordinates at the ends where a greater change of shape occurs.
[줄 202] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - A half transverse section only is drawn since the vessel is symmetrical about the center line, and forward half sections are drawn to the right of the center line with aft half sections to the left.
[줄 203] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Preliminary body plans are drawn initially to give the correct displacement, trim, capacity, etc. and must be laid off in plan and elevation to ensure fairness of the hull form.
[줄 204] [97.3%] (36/37) ✅ 유지 - When the final faired body plan is available the full lines plan is completed, showing also the profile or sheer plan of the vessel and the plan of the waterline shapes at different heights above the base.
[줄 205] [77.8%] (7/9) ✅ 유지 - A lines plan is illustrated in Figure 12.1.
[줄 206] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - The lines of the lateral sections in the sheer plan as indicated are referred to as 'bow lines' forward and 'buttock lines' aft.
[줄 207] [75.0%] (9/12) ✅ 유지 - Bilge diagonals would be drawnwith 'offsets'taken along thebilge diagonal to checkfairness.
[줄 208] [94.1%] (32/34) ✅ 유지 - When the lines plan was completed manually the draughtsmen would compile a 'table of offsets', i.e a list of half breadths, heights of decks and stringer, etc. at each of the drawn stations.
[줄 209] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - These 'offsets' and the lines plan were then passed to
[줄 210] [66.7%] (6/9) ✅ 유지 - loftsmen for full-size or 10:1 scale fairing.
[줄 211] [100.0%] (35/35) ✅ 유지 - Since the original lines plan was of necessity to a small scale, which varied with the size of ship, the offsets tabulated from widely spaced stations and the fairing were not satisfactory for building purposes.
[줄 212] [88.5%] (23/26) ✅ 유지 - The offsets used for building the ship would subsequently be lifted by the loftsman from the full size or 10:1 scale lines for each frame.
[줄 213] [100.0%] (39/39) ✅ 유지 - Three-dimensional representation of shell plating When preparing the layout and arrangement of the shell plating at the drawing stage, it was often difficult to judge the line of seams and plate shapes with a conventional two-dimensional drawing.
[줄 214] [96.9%] (31/32) ✅ 유지 - Shipyards therefore made use of a 'half block model', which was in effect a scale model of half the ship's hull from the center line outboard, mounted on a base board.
[줄 215] [92.9%] (26/28) ✅ 유지 - The model was either made up of solid wooden sections with faired wood battens to form the exterior, or of laminated planes of wood faired as a whole.
[줄 216] [97.1%] (34/35) ✅ 유지 - Finished with a white lacquer, the model was used to draw on the frame lines, plate seams and butts, lines of decks, stringers, girders, bulkheads, flats, stem and stern rabbets, openings in shell, bossings, etc.
[줄 217] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - Shell expansion The arrangement of the shell plating taken from a three-dimensional model may be represented on a two-dimensional drawing referred to as a shell expansion plan.
[줄 218] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - All vertical dimensions in this drawing are taken around the girth of the vessel rather than there being a direct vertical projection.
[줄 219] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - This technique illustrates both the side and bottom plating as a continuous whole.
[줄 220] [84.6%] (11/13) ✅ 유지 - In Figure 12.2 a typical shell expansion for a tanker is illustrated.
[줄 221] [93.3%] (28/30) ✅ 유지 - This also shows the numbering of plates and lettering of plate strakes for reference purposes, and illustrates the system where strakes 'run out' as the girth decreases forward and aft.
[줄 222] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - This drawing was often subsequently retained by the shipowner to identify plates damaged in service.
[줄 223] [100.0%] (39/39) ✅ 유지 - However, a word of caution is necessary at this point because since prefabrication became the accepted practice any shell expansion drawing produced will generally have a numbering system related to the erection of fabrication units rather than individual plates.
[줄 224] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Therefore, single plates were often marked in sequence to aid ordering and production identification.
[줄 225] [50.0%] (3/6) ❌ 제거 - Loftwork following drawing of fi ce
[줄 226] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - The mold loft in a shipyard was a large covered wooden floor area suitable for laying off ship details at full size.
[줄 227] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - The loft was usually located above the major hull steel workshops, hence the term 'loft', and the practice originally derived from wooden shipbuilding.
[줄 228] [93.3%] (28/30) ✅ 유지 - When the loftsmen received the scale lines plan, and offsets from the drawing office, the lines would be laid off on the mold loft floor full size and then faired.
[줄 229] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Fairing was achieved by using wooden battens that were bent to follow the offsets
[줄 230] [16.0%] (4/25) ❌ 제거 - L K J Side Bilge Sheerstrake plating plating H G F E D1 D2 D3 D4 D5 C1 C9 B11 B10 B9 B8 B7 B6
[줄 231] [70.7%] (29/41) ✅ 유지 - Bottom A plating Keel plate FRAMING, STRINGERS, DECKS AND OPENINGS IN SIDE SHELL ARE ALSO SHOWN ON THE SHELL EXPANSION BUT HAVE BEEN OMITTED FOR CLARITY B5 B4 B3 C8 C7 C6 C5 C4 C3 C2 Figure 12.2 Shell expansion.
[줄 232] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - then held in place while the fair curve was inscribed on the wooden floor.
[줄 233] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - This would mean using a great area of floor, even though a contracted sheer and plan were normally drawn, and aft and forward body lines were laid over one another.
[줄 234] [90.0%] (18/20) ✅ 유지 - Body sections were laid out full size as they were faired to form what was known as a 'scrieve board'.
[줄 235] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - The scrieve board was used for preparing 'set bars' and bevels for bending frames and for making templates and moldings for plates that required cutting and shaping.
[줄 236] [100.0%] (35/35) ✅ 유지 - Shell plates were developed full size on the loft floor and wooden templates made so that these plates could be marked and cut to the right shape before fitting to the framing on the berth.
[줄 237] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - The mold loft in effect produced an accurate, full-scale, three-dimensional model of the ship from which production information for the structure could be obtained.
[줄 238] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - However, the process was labor intensive and relatively slow, and therefore expensive.
[줄 239] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Shipbuilders in Europe, where labor costs were higher, began development of alternative methods to develop production information.
[줄 240] [75.0%] (15/20) ✅ 유지 - 10:1 scale lofting In the late 1950s the 10:1 lofting system was introduced and was eventually widely adopted.
[줄 241] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - This reduced the mold loft to a virtual drawing office and assisted in the introduction of production engineering methods.
[줄 242] [64.7%] (11/17) ✅ 유지 - Lines could be faired on a 10:1 scale and a 10:1 scale scrieve board created.
[줄 243] [88.9%] (16/18) ✅ 유지 - Many yards operated a flame profiling machine that used 10:1 template drawings to control the cutting operation.
[줄 244] [100.0%] (41/41) ✅ 유지 - In preparing these template drawings the developed or regular shape of the plates was drawn in pencil on to special white paper or plywood sheet painted white, and then the outline was traced in ink on to a special transparent material.
[줄 245] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - The material used was critical, having to remain constant in size under different temperature and humidity conditions, and having a surface that would take ink without 'furring'.
[줄 246] [92.0%] (23/25) ✅ 유지 - Many of the outlines of plates to be cut by the profiler could be traced directly from the scrieve board, for example floors and transverses.
[줄 247] [100.0%] (6/6) ✅ 유지 - Computer-aided design /computer-aided manufacturing
[줄 248] [95.6%] (43/45) ✅ 유지 - The first technical use of computers in the shipbuilding industry occurred in the 1960s and because of the high costs involved was only used by the largest shipbuilders running programs developed in-house on a mainframe computer for naval architecture, including hydrostatics and powering calculations.
[줄 249] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - The hull design was drawn by hand and stored on the computer as tables of offsets for use in the mold loft.
[줄 250] [95.0%] (19/20) ✅ 유지 - Early developments for steel plate cutting and even frame bending were also seen in a few shipyards in the 1960s.
[줄 251] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - In the late 1970s the graphics terminal and the engineering workstation became readily available and could be linked to a mini computer.
[줄 252] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - These computers cost considerably less than the earlier mainframes, and commercial ship design and construction software became available for them.
[줄 253] [100.0%] (7/7) ✅ 유지 - The larger shipyards quickly adopted these systems.
[줄 254] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - They developed further in the following two decades to run on UNIX workstations and Windows NT machines and have expanded to cover virtually all the computing needs of a large shipyard.
[줄 255] [92.3%] (24/26) ✅ 유지 - The early 1980s saw the appearance of the personal computer and several low-cost software packages that performed simple hull design, hydrostatics, and powering estimate tasks.
[줄 256] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - These were popular with small shipyards and also reportedly with some larger shipyards for preliminary design work.
[줄 257] [96.0%] (24/25) ✅ 유지 - They were, however, somewhat limited and incompatible so that it was difficult to build a system that covered all the shipyard's CAD/CAM requirements.
[줄 258] [97.4%] (38/39) ✅ 유지 - During the 1990s the available PC software standardized on hardware, operating systems, programming languages, data interchange file formats and hull geometry, and are now widely used by naval architects and the smaller ship and boat building industry in general.
[줄 259] [100.0%] (43/43) ✅ 유지 - Ship product model Software systems for large shipbuilders are based on the concept of the 'ship product model' in which the geometry and the attributes of all elements of the ship derived from the contract design and classification society structural requirements are stored.
[줄 260] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - This model can be visualized at all stages and can be exploited to obtain information for production of the ship.
[줄 261] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - At the heart of the 'ship product model' is the conceptual creation of the hull form and its subsequent fairing for production purposes, which is accomplished without committing any plan to paper.
[줄 262] [97.6%] (40/41) ✅ 유지 - This faired hull form is generally held in the computer system as a 'wire model', which typically defines the molded lines of all structural items so that any structural section of the ship can be generated automatically from the 'wire model'.
[줄 263] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - The model can be worked on interactively with other stored shipyard standards and practices to produce detailed arrangement and working drawings.
[줄 264] [97.8%] (45/46) ✅ 유지 - The precision of the structural drawings generated enables them to be used with greater confidence than was possible with manual drawings and the materials requisitioning information can be stored on the computer to be interfaced with the shipyard's commercial systems for purchasing and material control.
[줄 265] [94.1%] (48/51) ✅ 유지 - Subassembly, assembly, and block drawings can be created in two- and three-dimensional form and a library of standard production sequences and production facilities can be called up so that the draughtsman can ensure that the structural design uses the shipyard's resources efficiently and follows established and cost-effective practices.
[줄 266] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - Weld lengths and types, steel weights, and detailed parts lists can be processed from the information on the drawing and passed to the production control systems.
[줄 267] [85.7%] (18/21) ✅ 유지 - A threedimensional steel assembly can be rotated by the draughtsman on screen to assess the best orientation for maximum downhand welding.
[줄 268] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - The use of three-dimensional drawings is particularly valuable in the area of outfit drawings where items like pipework and ventilation/air-conditioning trunking can be
[줄 269] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - 'sighted' in the three-dimensional mode and more accurately measured before being created in the two-dimensional drawing.
[줄 270] [95.7%] (66/69) ✅ 유지 - Stored information can be accessed so that lofting functions such as preparing information for bending frames and longitudinals, developing shell plates, and Design Manufacture Final lines plans Hull definition and design calculations Design database Concept design General arrangements Ship's database 3D wire ship model Material lists weights centers of gravity Nested formats Shop drawings Production control drawings Model integration + drawing generator Interactive parts nesting Longitudinal frame development + offsets
[줄 271] [98.0%] (50/51) ✅ 유지 - Development of shell plates Shell expansion Plate line body plan 3D surface + interrogation lines fairing Generation preliminary lines to ship database Loading inner structure surface Loading and fairing seams + longitudinal Standard details Unit assembly models Parts NC tape Nested formats Drawing file Roll sets + transverse frame offsets Jig pin heights etc.
[줄 272] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - Interactive parts coding and assembly model builder Fabrication drawings Structural drawings Model interrogations + drawing generator Software Precoded rules – procedures builders standards Loading stiffening seams + butts cutouts etc.
[줄 273] [66.7%] (4/6) ✅ 유지 - Figure 12.3 Ship product model.
[줄 274] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - providing shell frame sets and rolling lines or heat-line bending information for plates can be done via the interactive visual display unit.
[줄 275] [97.0%] (32/33) ✅ 유지 - For a numerically controlled profiling machine the piece parts to be cut can be 'nested', i.e fitted into the most economic plate, which can be handled by the machine with minimum wastage.
[줄 276] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - This can be done at the drawing stage when individual piece parts are abstracted for steel requisitioning and stored later, being brought back to the screen for interactive nesting.
[줄 277] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - The order in which parts are to be marked and cut can be defined by drawing the tool head around the parts on the graphics screen.
[줄 278] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - When the burning instructions are complete the cutting sequence may be replayed and checked for errors.
[줄 279] [100.0%] (40/40) ✅ 유지 - Instructions for cutting flame planed plates and subsequently joining them into panel assemblies and pin heights of jigs for setting up curved shell plates for welding framing and other members to them at the assembly stage can also be determined.
[줄 280] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - The basic ship product model also contains software packages for the ship's outfit, including piping, electrical and heating, ventilating and air-conditioning systems for a ship.
[줄 281] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - More recent developments have seen the hugely increased memory and processing capability of computers harnessed to the ship product model.
[줄 282] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - This now includes all the hull structural information as well as outfitting.
[줄 283] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - All pipes and other systems information is available in the model.
[줄 284] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - There is, as close as possible, a complete representation of the whole ship.
[줄 285] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - This can then be developed into information for part production, cutting and forming, assembly instructions, material lists, welding instructions, and quality assurance checks.

[줄 289] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - It is also now possible to combine the product model with virtual reality software.
[줄 290] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - This enables visualization of a structure or a compartment within a ship, which can then effectively be entered by the workforce.
[줄 291] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - The work sequence, access requirements, and other details can be developed so that the actual work process is planned completely and production will proceed without any delays or mistakes.

[줄 298] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Some useful websites The following websites are those of a number of providers of software for ship design and construction purposes.
[줄 299] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - They provide much more detail, graphic illustrations of the products, and other information than can be accommodated in a single chapter of this book.

[줄 303] [100.0%] (38/38) ✅ 유지 - This chapter describes the processes that a plate or section undergoes from the time it is received into the shipyard until it is in its final shape ready to be welded into a unit of the ship structure.
[줄 304] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - In recent years many changes have occurred in this sphere of shipyard activity, and substantial economies can be achieved by obtaining an even flow of production at this stage.
[줄 305] [100.0%] (42/42) ✅ 유지 - Plate and section preparation For efficient ship production, the steel material must be in an ideal condition when it is ready to be processed, and its marshaling into order for production on arrival is essential to the efficiency of the shipbuilding process.
[줄 306] [100.0%] (3/3) ✅ 유지 - All rights reserved.
[줄 307] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Stockyard On arrival at the shipyard, plates and sections are temporarily stored in the stockyard.
[줄 308] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - In larger shipyards the stockyard is an uncovered space having sufficient area to provide storage for enough plates and sections required for the working of the yard some months ahead.
[줄 309] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - The stockyard is needed because the production schedule of a steelmaker will not conform to the needs of one particular shipyard.
[줄 310] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Also, the shipyard may not be located near a steelmaker and may choose to purchase steel from another country if prices are lower.
[줄 311] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - The stockyard ensures there is always steel to maintain production.
[줄 312] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - In some cases the quantity of steel in storage might be about three months' stock, but shipyards in countries that are not substantial steel producers may find it necessary to carry much larger stocks of material.
[줄 313] [96.6%] (28/29) ✅ 유지 - In contrast, Far East shipyards closely associated with and/or located near a steel manufacturer may carry as little as one month's stock, and in some cases less.
[줄 314] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - When the plates and sections are ordered the steel mills are provided with details of the identification code for each item so that they may be marked.
[줄 315] [100.0%] (39/39) ✅ 유지 - On arrival in the stockyard, since the coding is generally in terms of the unit structure for which each item is intended, it is convenient to store the plates and sections in their respective ship and ship unit areas.
[줄 316] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - In other words the material for each ship is allotted an area of the stockyard, this area being subdivided into plots for those items intended for a major structural fabrication block of the ship.
[줄 317] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Smaller shipyards may choose to buy steel from a stockist, removing the need for a stockyard, which is an expensive facility.
[줄 318] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - They may also standardize the steel plates used to reduce the need for marshaling.
[줄 319] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - The ideal is 'just in time' delivery of steel, although some stock is kept as a buffer against delivery failures.
[줄 320] [94.7%] (18/19) ✅ 유지 - Material delivery and storage are controlled in accordance with production engineering practices to suit the ship's construction program.
[줄 321] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Steel plates are now stacked horizontally in piles as required.
[줄 322] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Steel profiles or sections are laid horizontally in convenient batches, usually by size and type.
[줄 323] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - Where cranes are used for material handling it is important that there be adequate coverage for the full extent of the stockyard, and the material may be delivered to the covered workshop areas.
[줄 324] [97.1%] (34/35) ✅ 유지 - Craneage is generally of the electric overhead gantry type, traversing the stockyard on rails and extending into the workshop area; alternatively, the plates may be placed on a roller conveyor for delivery to the workshops.
[줄 325] [96.9%] (31/32) ✅ 유지 - Lifts are made with magnetic clamps for plates and slings for the sections; the crane capacity can be up to 30 tonnes, to suit the material sizes that the shipyard can process.
[줄 326] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Plates required for the work being processed may be selected and stored adjacent to a conveyor and then transferred into the preparation workshop in the correct sequence.
[줄 327] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - The preparation begins with a conveyor system that transports the plates through a sequence of processes to bring it to a suitable condition for cutting.
[줄 328] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Heating Usually, a water wash or gas heating system is provided that heats the plate ready for subsequent paint drying.
[줄 329] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - A wash system will also remove debris, and in some cases snow or ice.
[줄 330] [100.0%] (3/3) ✅ 유지 - Plate leveling rolls
[줄 331] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - This is a set of plate-straightening rolls through which the plate is passed prior to its being worked.
[줄 332] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - During production at the steelworks, the plates may acquire locked-in stresses, which are released with the use of thermal processes in the shipyard.
[줄 333] [100.0%] (7/7) ✅ 유지 - This can cause distortion, which slows production.
[줄 334] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Also, during transit to the shipyard, plates may become distorted, and for many of the modern machining processes it is important that the plates should be as flat as practicable.
[줄 335] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - Two sets of rolls may be provided, one for heavy plate and one for light plate, but types are now available that permit a wide range of thicknesses to be straightened.
[줄 336] [94.4%] (17/18) ✅ 유지 - Shot-blasting Plates and sections are in almost all cases now shot-blasted to remove rust and millscale.
[줄 337] [90.9%] (10/11) ✅ 유지 - The principles of shot-blasting are dealt with in Chapter 27.
[줄 338] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Shot-blasting plant in shipyards is generally of the impeller wheel type, where the abrasive is thrown at high velocity against the steel surface and may be recirculated.
[줄 339] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - The plant is installed so that the plate may pass through in the horizontal position, which allows the use of automated, roller conveyor systems.
[줄 340] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - The only disadvantage of the horizontal plant is the removal of spent abrasive from the top of the plate, which may be relatively easily overcome.
[줄 341] [100.0%] (6/6) ✅ 유지 - The shot is recovered and recycled.
[줄 342] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - As it breaks down into smaller pieces, the mix of whole shot and fragments assists the blasting process.
[줄 343] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - Spent shot and debris is removed for disposal.
[줄 344] [100.0%] (5/5) ✅ 유지 - The whole process is enclosed.
[줄 345] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - A separate shot-blast plant is often installed for sections.
[줄 346] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Priming paint Following the shot-blasting of plates and sections, the material passes immediately through an airless spray painting plant.
[줄 347] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - In one pass the material is automatically sprayed with a priming paint of controlled coat thickness.
[줄 348] [95.2%] (20/21) ✅ 유지 - A number of suitable priming paints are available; the requirements for these and their formulation may be found in Chapter 27.
[줄 349] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - Following the priming paint stage a drying process may be provided.
[줄 350] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - This is a tunnel with fans to create an airstream, in conjunction with the preheating, so that the plate that emerges is dry and ready for processing.
[줄 351] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - The drying also reduces the potential for damage to the primer coating.
[줄 352] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Smaller shipyards that do not use large quantities of steel can purchase the material ready shot-blasted and primed by a supplier, which eliminates the expensive preparation equipment.
[줄 353] [94.7%] (36/38) ✅ 유지 - Plate handling in machine shops Throughout the machining shops, overhead electric cranes having capacities from 5 to 30 tonnes, depending on the ship and material sizes, are normally used to transport plates and sections to each machine process.
[줄 354] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Individual machines may have jib cranes mounted on the frame that can be employed to handle the plate during the machining process.
[줄 355] [92.3%] (24/26) ✅ 유지 - Distribution of plates in the shop may also be by means of conveyors or electricpowered trollies running on rails in bays between the plate working machines.
[줄 356] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Highly mechanized plant systems are also available where conveyor systems, flame cutting tables, and aligning and clamping equipment are installed as integrated units.
[줄 357] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - Plate and section part preparation A number of the methods in use for forming plates into the required shapes have been in use for many years.
[줄 358] [100.0%] (43/43) ✅ 유지 - This is particularly true of the methods adopted for fitting plates and frames to the curve of the hull, but as we have seen in the previous chapter the information for doing this can now be derived using the CAD/CAM systems available.
[줄 359] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Cutting flat plates to the required profiles has become highly automated, very sophisticated machine tools having been introduced for this purpose.
[줄 360] [94.1%] (16/17) ✅ 유지 - In the main, cutting is achieved by the use of an oxy-fuel flame or plasma arcs.
[줄 361] [91.7%] (22/24) ✅ 유지 - Plate pro fi le cutting machines Where a plate is to be cut into one or more complicated shapes, a profiling machine is employed.
[줄 362] [91.3%] (21/23) ✅ 유지 - Cutting is achieved by the use of an oxy-fuel gas or plasma-arc flame, or plasma-arc profilers are usually numerically controlled.
[줄 363] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - In this case the computer-generated information on the plate geometry is fed directly to the cutting machine.
[줄 364] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - The information is processed so that, in addition to the shape of the plate part, the start and finish of cutting, the speed of cutting, and information to mark the plate are provided.
[줄 365] [96.0%] (24/25) ✅ 유지 - Marking is generally done using an inkjet printing system, although some machines use a powder that is fused onto the plate using the gas heating.
[줄 366] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Provision can also be made for the shrinkage of the plate part as it cools after cutting.
[줄 367] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - The predicted shrinkage of the plate part is added to the nominal dimensions from the CAD system, so after cooling the part size is correct.
[줄 368] [77.8%] (7/9) ✅ 유지 - The overall arrangement is shown in Figure 13.1.
[줄 369] [84.6%] (11/13) ✅ 유지 - In some cases, 1:1 template or drawing controlled systems may be used.
[줄 370] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - This can be for small, repetitive parts such as brackets.
[줄 371] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - Such parts are more usually programmed using a basic CAD system.
[줄 372] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - A full-size template or drawing may be used to control a cutting machine, and can be useful where a single small item is to be cut in large numbers.
[줄 373] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - The size of the item is obviously restricted, and the location from which the item is cut in a large plate is selected by the operator.
[줄 374] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - Where a template is used a mechanical follower may be employed, and where a drawing is used an electronic scanning device may follow the outline.
[줄 375] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - Profilers of this type have a limited application in shipbuilding, but can be
[줄 376] [83.3%] (25/30) ✅ 유지 - Loftsman Cutting data and sequence plotter verification NC tape Director at work station Numerically controlled flame profiler Draughtsman parts programming interactive nesting Figure 13.1 Numerical flame cutting control system.
[줄 377] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - efficient for cutting batches of, say, identical beam knees or stiffener brackets.
[줄 378] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - More basic cutting systems are likely to be found in very small shipyards and in ship repair.
[줄 379] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Planing machines Profiling machines are essentially for use where a plate requires extensive shaping with intricate cuts being made.
[줄 380] [97.6%] (41/42) ✅ 유지 - Many of the plates in the ship's hull, particularly those in straightforward plate panels, decks, tank tops, bulkheads, and side shell, will only require trimming and edge preparation, and perhaps some shallow curves may need to be cut in shell plates.
[줄 381] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - This work may be carried out on a planing machine, usually a flame or plasma-arc planer.
[줄 382] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - A flame planer consists basically of three beams carrying burning heads and running on two tracks, one either side of the plate working area.
[줄 383] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - One beam carries two burning heads for trimming the plate sides during travel, whilst the other two beams have a single burning head traversing the beam in order to trim the plate ends.
[줄 384] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Each burning head may be fitted with triple nozzles and is used to give the required edge preparation.
[줄 385] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Plate, beam, and burning head positioning is manual, but cutting conditions are maintained once set.
[줄 386] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - Mechanical planing machines were in existence prior to the flame planer, and have an advantage where they are able to cut materials other than steels.
[줄 387] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - Higher cutting speeds than that obtained with flame cutting may be obtained for vertical edges with a rotary shearing wheel on a carriage, where the plate is held by hydraulic clamping.
[줄 388] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - For edge preparations, older machines with a conventional planing tool require a large number of passes and are much slower than flame planers.
[줄 389] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - There are, however, merits in mechanically machined edge preparations where the superior finish is advantageous for critical welds.
[줄 390] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - The use of plasma-arc planers, which also provide a superior and faster cut, tends to make the use of mechanical planers obsolete.
[줄 391] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Drilling machines Some plates or sections may need to have holes drilled in them, for example bolted covers and portable plates.
[줄 392] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Drilling machines generally consist of a single drilling head mounted on a radial arm that traverses the drill bed.
[줄 393] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Guillotines Smaller 'one-off' plate shapes such as beam knees, various brackets, and flat bar lengths may be cut in a hydraulically operated guillotine.
[줄 394] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - Plate feed to the guillotine is usually assisted by the provision of plate-supporting roller castors, and positioning of the cut edge is by hand.
[줄 395] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Presses Hydraulic presses may be extensively used in the shipyard for a variety of purposes.
[줄 396] [81.8%] (9/11) ✅ 유지 - They are capable of bending, straightening, flanging, dishing, and swaging plates
[줄 397] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - All of the work is done with the plate cold, and it is possible to carry out most of the work undertaken by a set of rolls.
[줄 398] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - This is done at less capital cost, but the press is slower when used for bending and requires greater skill.
[줄 399] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Plate rolls Heavy-duty bending rolls used for rolling shell plates etc to the correct curvature are hydraulically operated.
[줄 400] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - Two lower rolls are provided and are made to revolve in the same direction so that the plate is fed between them and a slightly larger diameter top roll that runs idly.
[줄 401] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Either or both ends of the top roll may be adjusted for height, and the two lower rolls have adjustable centers.
[줄 402] [95.8%] (23/24) ✅ 유지 - With modern bending rolls, plates up to 45 mm thick may be handled and it is possible to roll plates into a half circle.
[줄 403] [93.3%] (28/30) ✅ 유지 - These large rolls are also supplied with accessories to allow them to undertake heavy flanging work with the pressure exerted by the upper beam, for example 'troughing' corrugated bulkhead sections.
[줄 404] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Shorter pyramid full-circle rolls are also used in shipyards, these being very useful for rolling plates to a full circle.
[줄 405] [94.4%] (17/18) ✅ 유지 - This may be done to obtain large mast and derrick post sections for example, or bow thruster tunnel.
[줄 406] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Arrangements are made for removing the rolled full-circle plate by releasing the top roller end bearing.
[줄 407] [91.8%] (45/49) ✅ 유지 - Vertical rolls are also available and may be used to roll plates full circle, but can be much more useful for rolling heavy flats used as facing bars on transverses of large tankers, etc PLATE SWAGING EDGE CURVING PLATE FLANGING OR BENDING PLATE STRAIGHTENING Figure 13.2 Gap presses.
[줄 408] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Heat-line bending The 'heat-line' bending procedure is a widely used technique to obtain curvature in steel plates for shipbuilding purposes.
[줄 409] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - It is, however, a process that until recently relied on highly skilled personnel and did not guarantee constant accuracy of shapes formed.
[줄 410] [83.8%] (31/37) ✅ 유지 - Apply heat Expansion Bend Contraction Single-plane bending Two-plane bending 1 2 4 3 Heat line bending principle Beam applying load PLATE ROLLS Top roller Driven roll Driven roll Plate Figure 13.3 Forming shell plates.
[줄 411] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Heat is applied in a line to the surface of a plate by a flame torch, with immediate cooling using air or water.
[줄 412] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - The narrow heated line of material is prevented from expanding in the direction of the plate surface by the large mass of cold plate, and therefore expands outwards perpendicular to the plate surface.
[줄 413] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - On cooling, contraction will take place in the direction of the plate surface, causing the plate to become concave on the side to which heat was applied.
[줄 414] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - An experienced operator is able to make a pattern of such heat lines on a plate, producing controlled distortion to obtain a required shape.
[줄 415] [100.0%] (39/39) ✅ 유지 - Heat-line bending can be more time consuming than using rolls or presses, but it has an advantage in that the plate holds its form more accurately when stiffening and other members are added later in the fabrication process.
[줄 416] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - This is an important consideration since shape inaccuracy can be critical at the erection stage in terms of lost production time.
[줄 417] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Heat-line bending may be used after cold forming to obtain improved accuracy.
[줄 418] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - It is also used where a double curvature is required, for example on bulbous bow plates.
[줄 419] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - In recent years fully automated heat-line bending systems have been developed and installed in shipyards.
[줄 420] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - These numerically controlled heat-line bending machines permit highly accurate, reproducible thermal forming of any steel plate using the data originating from the shipyard's CAD system.
[줄 421] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - More than double the productivity of the traditional manual process is achieved.
[줄 422] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Frame bending The traditional system of bending side frames may still be in use for repair work, and is described as follows.
[줄 423] [93.8%] (30/32) ✅ 유지 - A 'set-bar', which is a flat bar of soft iron, is bent to the scrieve line of the frame on the scrieve board and then taken to the frame bending slabs.
[줄 424] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - On these solid cast-iron slabs pierced with holes the line of the frame is marked, and modified to agree with the line of the toe of the frame.
[줄 425] [100.0%] (42/42) ✅ 유지 - As the heated frame on cooling will tend to bend, the set-bar is sprung to allow for this change in curvature before it is fixed down on the bending slabs by means of 'dogs' and pins inserted in the slab holes.
[줄 426] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Whilst the set-bar is being fixed the frame section is heated in a long oil-fired furnace adjacent to the bending slabs.
[줄 427] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - When at the right temperature it is pulled out onto the slabs and fixed with dogs and pins against the set-bar, as quickly as possible.
[줄 428] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - Tools are available for forcing the frame round against the set-bar, including a portable hydraulic ram, and the toe of the web may require constant hammering to avoid buckling under compression.
[줄 429] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - As the frames fitted have their webs perpendicular to the ship's center line, all except those immediately amidships will require beveling.
[줄 430] [100.0%] (50/50) ✅ 유지 - A beveling machine is available that is placed in front of the furnace door, and as the frame is removed it passes between its rollers, which are controlled so that the flange is bent at every point to an angle indicated by a bevel board prepared by the mold loft.
[줄 431] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Once bent, the bar is put aside to cool, but is fastened down to prevent its warping in the vertical direction.
[줄 432] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - When cold it is checked against the frame line drawn on the slabs.
[줄 433] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Meanwhile, the set-bar is turned over and used to bend the corresponding frame for the opposite side of the ship.
[줄 434] [100.0%] (6/6) ✅ 유지 - Container ships Ultra-large container ships.
[줄 435] [66.7%] (6/9) ✅ 유지 - Ships with a capacity of over 14,000 TEU.
[줄 436] [100.0%] (6/6) ✅ 유지 - Few have been built to date.
[줄 437] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - These ships are too large for any canals.
[줄 438] [87.5%] (14/16) ✅ 유지 - Post-Panamax ships are too large to transit the current Panama Canal and undertake transocean voyages.
[줄 439] [68.4%] (13/19) ✅ 유지 - Their size is typically 5500–8000 TEU though larger ships with over 10,000 TEU capacity have been built.
[줄 440] [91.7%] (11/12) ✅ 유지 - New Panamax ships would be able to transit the expanded Panama Canal.
[줄 441] [66.7%] (6/9) ✅ 유지 - They may carry up to around 12,000 TEU.
[줄 442] [73.3%] (11/15) ✅ 유지 - Panamax ships that can transit the current Panama Canal carry between 3000 and 5000 TEU.
[줄 443] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Feeder ships are smaller vessels that do not undertake oceanic voyages but are generally engaged in shipping containers.
[줄 444] [90.0%] (9/10) ✅ 유지 - The smallest of these may only carry several hundred TEU.
[줄 445] [87.5%] (7/8) ✅ 유지 - There is no specific subclass below Panamax size.
[줄 446] [86.8%] (46/53) ✅ 유지 - IMO oil tanker categories Category 1 includes oil tankers of 20,000 tonnes deadweight and above carrying crude oil, fuel oil, heavy diesel oil, or lubricating oil as cargo, and of 30,000 tonnes deadweight and above carrying other oils, which do not comply with the requirements for protectively located segregated ballast tanks.
[줄 447] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - These ships have been phased out under IMO regulations.
[줄 448] [84.1%] (37/44) ✅ 유지 - Category 2 includes oil tankers of 20,000 tonnes deadweight and above carrying crude oil, fuel oil, or lubricating oil as cargo, and of 30,000 tonnes deadweight and above carrying other oils, which do comply with the protectively located segregated ballast tank requirements.
[줄 449] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - These ships are due to be phased out.
[줄 450] [73.9%] (17/23) ✅ 유지 - Category 3 includes oil tankers of 5000 tonnes deadweight and above but less than the tonnes deadweight specified for Categories 1 and 2.

[줄 457] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Cold frame bending It is now almost universal practice to cold-bend ship frames using commercially available machines for this purpose.
[줄 458] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - The frames are progressively bent by application of a horizontal ram whilst the frame is held by gripping levers.
[줄 459] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Any type of rolled section can be bent in some machines with a limitation on the size of section.
[줄 460] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Obtaining the correct frame curvature can be achieved by the 'inverse curve' method or numerical control.
[줄 461] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - With the 'inverse curve' method the inverse curve information can be determined for each frame using a CAD/CAM system.
[줄 462] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - The inverse curve is marked onto the straight frame and the frame bent until the inverse curve becomes straight on the curved frame.
[줄 463] [94.4%] (34/36) ✅ 유지 - A hydraulic cold-frame-bending machine can be controlled by numerical control tapes prepared in a similar manner to the numerically controlled flame profilers, the frame line being initially defined from the computer-stored faired hull.
[줄 464] [91.2%] (31/34) ✅ 유지 - Section pro fi lers Plate profilers produce very accurate plate components for assembly into ship units and it is important that the supporting stiffening members of the structure are produced with the same accuracy.
[줄 465] [94.4%] (17/18) ✅ 유지 - Section profilers accurately cut, scallop, and bevel, as necessary, the profile edge to be welded to the plate.
[줄 466] [96.4%] (27/28) ✅ 유지 - Cutting is by oxy-fuel gas or plasma and in modern systems is undertaken by a compact robot operating in a viewable enclosed workstation with integral fume extraction.
[줄 467] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - Prior to cutting, the stiffening member can be moved through a marking cell where part identification and, where required, bending lines for inverse curve frame bending can be marked.
[줄 468] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Robotics Robots have in recent years been provided with improved control features that have made them more adaptable to the workshop floor situation.
[줄 469] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - For example, most robots are now available with some form of 'adaptive control', which provides feedback from the environment permitting, say, automatic adjustment of the robots path and/or its functions.
[줄 470] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Also, the provision of 'off-line' programming and simulation packages makes it possible to develop and test programs for the robot remotely.
[줄 471] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Thus, the robot carries on working whilst new programs are produced for it.
[줄 472] [94.4%] (17/18) ✅ 유지 - Many of the world's shipyards and shipyard systems suppliers have been developing and implementing robots in shipbuilding.
[줄 473] [97.5%] (39/40) ✅ 유지 - A large proportion of these developments have been in fully automating the machine welding processes described in Chapter 9, but other areas of adoption and trial have involved flame and plasma-arc cutting, local shot-blasting and painting, and marking.
[줄 474] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Robots developed to date for shipyard usage are either associated with large gantry structures or are small portable units.
[줄 475] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - The former often have the movable robot mounted on the traveling gantry with sensors providing the adaptive control, and are employed for cutting and welding processes.
[줄 476] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - The latter can be manually transported or self-propelled, even climbing vertically, or for robotic transportation, and have been used for local welding in difficult situations and cleaning and painting.

[줄 494] [87.5%] (21/24) ✅ 유지 - Joining ship sections a fl oat 158 Further reading 159 Some useful websites 159 Historically, ships were constructed on a slipway piece by piece.
[줄 495] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - The transition from wood, to iron and then steel made little initial difference to the construction process, and the result was the typical shipyard layout as described in Chapter 11.
[줄 496] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - Exceptions were for military and large passenger ships.
[줄 497] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - During the Second World War a large number of merchant and war ships were required to be built in a short period of time.
[줄 498] [95.2%] (20/21) ✅ 유지 - These requirements speeded the adoption of welding in shipyards, and often led to the application of mass production techniques in shipbuilding.
[줄 499] [91.7%] (22/24) ✅ 유지 - Prefabrication of ship units, i.e the construction of individual sections of the ship's structure prior to erection, became a highly developed science.
[줄 500] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Often, the units were manufactured at a location remote from the shipyard, and erection in the shipyards was carried out with schedules that still look very impressive today.
[줄 501] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Many of the more spectacular achievements in this field were obtained in the USA, where much of the tonnage required during the war period was constructed using these new advances.
[줄 502] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - Unfortunately, the results of this crash building program were not always entirely satisfactory; the reputation of welded structures, for example, suffered for quite a time as a result of wholesale application without a background of experience.
[줄 503] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Also, the adoption of the prefabricated units was dictated by speed and large-scale production, rather than economics.
[줄 504] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - However, the potential benefits of units were identified and shipyards began to make the necessary investment, in additional assembly workshops and larger cranes, to use prefabricated units.
[줄 505] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - The initial low cost of labor made traditional methods still reasonably economic.
[줄 506] [96.9%] (31/32) ✅ 유지 - During the 1950s there was an increase in ship size and the greater quantity of steel required for the structures of these ships was a major driver for the adoption of units.
[줄 507] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Also, the costs of labor in traditional shipbuilding countries increased.
[줄 508] [100.0%] (3/3) ✅ 유지 - All rights reserved.
[줄 509] [93.8%] (30/32) ✅ 유지 - From the mid 1950s, prefabrication was gradually being applied to merchant ship construction as shipyards benefitting from a high demand for ships were able to invest in the additional workshops and cranes.
[줄 510] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - Today, all vessels are to varying degrees prefabricated.
[줄 511] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - With riveted construction unit fabrication was rarely employed; the introduction of welding lent itself more favorably to this form of construction.
[줄 512] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - With welding, simpler unit shapes and at first less critical tolerances could be applied.
[줄 513] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - In the early days of unit construction, the units were assembled over size, so they could be trimmed to fit on the building berth.
[줄 514] [93.3%] (14/15) ✅ 유지 - What is termed 'green' material was left on the unit edges, typically around 20 mm.
[줄 515] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - The unit was then lifted into place and cut to fit the structure, which had already been erected.
[줄 516] [100.0%] (44/44) ✅ 유지 - The pressures of cost and required speed of construction have led to much greater accuracy of assembly, so that for parallel body in particular, units and blocks can be produced with sufficient accuracy to allow them to be fitted and welded without any adjustment.
[줄 517] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - This provides a saving in man-hours and time.
[줄 518] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - Units may be constructed under cover, which is an attractive advantage, for example, in Northern Europe and also in hot climates, not only because of working conditions, but because of the better welding conditions.
[줄 519] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - It is possible to turn units over to allow downhand welding, which is easier to perform and likely to provide better results.
[줄 520] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - There is great advantage in keeping vertical and overhead welding to a minimum.
[줄 521] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - Also, central services are more readily available at the shop, with gases for cutting, air for chipping, and electric current for welding being placed where needed.
[줄 522] [100.0%] (38/38) ✅ 유지 - Production planning techniques may be adopted with prefabrication sequences, the material and labor being planned in unit groups and the whole shipbuilding sequence being controlled to fit the time allowed on the berth, or in the building dock.
[줄 523] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Once the unit construction method became established, and ships continued to become larger, the units were also made bigger and then several units were assembled into large blocks.
[줄 524] [85.7%] (12/14) ✅ 유지 - Figure 14.1 shows a typical side block for a single hull bulk carrier.
[줄 525] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - When the first large tankers were built, typical units were around 50 tonnes.
[줄 526] [80.0%] (8/10) ✅ 유지 - By 1970, lifting blocks of 500 tonnes were not uncommon.
[줄 527] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - As the ships grew in size they also grew in complexity and outfitting began to be a bottleneck.
[줄 528] [81.0%] (17/21) ✅ 유지 - In 1970, a 200,000-tonne deadweight tanker could be constructed in two or three months in new or modernized shipyards.
[줄 529] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - It was then necessary to speed the outfitting of ships to avoid having several ships outfitting at the same time and to gain the advantages that faster construction offered in terms of increased income.
[줄 530] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - The traditional approach of completing and launching the hull prior to outfitting in a basin or at a quay had to be modified.
[줄 531] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - Until unit and then block construction was established, the outfit and equipment were fitted at the berth and after launching at the fitting-out quay.
[줄 532] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Piping systems, ventilation, and the machinery units were fitted into the erected hull as independent items.
[줄 533] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Likewise, the accommodation spaces were lined out and fitted with the furniture and other fittings in situ.
[줄 534] [97.1%] (33/34) ✅ 유지 - Whilst the production methods applied to the steelwork fabrication and erection were time saving and cost-effective, the haphazard and largely uncontrolled methods of outfitting detracted from the overall production engineering of the ship.
[줄 535] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Rather than plan outfit installation on a total ship system basis, it is today standard practice to plan this work for zone installation, the zone corresponding to
[줄 536] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - a main compartment area that may be broken down into blocks or smaller assemblies.
[줄 537] [80.0%] (12/15) ✅ 유지 - Pre-outfitting of each assembly or block may be of the order of 85–90%.
[줄 538] [97.0%] (32/33) ✅ 유지 - Both steelwork and outfit are highly planned for each assembly and block unit, and fabrication and outfit installation are undertaken at a workstation where the facilities and material are supplied to the workforce.

[줄 540] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Assembly Assembly is any process that takes a number of steel piece parts, or larger structures, and combines them into a larger structure.
[줄 541] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - For very large ships, assembly consists of a number of stages, putting together increasingly larger elements of the ship.
[줄 542] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - The number of stages varies between shipyards and especially varies with ship size.

[줄 547] [96.2%] (25/26) ✅ 유지 - Unit assembly : A structure that can be erected in the building dock, typically one or two panels and associated internal structure, weight up to 60 tonnes.
[줄 548] [94.7%] (18/19) ✅ 유지 - Block : An assembly of two or more units into a bottom or side block, weighing up to 200 tonnes.

[줄 550] [87.5%] (7/8) ✅ 유지 - Subassemblies When plates and sections have been machined
[줄 551] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - they are ready for assembly into two-dimensional ship units.
[줄 552] [96.9%] (31/32) ✅ 유지 - Within the fabrication shop there are often arranged a number of bays for different assemblies, for example flat plate panels, curved shell units, matrix or 'egg box' structures and some minor subassemblies.
[줄 553] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - All these may be termed subassemblies if they are subsequently to be built into a larger three-dimensional unit prior to erection.
[줄 554] [100.0%] (43/43) ✅ 유지 - A two-dimensional plate panel assembly may be highly automated with prepared plates being placed and tack welded prior to automatic welding of the butts, after which the plates are turned and back welded unless a single-sided weld process has been used.
[줄 555] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - The panel is marked and the stiffeners placed and welded automatically or with semi-automatic process.
[줄 556] [90.9%] (10/11) ✅ 유지 - Marking and welding of two-dimensional panels is often robotically controlled.
[줄 557] [94.7%] (18/19) ✅ 유지 - Minor subassemblies such as deep frames consisting of web and welded face flat are also attached at this stage.
[줄 558] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Curved shell plates are placed on jigs and welded, and the various stiffening members can be aligned and welded in a similar manner to those on a flat panel assembly.
[줄 559] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - Assembly jigs may also be used for matrix or 'egg box' assemblies, for example structures of solid and bracket plate floors with longitudinal side girders that are to go into double-bottom units.
[줄 560] [87.5%] (14/16) ✅ 유지 - Unit assembly In most instances the two-dimensional subassemblies will be built into threedimensional unit assemblies.
[줄 561] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - The size of the unit assembly will have been decided at an early stage of the planning process, ideally at the structural design stage.
[줄 562] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - Constraints such as lifting capacities and dimensions that can be handled are taken into consideration, as is the provision of breaks at natural features ensuring the blocks are self-supporting and easily accessed, etc.

[줄 567] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Block assembly Several units can be combined into a block.
[줄 568] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - Where a typical unit is a double-hull section, a block can combine several of these to form a complete double-bottom block over a plate length, or a side block.
[줄 569] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - Units will have generally been outfitted during assembly, for example the piping in a double-bottom unit, installed when the unit is in the most convenient orientation and access is good.
[줄 570] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - The block is sufficiently large, especially in zones such as machinery spaces or pump rooms, for substantial outfitting before transport to the building dock.
[줄 571] [100.0%] (47/47) ✅ 유지 - Units can be easily turned to effect outfit installation, particularly those containing machinery flats in the aft engine room areas where pipework etc can be fitted on the underside of the flat in the inverted position and then it is turned to install equipment above the flat.
[줄 572] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - These already outfitted units can then be assembled into a larger block and additional outfitting installed.
[줄 573] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - Also, outfit modules can be installed into the blocks.
[줄 574] [97.6%] (41/42) ✅ 유지 - A block's center of gravity is calculated and lifting lugs so provided that these operations can be undertaken, and finally the block can be suspended for erection at the building dock or berth and put into place in the correct plane.

[줄 597] [94.7%] (36/38) ✅ 유지 - Unit erection When any panel and the block assemblies are complete there will be some time buffer before their erection at the building berth, building dock, or within the building hall to Figure 14.4 Cabin/toilet module.

[줄 639] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - More recently, the use of digital photogrammetry has been adopted in some shipyards.

[줄 646] [100.0%] (46/46) ✅ 유지 - Joining ship sections a fl oat Owing to the enormous increase in size of bulk carriers and tankers, some shipyards with restricted facilities, building berth or dock size in particular, have resorted in the past to building the ship in two halves and joining these afloat.
[줄 647] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - This is not a very efficient process and is adopted as an expedient only.
[줄 648] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Where the two sections are to be joined afloat, extremely accurate fit-up of the sections is aided by the possibility of ballasting the two ship halves.
[줄 649] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - The two sections may then be pulled together by tackles, and for the finer adjustments hydraulic cylinders may be used, extremely accurate optical instruments being employed to mark off the sections for alignment.
[줄 650] [97.0%] (32/33) ✅ 유지 - One method adopted is that where a cofferdam is arranged in way of the joint, a caisson is brought up against the ship's hull, and the cofferdam and caisson are pumped dry.
[줄 651] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - To balance any tendency for the vessel to hog during the pumping of the cofferdam, it is necessary to shift ballast in the fore and aft sections.
[줄 652] [93.1%] (27/29) ✅ 유지 - Once the spaces are dried out, welding of the complete joint may be undertaken, the resulting weld being X-rayed to test the soundness of such a critical joint.
[줄 653] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - On completion of the paint scheme in way of the joint the caisson is removed.
[줄 654] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - A similar method makes use of a rubber 'U' form ring rather than a caisson, which needs modification for each ship size.
[줄 655] [96.8%] (30/31) ✅ 유지 - If a dry dock is available the sections may be aligned afloat and even welded above the waterline, the rest of the joint or the complete joint being secured by strongbacks.
[줄 656] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - The welding of the rest or the whole joint is carried out in the dock.
