[줄 1878] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Bulkheads Bulkhead spacing throughout the cargo tank space is determined by the permissible length of cargo tanks.
[줄 1879] [92.5%] (49/53) ✅ 유지 - MARPOL requires that the length of each cargo tank shall not exceed the greater of 10 meters or a length expressed as a percentage of the ship's length that is dependent on the number of longitudinal bulkheads fitted and the minimum distance from the ship's side of the outer longitudinal bulkhead.
[줄 1880] [90.9%] (20/22) ✅ 유지 - Tankers with two or more longitudinal bulkheads may have wing and center tank lengths up to 20% of the ship's length.
[줄 1881] [88.5%] (23/26) ✅ 유지 - Lloyd's Register require the disposition of transverse bulkheads to comply with the stipulations given in Table 18.1, as applicable to ships with machinery aft.
[줄 1882] [92.0%] (23/25) ✅ 유지 - Cofferdams, which may be formed with two adjacent oiltight transverse bulkheads at least 760 mm apart, are required at the ends of the cargo space.
[줄 1883] [100.0%] (38/38) ✅ 유지 - However, in many cases a pump room is fitted at the after end of the cargo space and a ballast tank is fitted at the forward end, each of these compartments being accepted in lieu of a cofferdam.
[줄 1884] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - A cofferdam is also provided between any accommodation and oil cargo tanks.
[줄 1885] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - Construction of the transverse bulkheads is similar to that in other ships, the bulkhead being oiltight.
[줄 1886] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Vertical stiffeners are fitted, or corrugated plating is provided with the corrugations running either vertically or horizontally.
[줄 1887] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Horizontal stringers support the vertical stiffeners and corrugations, and vertical webs support any horizontal corrugations.
[줄 1888] [100.0%] (44/44) ✅ 유지 - Further support is provided by the vertical center-line web, which is as a rule deeper on one side of the bulkhead than on the other, unless the tank is very long and the web may then be symmetrical either side of the bulkhead.
[줄 1889] [94.4%] (17/18) ✅ 유지 - Longitudinal bulkheads, which are oiltight, may be conventionally stiffened or may be corrugated with the corrugations running horizontally.
[줄 1890] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - Vertical corrugated center-line bulkheads may be fitted.
[줄 1891] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Conventional stiffening is arranged vertically where the side framing is vertical and arranged longitudinally when the side is longitudinally framed.
[줄 1892] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Vertical webs are fitted to the longitudinal bulkhead when this is corrugated or longitudinally framed.
[줄 1893] [86.7%] (13/15) ✅ 유지 - Corrugated longitudinal bulkheads are only permitted in ships of less than 200 m in length.
[줄 1894] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - Hatchways Oiltight hatchways provide access to the tank spaces at the exposed deck.
[줄 1895] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - The openings for these are kept as small as possible, and the corners are well rounded, circular openings being not uncommon.
[줄 1896] [92.3%] (24/26) ✅ 유지 - Coamings provided for the openings should be of steel and at least 600 mm high, and suitably fastened steel or other approved material covers are fitted.
[줄 1897] [93.3%] (14/15) ✅ 유지 - Patent oiltight hatches are available and approved with both steel- and fiber-reinforced plastic covers.
[줄 1898] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Access to any cofferdams and water ballast tanks may be by similar hatches in the deck, or alternatively a watertight manhole may be fitted with a cover of suitable thickness.
[줄 1899] [96.0%] (24/25) ✅ 유지 - Other openings are provided in the deck for ullage plugs and tank cleaning, these being on the open deck, and not within enclosed deck spaces.
[줄 1900] [93.5%] (43/46) ✅ 유지 - Testing tanks Each cargo tank and cofferdam may be tested separately when complete by filling the tank with water to a head 2.45 m above the highest point of the tank excluding the hatchways, and by filling the cofferdam to the top of the hatch.
[줄 1901] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - Water testing on the building berth or dry dock may be undesirable owing to the size of flooded tanks, which gives rise to large stresses on the supporting material and structure.
[줄 1902] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Testing afloat is therefore permitted, each tank being filled separately until about half the tanks are full, when the bottom and lower side shell in the empty tanks are examined.
[줄 1903] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Water is then transferred to the empty tanks, and the remainder of the bottom and side shell is inspected.
[줄 1904] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - This testing may take place after the application of protective coatings, provided that welds have been carefully examined beforehand.
[줄 1905] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - In practice, a combination of a structural water test and air leak test is often used.
[줄 1906] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - The air leak test is carried out on the building berth, the tanks being subject to an air pressure similar to that required for testing double-bottom tanks.
[줄 1907] [94.4%] (17/18) ✅ 유지 - Awater pressure test is carried out on one center tank and two wing tanks selected by the surveyors.
[줄 1908] [91.3%] (42/46) ✅ 유지 - Clean water ballast tanks are tested in the same manner as the cargo tanks, but bunkers and deep tank test requirements are similar to those in dry cargo ships, i.e a head of water 2.45 m above the crown of the tank is applied.
[줄 1909] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Any bulkhead not forming a tank boundary is hose tested.
[줄 1910] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Fore end structure Forward of the tank space deep tanks may be fitted.
[줄 1911] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - Framing throughout this space and the forepeak may be transverse, longitudinal, or a combination of both.
[줄 1912] [97.5%] (39/40) ✅ 유지 - Deep tank If transverse framing is adopted, forward floors are fitted at every frame space in conjunction with a center-line girder or center-line bulkhead and intercostal side girders not more than three times the transverse frame spacing apart.
[줄 1913] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - If longitudinal bulkheads are fitted port and starboard in the cargo tanks, these may be extended to the fore side of the deep tank in lieu of a center-line bulkhead.
[줄 1914] [95.8%] (46/48) ✅ 유지 - Above the floors the transverse frames are supported by stringers spaced not more than 5 m apart, which are either supported by web frames connected to deep beams to form a vertical ring frame, or connected to longitudinal stringers on the transverse bulkheads to form horizontal ring frames.
[줄 1915] [76.9%] (10/13) ✅ 유지 - Alternatively, in narrow tanks perforated flats may be fitted at 5 m spacings.
[줄 1916] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Longitudinally framed deep tanks are supported by side transverses five frame spaces apart.
[줄 1917] [95.5%] (42/44) ✅ 유지 - Where the depth of the tank exceeds 16 m the side transverses, and the web frames in a transversely framed tank, either have one or more deep stringers fitted, cross ties, or perforated flats with deep beams in way of the transverses or webs.
[줄 1918] [93.1%] (27/29) ✅ 유지 - A longitudinal bulkhead generally must be provided if the tank width exceeds 50% of the ship's beam and may solely be a wash bulkhead on the center line.
[줄 1919] [90.5%] (19/21) ✅ 유지 - breadth of tank exceeds 70% of the ship's beam, at least one solid bulkhead on the center line is recommended.
[줄 1920] [90.9%] (20/22) ✅ 유지 - Forepeak A transversely framed forepeak has a similar construction to that of a conventional cargo ship and includes the usual panting arrangements.
[줄 1921] [85.7%] (36/42) ✅ 유지 - If the forepeak is longitudinally framed the side transverses have a maximum spacing of between 2.5 and 3.5 m depending on the length of ship, and are connected to transverses arranged under the decks in line with the side transverses.
[줄 1922] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Forecastles have web frames to support any longitudinal side framing, and the forecastle deck may be supported by pillars at its center line.
[줄 1923] [100.0%] (40/40) ✅ 유지 - Ice strengthening With the growing export of oil from Russia an increasing number of new tankers are being provided with ice strengthening forward so that they can trade to parts of the Baltic Sea that can be frozen in winter.
[줄 1924] [72.7%] (8/11) ✅ 유지 - These include several 20,000 tonne deadweight ice-breaking oil tankers.
[줄 1925] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - After end structure The machinery is arranged aft in ocean-going tankers, and a transversely framed double-bottom structure is adopted in way of the machinery space.
[줄 1926] [100.0%] (35/35) ✅ 유지 - Constructional details of this double bottom are similar to those of the conventional dry cargo ship, with floors at each frame space, additional side girders, and the engine seating integral with the bottom stiffening members.
[줄 1927] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Transverse or longitudinal side and deck framing may be adopted in way of the engine room and aft of this space.
[줄 1928] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - If transversely framed, web frames are fitted not more than five frame spaces apart below the lowest deck and may be supported by side stringers.
[줄 1929] [95.8%] (23/24) ✅ 유지 - The web frames may be extended into the poop, and where an allhouses aft arrangement is adopted they may also extend into the superstructure.
[줄 1930] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Similar transverse webs are introduced to support any longitudinal framing adopted in a machinery space.
[줄 1931] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - Transverse webs have the same spacing as web frames except in tween decks above the aft peak, where the maximum spacing is four frame spaces.
[줄 1932] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - The aft peak and stern construction follows that of other merchant ship types, a center-line bulkhead being provided in the aft peak.
[줄 1933] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - Any ice strengthening is similar to that required in other ships.
[줄 1934] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - Superstructures To permit the assignment of deeper freeboards for oil tankers, the conditions of assignment of load line stipulate the requirements for protective
[줄 1935] [88.9%] (8/9) ✅ 유지 - housings enclosing openings in the freeboard and other decks.
[줄 1936] [86.7%] (13/15) ✅ 유지 - They also require provision of a forecastle covering 7% of the ship's length forward.
[줄 1937] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Structurally, the houses are similar to those of other vessels, special attention being paid to the discontinuities in way of breaks at the ends of the houses.
[줄 1938] [93.3%] (14/15) ✅ 유지 - Particular attention must be paid to any endings in the midship length of the hull.
[줄 1939] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - As the machinery is aft the poop front merits special attention, and is in fact structurally similar to the bridge front, since its integrity is essential.
[줄 1940] [96.6%] (28/29) ✅ 유지 - A particular feature of the tanker with its lower freeboard is the requirement for an access gangway at the level of the first tier of superstructure between accommodation spaces.
[줄 1941] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - This is still often found on vessels with all accommodation aft, although the regulations would permit a rail or similar safety arrangement at the deck level.
[줄 1942] [96.4%] (27/28) ✅ 유지 - The provision of a gangway in the latter case is at the owner's wish, and is an added safety factor at greater initial cost, requiring additional maintenance.
[줄 1943] [100.0%] (35/35) ✅ 유지 - Another feature is the absence of bulwarks on the main decks, the regulations requiring the provision of open rails over at least half the length of the wells, which are often awash in heavy weather.
[줄 1944] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - Floating production, storage, and of fl oading vessels Floating production, storage, and offloading vessels and floating storage units are now a common feature of offshore oil installations.
[줄 1945] [68.2%] (15/22) ✅ 유지 - A typical FSU is of 100,000 tons deadweight with a storage capacity of 112,000 cubic meters representing 10 days production.
[줄 1946] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - Crude oil from a floating production unit is transferred to the FSU, where it is loaded via a submerged turret loading system.
[줄 1947] [92.0%] (23/25) ✅ 유지 - From the FSU the crude oil is transferred to shore by shuttle tankers, which are loaded by flexible hoses from the stern of the FSU.
[줄 1948] [80.0%] (12/15) ✅ 유지 - An FPSO combines the functions of the FPU and FSU in a single floating unit.
[줄 1949] [94.6%] (35/37) ✅ 유지 - Many oil tankers, more recently those with a single hull that are barred from some trades, have been converted to FPSOs and FSUs, but there are also numbers of new design and build contracts for such vessels.
[줄 1950] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - The basic hull construction is similar to that for conventional tankers but there are arrangements and structural features peculiar to these vessels.
[줄 1951] [96.4%] (27/28) ✅ 유지 - The vessels are moored using a turret system forward, which allows the hull to weathervane into the wind and waves to reduce dynamic loading on the hull girder.
[줄 1952] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - However, because the waves will be coming mainly towards the bow for the whole of its life, the hull girder will experience greater fatigue problems than would be the case for a conventional tanker.
[줄 1953] [91.2%] (31/34) ✅ 유지 - The conventional tanker carries little in the way of loading on its main deck, whereas an FPSO is fitted with a substantial oil production facility, which can weigh in excess of 20,000 tons.
[줄 1954] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - This loading needs to be transferred into the hull structure, which means that vertical structural components are more complex and substantial than those of a tanker.
[줄 1955] [94.3%] (33/35) ✅ 유지 - Further, because both FSUs and FPSOs are expected to remain on station for their lifetime and withstand arduous conditions without dry-docking, the exposed hull construction is generally upgraded and strengthened with increased corrosion protection.
[줄 1956] [70.6%] (12/17) ✅ 유지 - Note: Tank stiffening above deck Figure 22.4 Oil products/chemical tanker of 12,700 tonnes deadweight.
[줄 1957] [100.0%] (35/35) ✅ 유지 - Chemical tankers The structural configurations and arrangements of chemical tankers often are basically similar to those described for oil tankers, particularly where the chemical product is not required to be carried in an independent tank.
[줄 1958] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - For some cargoes tanks constructed of stainless steel are preferred.
[줄 1959] [96.6%] (28/29) ✅ 유지 - Where the chemical product is required to be carried in an independent tank the structure and arrangements may be similar to ships carrying liquefied gases described in Chapter 23.
[줄 1960] [96.4%] (53/55) ✅ 유지 - Regardless of size, ships built or converted on or after 1 July 1986 and engaged in the carriage of bulk cargoes of dangerous or noxious liquid chemical substances, other than petroleum or similar flammable products, are required to comply with the International Code for the Construction and Equipment of Ships Carrying Dangerous Chemicals in Bulk.
[줄 1961] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Such ships built or converted before that date are to comply with the earlier Code for the Construction and Equipment of Ships Carrying Dangerous Chemicals in Bulk.
[줄 1962] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Ships that comply with these requirements are issued with an 'International Certificate of Fitness for the Carriage of Dangerous Chemicals in Bulk'.
[줄 1963] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - Under the IBC Code chemical tankers are designed and constructed to one of three specified standards.
[줄 1964] [95.2%] (20/21) ✅ 유지 - A type 1 ship is a chemical tanker intended for the transportation of products considered to present the greatest overall hazard.
[줄 1965] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - It should be capable of surviving the most severe standard of damage and its cargo tanks should be located at the maximum prescribed distance inboard from the shell plating.
[줄 1966] [81.8%] (9/11) ✅ 유지 - Type 2 and 3 ships carry products of progressively lesser hazards.
[줄 1967] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Where a ship is intended to carry a range of products it is assigned the standard applicable to the product having the most stringent ship type requirement.
[줄 1968] [87.5%] (7/8) ✅ 유지 - The IBC Code also defines cargo tank types.
[줄 1969] [94.4%] (17/18) ✅ 유지 - Tank type 1 is an independent tank that is not contiguous with, or part of, the hull structure.
[줄 1970] [83.3%] (15/18) ✅ 유지 - Tank type 2 is an integral tank, i.e it is part of the ship's hull structure.
[줄 1971] [89.3%] (25/28) ✅ 유지 - A gravity tank is an independent or integral tank that has a design pressure of not more than 0.7 bar gage at the top of the tank.
[줄 1972] [84.2%] (16/19) ✅ 유지 - A pressure tank is an independent tank that has a design pressure of more than 0.7 bar gage.
[줄 1973] [86.7%] (52/60) ✅ 유지 - The IBC Code specifies for each individual product to be carried the ship type and required tank type, e.g sulfuric acidship type 3tank type 2G Also, requirements for the materials of construction, freeboard, stability, general arrangement, piping arrangements, electrical and environmental arrangements, tank venting and gas freeing, fire protection, etc of chemical tankers are covered by the IBC Code.
[줄 1974] [57.9%] (11/19) ❌ 제거 - Figure 22.4 shows a 130 m LOA type II oil products/chemical tanker of 12,700 tonnes deadweight.
[줄 1975] [83.3%] (25/30) ✅ 유지 - The 130 meter length overall by 20 meter breadth by 9.75 meter depth vessel has 12 cargo tanks, equipped to carry six different types or grades of cargo simultaneously.
[줄 1976] [88.2%] (30/34) ✅ 유지 - Each tank has a deepwell pump rated at 300 cubic meters per hour and the ship's maximum discharge rate is 1800 cubic meters per hour with six lines working at the same time.
[줄 1977] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Further reading Code for the Construction and Equipment of Ships Carrying Dangerous Chemicals in Bulk .
[줄 1978] [75.0%] (3/4) ✅ 유지 - IMO publication, 2005 edition.

[줄 1980] [100.0%] (7/7) ✅ 유지 - Design and operation of double hull tankers.

[줄 2028] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Membrane tanks These are non-self-supporting tanks consisting of a thin layer supported through insulation by the adjacent hull structure.
[줄 2029] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - The membrane is designed in such a way that thermal and other expansion or contraction is compensated for without undue stressing of the membrane.
[줄 2030] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - Membrane tanks are primarily used for LNG cargoes.
[줄 2031] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Semi-membrane tanks These are non-self-supporting tanks in the load condition.
[줄 2032] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - The flat portions of the tank are supported, transferring the weight and dynamic forces through the hull, but the rounded corners and edges are not supported so that tank expansion and contraction is accommodated.
[줄 2033] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Such tanks were developed for the carriage of LNG, but have been used for a few LPG ships.
[줄 2034] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - Independent tanks These are self-supporting and independent of the hull.
[줄 2035] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - There are three types: 'Type A', which are designed primarily using standard traditional methods of ship structural analysis.
[줄 2036] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - LPG at or near atmospheric pressure or LNG may be carried in such tanks.
[줄 2037] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - 'Type B', which are designed using more sophisticated analytical tools and methods to determine stress levels, fatigue life, and crack propagation characteristics.
[줄 2038] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - The overall design concept of these tanks is based on the so-called 'crack detection before failure principle', which permits their use with a reduced secondary barrier.
[줄 2039] [100.0%] (7/7) ✅ 유지 - LNG is normally carried in such tanks.
[줄 2040] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - 'Type C', which are designed as pressure vessels, the dominant design criteria being the vapor pressure.
[줄 2041] [100.0%] (7/7) ✅ 유지 - Normally used for LPG and occasionally ethylene.
[줄 2042] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - Internal insulation tanks These are non-self-supporting and consist of thermal insulation materials, the inner surface of which is exposed to the cargo supported by the adjacent inner hull or an independent tank.
[줄 2043] [95.8%] (23/24) ✅ 유지 - There are two types: 'Type 1', where the insulation or combination of insulation and one or more liners act only as the primary barrier.
[줄 2044] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - The inner hull or independent tank forms the secondary barrier.
[줄 2045] [96.4%] (27/28) ✅ 유지 - 'Type 2', where the insulation or combination of insulation and one or more liners act as both the primary and secondary barriers and are clearly distinguishable as such.
[줄 2046] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - The liners on their own do not act as liquid barriers and therefore differ from membranes.
[줄 2047] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - These tanks are a later addition to the Code and Type 1 is known to have been used for the carriage of LPG.

[줄 2195] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - Masts and Sampson posts Masts on a general cargo ship may fulfill a number of functions, but their prime use in modern ships is to carry and support the derricks used for cargo handling.

[줄 2206] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Mast construction and stiffening Tubular steel sections are commonly used in mast and post construction, the sections being rolled in short lengths and welded in the shipyard.
[줄 2207] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - The short lengths may be tapered and are of different plate thicknesses to allow for the greater stresses experienced at the base of the mast.
[줄 2208] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - Where connections are made for fittings such as the gooseneck and a masthead span swivel, doubling or welded reinforcing pads may be provided.
[줄 2209] [97.0%] (32/33) ✅ 유지 - To obtain the necessary mast scantlings, excessive doubling or internal stiffeners are rarely found in modern practice, except where a heavier derrick than that for which the mast was originally designed is carried.
[줄 2210] [96.9%] (31/32) ✅ 유지 - Higher tensile steels are often used to advantage in mast construction, giving less weight high up in the ship and dispensing with the need for any form of support, without excessive scantlings.
[줄 2211] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Cross-trees, mast tables, etc may be fabricated from welded steel plates and sections.
[줄 2212] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Derrick booms are as a rule welded lengths of seamless tubular steel.
[줄 2213] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - The middle length may have a greater diameter to allow for the bending moment, to which the boom is subject in addition to the axial thrust.
[줄 2214] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - At the base of the mast adequate rigidity must be provided, the amount of additional structural stiffening increasing with the size of derricks carried by the mast.
[줄 2215] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Many cargo ships have mast houses into which the masts are built, the house being suitably strengthened.
[줄 2216] [92.0%] (23/25) ✅ 유지 - These houses need not be designed to support the mast, the structure being of light scantlings and the support provided by stiffening in the tweens.
[줄 2217] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - Where the house is strengthened the masts or posts generally land on the upper deck, but where heavy derricks are installed the mast may then land on the upper tween deck.
[줄 2218] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Since the derricks and mast are as a rule midway between holds they land over the hold transverse bulkheads, which lend further support.
[줄 2219] [94.6%] (35/37) ✅ 유지 - Heavy derrick masts will require extensive stiffening arrangements in the mast house, and also in the tweens, with support for the transverse bulkhead so that the loads are transmitted through the structure to the ship's bottom.
[줄 2220] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Partial longitudinal and transverse bulkheads with deck girders may provide the mast house stiffening.
[줄 2221] [93.1%] (27/29) ✅ 유지 - Stiffened plate webs at the ship's center line in the tweens and heavier stiffeners on the transverse bulkhead in the hold then provide the additional strengthening below decks.
[줄 2222] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Heavy insert plates are fitted in way of the mast at the various decks.

[줄 2242] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Forces in derrick rigs The geometry of the derrick rig will to a large extent influence the loads carried by the rig components.
[줄 2243] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - Those dimensions that have the greatest influence are the length of boom, the distance between the boom heel and the masthead span connection, and the angle at which the boom is topped.
[줄 2244] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - When the ratio between boom length and height of suspension is increased, the boom thrust will be higher; therefore, should a long boom be required the height of suspension must be adequate.
[줄 2245] [100.0%] (42/42) ✅ 유지 - It is not unusual, however, for shipowners to object to having posts at the bridge front and if the height of suspension is then restricted there is some limitation on the boom length, which can make working cargo from that position difficult.
[줄 2246] [100.0%] (40/40) ✅ 유지 - The angle at which the derrick is topped has no effect on the axial thrust, but the lead from the cargo purchase often increases the thrust as it is led parallel to the boom on all except heavy lift derricks.
[줄 2247] [94.4%] (17/18) ✅ 유지 - Loads carried by the span are dependent on both the ratio of boom length to height of suspensionandtheangleatwhichthederrickistopped.
[줄 2248] [93.3%] (14/15) ✅ 유지 - Thespanloadisgreateratalower angle to the horizontal, and increases with longer booms for a given suspension height.
[줄 2249] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - To determine these forces simple space and force diagrams may be drawn and the resultant forces determined to give the required wire sizes, block and connection safe working loads, and the thrust experienced by the boom.
[줄 2250] [95.0%] (19/20) ✅ 유지 - The horizontal and vertical components of the span load and boom thrust are also used to determine the mast scantlings.
[줄 2251] [88.9%] (16/18) ✅ 유지 - Force diagrams are shown for the rig components of the single swinging derrick illustrated in Figure 24.6.
[줄 2252] [92.9%] (39/42) ✅ 유지 - For a safe working load of 15 tonnes or less the forces may be calculated with the derrick at angles of 30  and 70  to the horizontal unless the owner specifies that the derrick is to be used at a lower angle.

[줄 2260] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - The loads on all the blocks except the lower block of a cargo purchase will be the resultant of the two forces to which the block is subjected.
[줄 2261] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - A single-sheave block has a safe working load that is half the resultant, and multi-sheave blocks have a safe working load that is the same as the resultant.
[줄 2262] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - In determining the span loads and boom thrusts, not only is the derrick safe working load considered to be supported by the span, but also the weight of the cargo purchase and half the boom weight.
[줄 2263] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - The other half of the boom weight is supported by the gooseneck fitting.
[줄 2264] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Allowances must be made for the frictional resistance of the blocks when determining the forces.
[줄 2265] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - This includes an allowance for the rope friction, i.e the effort required to bend and unbend the rope around the pulley, as well as an allowance for journal friction.
[줄 2266] [90.2%] (74/82) ✅ 유지 - Shipbuilders using British Standards adopt the following assumed cumulative friction values: Small and medium sheaves 8% sheave with bushed plain bearings 5% sheave with ball or roller bearings Large diameter sheaves 6% sheave with bushed plain bearings 4% sheave with ball or roller bearings Derrick exceeding 80 tonnes SWL 5% sheave with bushed plain bearings 3% sheave with ball or roller bearings Force diagrams that are more involved than those for the single swinging derrick are prepared for the union purchase rig.
[줄 2267] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - These diagrams indicate the safe working load of the rig, the 'limiting height', the boom thrusts, and the optimum guy leads.
[줄 2268] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - The 'limiting height' is that height below which all positions of the lifted weight will result in an included angle between the outboard and inboard runners of less than 120 .
[줄 2269] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - At 120 , if the boom heads are level the inboard and outboard runners will experience a force equivalent to the cargo weight.
[줄 2270] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Usually the runner size determines the safe working load in union purchase, but the thrust experienced by the derrick boom can determine this value where only light derricks are fitted.
[줄 2271] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - The positioning of the guys may be important to the loads experienced by the span and the guys themselves.
[줄 2272] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - If these are at too narrow an angle to the boom, excessive tension in the guys will result; a good lead is therefore essential.
[줄 2273] [97.4%] (37/38) ✅ 유지 - Unfortunately, in practice the magnitude of the guy loads is not always appreciated, but more attention has been paid to this problem of late and preventers are now often set up to reduce the load in the guy.
[줄 2274] [90.5%] (19/21) ✅ 유지 - There is available a suitable preventer for this purpose; the use of old runners etc as preventers should not be tolerated.
[줄 2275] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - In union purchase rigs it is possible to obtain a condition where the load comes off the outboard span, and the boom may then close to the mast under load.
[줄 2276] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - This condition is referred to as 'jack-knifing', and may be apparent from the force diagram prepared for the rig, since the triangle of forces does not close.
[줄 2277] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - At the design stage the guy positions can be adjusted to avoid this happening.
[줄 2278] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - In practice this condition appears to occur occasionally where derricks are used in union purchase at the bridge front.
[줄 2279] [96.4%] (27/28) ✅ 유지 - Here the positioning of the guys is made difficult by the presence of the bridge structure, but the correct placing of a suitable preventer should overcome this problem.
[줄 2280] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - Studies by IMO and the US National Academy of Sciences confirmed the effectiveness of the double hull in preventing oil spills caused by grounding and collision where the inner hull is not breached.
[줄 2281] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - The mid-deck tanker was shown to have more favorable outflow performance in extreme accidents where the inner hull is breached.
[줄 2282] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - The United States authorities considered grounding the most prevalent type of accident in their waters and believed only the double-hull type prevented spills from tanker groundings in all but the most severe incidents.
[줄 2283] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - Thus, whilst MARPOL provided for the acceptance of alternative tanker designs, the United States legislation did not, and no alternative designs were built.
[줄 2284] [93.5%] (29/31) ✅ 유지 - As the result of the break-up of the tanker Erika and subsequent pollution of the French coastline in 1999, IMO members decided to accelerate the phase-out of singlehull tankers.
[줄 2285] [91.3%] (21/23) ✅ 유지 - As a result, in April 2001 a stricter timetable for the phasing out of single-hull tankers entered into force in September 2003.
[줄 2286] [84.8%] (28/33) ✅ 유지 - In December 2003 a decision to further accelerate the phase-out dates of single-hull tankers was agreed, PreMARPOL tankers being phased out in 2005 and MARPOL tankers and small tankers in 2010.
[줄 2287] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Oil tankers now generally have a single pump space aft, adjacent to the machinery, and specified slop tanks into which tank washings and oily residues are pumped.
[줄 2288] [91.4%] (32/35) ✅ 유지 - Tank cleaning may be accomplished by water-driven rotating machines on the smaller tankers but for new crude oil tankers of 20,000 tonnes deadweight and above the tank cleaning system uses crude oil washing.
[줄 2289] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Passenger ships Early passenger ships did not have the tiers of superstructure associated with modern vessels, and they also had a narrower beam in relation to their length.
[줄 2290] [96.0%] (24/25) ✅ 유지 - The reason for the absence of superstructure decks was the Merchant Shipping Act 1894, which limited the number of passengers carried on the upper deck.
[줄 2291] [95.0%] (19/20) ✅ 유지 - An amendment to this Act in 1906 removed this restriction and vessels were then built with several tiers of superstructures.
[줄 2292] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - This produced problems of strength and stability, stability being improved by an increase in beam.
[줄 2293] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - The transmission of stresses to the superstructure from the main hull girder created much difference of opinion as to the means of overcoming the problem.
[줄 2294] [90.0%] (27/30) ✅ 유지 - Both light structures of a discontinuous nature, i.e fitted with expansion joints, and superstructures withheavier scantlings able to contribute to the strength of the main hull girder were introduced.
[줄 2295] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - Present practice, where the length of the superstructure is appreciable and has its sides at the ship side, does not require the fitting of expansion joints.
[줄 2296] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - The introduction of aluminum alloy superstructures provided increased passenger accommodation on the same draft, and/or a lowering of the lightweight center of gravity with improved stability.
[줄 2297] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - This was brought about by the lighter weight of the aluminum alloy structure.
[줄 2298] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Subsequent experience, however, has shown that for passenger liners, that are required to maintain a service speed in a seaway, the maintenance costs of aluminum alloy superstructures can be higher.
[줄 2299] [81.9%] (59/72) ✅ 유지 - Initial tests and re-tests of derrick rigs To comply with the national and class regulations, ships' derricks designed to operate as single swinging derricks are initially tested with a proof load that exceeds the specified safe working load of the derrick by the following amounts: SWL less than 20 tonnes25% in excess of SWL SWL 20–50 tonnes5 tonnes in excess of SWL SWL over 50 tonnes10% in excess of SWL.
[줄 2300] [93.3%] (28/30) ✅ 유지 - Heavy-lift derricks are tested at an angle of not more than 45  to the horizontal and other derricks at an angle of not more than 30  to the horizontal.
[줄 2301] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - During the test the boom is swung as far as possible in both directions, and any derrick intended to be raised by power under load is raised to its maximum working angle at the outermost position.
[줄 2302] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Before the test for a heavy derrick it is usual to ensure that the vessel has adequate transverse stability.
[줄 2303] [97.9%] (47/48) ✅ 유지 - Before, during, and after all tests it is necessary to ensure that none of the components of the rig show signs of any failure, and it is good practice to have a preventer rigged during the test as a precaution against any of the span gear carrying away.
[줄 2304] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - On completion of the test the heel of the derrick boom is clearly marked with: 1.

[줄 2307] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - Its safe working load in union purchase, if it is designed for that purpose, the letter 'U' preceding the safe working load.

[줄 2322] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Stern and bow doors Roll-on roll-off vessels are used primarily on short sea crossings and are designed to carry road vehicles.
[줄 2323] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - They provide a link in a road journey, often overnight, and the speed of loading and unloading is often critical.
[줄 2324] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - The vehicles are driven on and off using large doors and a series of ramps to access different deck levels.
[줄 2325] [90.9%] (20/22) ✅ 유지 - Ro-ro vessels may be fitted with stern doors of the hinge-down or hinge-up type, which if large are articulated.
[줄 2326] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - Bow doors are either of the visor type or of the sidehinged type.
[줄 2327] [94.6%] (35/37) ✅ 유지 - These are situated above the freeboard deck and where the bow doors lead to a complete or long forward enclosed superstructure, Lloyd's require an inner door to be fitted that is part of the collision bulkhead.
[줄 2328] [94.9%] (37/39) ✅ 유지 - This would also be in keeping with the SOLAS requirements for passenger ships, where the collision bulkhead is to be extended weathertight to the deck next above the bulkhead deck, but need not be fitted directly above that bulkhead.
[줄 2329] [90.9%] (20/22) ✅ 유지 - A sloping weathertight vehicle ramp may be fitted in some ships to form the collision bulkhead above the freeboard deck Ship Construction.

[줄 2336] [91.8%] (45/49) ✅ 유지 - Ramps Ro-ro ships fitted with ramps usually have a stern ramp, but some vessels fitted with bow doors may also have a bow ramp that doubles as the inner weathertight door and is lowered onto a linkspan when the bow visor or side-hinged doors have been opened.
[줄 2337] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Ramps may also be fitted internally to give access from deck to deck.
[줄 2338] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - These can be hydraulically or mechanically tilted to serve more than one deck and can be fixed in the horizontal position to serve as decks themselves.
[줄 2339] [94.1%] (16/17) ✅ 유지 - In some ships they can even be raised into the hatch space and serve as weathertight covers.

[줄 2375] [95.0%] (38/40) ✅ 유지 - Cargo restraint In ro-ro and container ships the lashing of cargo is an important safety consideration and usually calls for fittings that will permit rapid and easy but effective securing of the cargo because of short ship turnaround times.
[줄 2376] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - The shipbuilder is responsible for the deck and perhaps hatch fittings for the securing devices, and will look to the ship operator for guidance on their type and positions.
[줄 2377] [91.9%] (34/37) ✅ 유지 - On the decks of ro-ro ships where the direction of lashing is unpredictable and vehicles must transverse the fitting, a cloverleaf deck socket in conjunction with an elephant's foot type of end lashing is popular.
[줄 2378] [96.8%] (30/31) ✅ 유지 - Containers have very little strength in any direction other thanvertically through the corner posts, thus it is necessary to provide substantial support to the containers when they are on the ship.
[줄 2379] [100.0%] (43/43) ✅ 유지 - Stowage of containers is with their longer dimension fore and aft since the ship motion transmitted to cargo is greater in rolling than pitching and it is therefore prudent to limit any possible cargo movement within the container to the shorter transverse dimension.
[줄 2380] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Also, of course, when offloading the fore and aft container is more easily received by road or rail transport.
[줄 2381] [91.3%] (42/46) ✅ 유지 - Below-decks containers are restrained in vertical cell guides, which are typically 150  150  12 angles and they are structurally supported so that any dynamic forces other than purely vertical are transmitted as much as possible through the ship's structure and not into the containers.
[줄 2382] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - The cell guides are not to form an integral part of the ship's structure, they are to be so designed that they do not carry the main hull stresses.
[줄 2383] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Where four container corners are adjacent the cell guides may be built into a composite pillar.
[줄 2384] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - The clearance between container and cell guide is critical.
[줄 2385] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - If it is too small the container will
[줄 2386] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - jam, if it is too large when one container lands on the one below the corner posts and castings that accept a maximum eccentricity may not mate.
[줄 2387] [85.0%] (17/20) ✅ 유지 - Lloyd's stipulate a maximum clearance of 25 mm in the transverse direction and 40 mm in the longitudinal direction.
[줄 2388] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - The tolerances are such that the cell guides have to be fitted to an accuracy exceeding normal shipyard practice with the use of jigs to ensure the dimensions are maintained following welding.
[줄 2389] [89.7%] (26/29) ✅ 유지 - Lloyd's require that the cell guide not deviate from its intended line by more than 4 mm in the transverse direction and 5 mm in the longitudinal direction.
[줄 2390] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - Lead-in devices are fitted at the top of the guides.

[줄 2504] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - Cargo pumping and piping arrangements in tankers Cargo pumps are provided in tankers to load and discharge cargo, and also to ballast some of the tanks, which becomes necessary when making voyages in the unloaded condition.
[줄 2505] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Many modern tankers have clean ballast capacity and these tanks are served by a separate pumping system.
[줄 2506] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - The particular cargo pumping system adopted depends very much on the range of cargo carried.

[줄 2508] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Where smaller tankers carry a number of oil products at one time, which must be kept separate, the pumping system is more complex.

[줄 2518] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Multi-product tankers Where a number of oil products are carried, the more complex pumping arrangements require two and in some cases three pump rooms to be fitted.

[줄 2520] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - On many older tankers the piping was often arranged on the 'ring main' system to provide flexibility of pumping conditions.
[줄 2521] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - To obtain the optimum number of different pumping combinations in modern multiproduct carriers the tanks may be fitted with individual suction lines.
[줄 2522] [92.9%] (39/42) ✅ 유지 - Cargo pumps Initially, on modern tankers the main cargo pumps were of the centrifugal type, either geared turbine or motor driven, and had a very high pumping capacity, those on the large tankers being capable of discharging say 3500 m 3 /hour.
[줄 2523] [91.9%] (34/37) ✅ 유지 - Because of their high capacities the centrifugal cargo pumps are unsuitable for emptying tanks completely, and for this purpose reciprocating stripping pumps with capacities of, say, 350 m 3 /hour are provided with a separate stripping line.
[줄 2524] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - More recent developments have seen the use of individual hydraulically driven submerged cargo pumps in the cargo tanks with a single discharge line and the conventional pump room dispensed with.
[줄 2525] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Also, cargo tanks are being fitted with submerged cargo pumps driven by explosion-proof electric motors.
[줄 2526] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - Tanker cargo discharge systems are now often fully computerized.
[줄 2527] [100.0%] (41/41) ✅ 유지 - Cargo tank ventilators The cargo tank ventilators are to be entirely separate from air pipes from other compartments of the tanker and positioned so that flammable vapor emissions cannot be admitted to other spaces or areas containing any source of ignition.
[줄 2528] [93.3%] (42/45) ✅ 유지 - Cargo tank protection Oil tankers of less than 20,000 tonnes deadweight are required to be fitted with a fixed deck foam system capable of delivering foam to the entire cargo tanks deck area and into any tank the deck of which has been ruptured.

[줄 2530] [86.4%] (19/22) ✅ 유지 - Oil tankers of 20,000 tonnes deadweight or more should have a fixed deck foam system and a fixed inert gas system.
[줄 2531] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - Inert gas system The inert gas system is to be so designed and operated as to render and maintain the atmosphere of the cargo tanks nonflammable, other than when the tanks are gas free.
[줄 2532] [95.7%] (44/46) ✅ 유지 - Hydrocarbon gas normally encountered in oil tanks cannot burn in an atmosphere containing less than 11% of oxygen by volume, thus if the oxygen content in a cargo tank is kept below, say, 8% by volume fire or explosion in the vapor space should not occur.
[줄 2533] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - Inert gas introduced into the tank will reduce the air content.
[줄 2534] [91.7%] (33/36) ✅ 유지 - On an oil tanker, inert gas may be produced by one of two processes: 1 Ships with main or auxiliary boilers normally use the flue gas, which contains typically only 2–4% by volume of oxygen.
[줄 2535] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - This is scrubbed with sea water to cool it and to remove sulfur dioxide and particulates, and it is then blown into the tanks through a fixed pipe distribution system.
[줄 2536] [95.2%] (20/21) ✅ 유지 - On diesel-engined ships the engine exhaust gas will contain too high an oxygen level for use as an inert gas.
[줄 2537] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - An inert gas generating plant may then be used to produce gas by burning diesel or light fuel oil.
[줄 2538] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - The gas is scrubbed and used in the same way as boiler flue gas.
[줄 2539] [95.0%] (38/40) ✅ 유지 - Nonreturn barriers in the form of a deck water seal, and nonreturn valve are maintained between the machinery space and deck distribution system to ensure no petroleum gas or liquid petroleum passes back through the system to the machinery space.
[줄 2540] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - The double-hull and double-bottom spaces of tankers required to have an inert gas system are to have connections for the supply of inert gas.
[줄 2541] [97.4%] (38/39) ✅ 유지 - Cargo tank purging and gas freeing When the tanker is fitted with an inert gas system, the discharged cargo tanks are purged until the hydrocarbon vapors in the cargo tanks have been reduced to less than 2% by volume.
[줄 2542] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Gas freeing may then take place at the cargo tank deck level.
[줄 2543] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - For tankers not provided with an inert gas system the flammable vapor is discharged initially through the tank venting outlets specified by MARPOL.
[줄 2544] [96.4%] (27/28) ✅ 유지 - When the flammable vapor concentration at the outlet has been reduced to 30% of the lower flammable limit, gas freeing can be continued at cargo tank deck level.
[줄 2545] [88.9%] (24/27) ✅ 유지 - A range of portable gas-freeing fans with associated equipment is readily available, with typical air movement ranging from 8000 to 15,000 cubic meters per hour.
[줄 2546] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - Cargo tank washing After discharge of cargoes, oil tanker cargo tanks can be cleaned by either hot or cold water, fresh or sea water, or by crude oil washing.
[줄 2547] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - Water cleaning machines can be fixed in a tank or may be portable, the portable machine being connected by hose to a deck water main before being introduced through a tank-cleaning hatch into the tank.

[줄 2576] [89.7%] (26/29) ✅ 유지 - ballast tanks 342 Further reading 343 Some useful websites 343 Nature and forms of corrosion There is a natural tendency for nearly all metals to react with their environment.
[줄 2577] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - The result of this reaction is the creation of a corrosion product that is generally a substance of very similar chemical composition to the original mineral from which the metal was produced.
[줄 2578] [100.0%] (3/3) ✅ 유지 - All rights reserved.
[줄 2579] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Atmospheric corrosion Protection against atmospheric corrosion is important during the construction of a ship, both on the building berth and in the shops.
[줄 2580] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - Serious rusting may occur where the relative humidity is above about 70%; the atmosphere in many shipyards is unfortunately sufficiently humid to permit atmospheric corrosion throughout most of the year.
[줄 2581] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - However, even in humid atmospheres the rate of rusting is determined mainly by the pollution of the air through smoke and/or sea salts.
[줄 2582] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Corrosion due to immersion When a ship is in service the bottom area is completely immersed and the waterline or boot topping region may be intermittently immersed in sea water.
[줄 2583] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Under normal operating conditions a great deal of care is required to prevent excessive corrosion of these portions of the hull.
[줄 2584] [94.1%] (16/17) ✅ 유지 - A steel hull in this environment can provide ideal conditions for the formation of electrochemical corrosion cells.
[줄 2585] [94.1%] (16/17) ✅ 유지 - Electrochemical nature of corrosion Any metal, in tending to revert to its original mineral state, releases energy.
[줄 2586] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - At ordinary temperatures in aqueous solutions the transformation of a metal atom into a mineral molecule occurs by the metal passing into solution.
[줄 2587] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - During this process the atom loses one or more electrons and becomes an ion, i.e an electrically charged atom, with the production of an electric current.
[줄 2588] [93.3%] (14/15) ✅ 유지 - This reaction may only occur if an electron acceptor is present in the aqueous solution.
[줄 2589] [100.0%] (35/35) ✅ 유지 - Thus, any corrosion reaction is always accompanied by a flow of electricity from one metallic area to another through a solution in which the conduction of an electric current occurs by the passage of ions.
[줄 2590] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Such a solution is referred to as an electrolyte solution, and because of its high salt content sea water is a good electrolyte solution.
[줄 2591] [90.0%] (18/20) ✅ 유지 - A simple corrosion cell is formed by two different metals in an electrolyte solution, as illustrated in Figure 27.1.
[줄 2592] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - It is not essential to have two different metals, as we shall see later.
[줄 2593] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - As illustrated, a pure iron plate and a similar pure copper plate are immersed in a sodium chloride solution that is in contact with oxygen at the surface.
[줄 2594] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Without any connection the corrosion reaction on each plate would be small.
[줄 2595] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Once the two plates are connected externally to form an electrical path, then the corrosion rate of the iron will increase considerably and the corrosion on the copper will cease.
[줄 2596] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - The iron electrode, by means of which the electrons leave the cell and by way of which the conventional current enters the cell, is the anode.
[줄 2597] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - This is the electrode at which the oxidation or corrosion normally takes place.
[줄 2598] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - The copper electrode, by means of which the electrons enter the cell and by way of which the conventional current leaves the cell, is the cathode, at which no corrosion occurs.
[줄 2599] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - A passage of current through the electrolyte solution is by means of a flow of negative ions to the anode and a flow of positive ions to the cathode.
[줄 2600] [91.7%] (22/24) ✅ 유지 - Electrochemical corrosion in aqueous solutions will result from any anodic and cathodic areas coupled in the solution, whether they are metals of different potential
[줄 2601] [84.0%] (42/50) ✅ 유지 - Conventional current Oxygen Anode iron Cathode copper Conventional current + ve ions –ve ions Sodium chloride solution GALVANIC CELL –ve ions –ve ions Oxygen Sea water CORROSION CELL SET UP BY BREAKS IN MILLSCALE OR PAINT FILM ON PLATE SURFACE Millscale or paint Anode Cathode Cathode Figure 27.1 Corrosion cell.
[줄 2602] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - in the environment or they possess different potentials as the result of physical differences on the metal surface.
[줄 2603] [96.4%] (27/28) ✅ 유지 - The latter is typified by steel plate carrying broken millscale in sea water or corrosion currents flowing between areas of well-painted plate and areas of defective paintwork.
[줄 2604] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - In atmospheric corrosion and corrosion involving immersion, both oxygen and an electrolyte play an important part.
[줄 2605] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Plates freely exposed to the atmosphere will receive plenty of oxygen but little moisture, and the moisture present therefore becomes the controlling factor.
[줄 2606] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Under conditions of total immersion it is the presence of oxygen that becomes the controlling factor.
[줄 2607] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - Bimetallic corrosion Although it is true to say that all corrosion is basically galvanic, the term 'galvanic corrosion' is usually applied when two different metals form a corrosion cell.
[줄 2608] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Many ship corrosion problems are associated with the coupling of metallic parts of different potential, which consequently form corrosion cells under service conditions.
[줄 2609] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - The corrosion rates of metals and alloys in sea water have been extensively investigated and as a result galvanic series of metals and alloys in sea water have been obtained.
[줄 2610] [84.6%] (11/13) ✅ 유지 - A typical galvanic series in sea water is shown in Table 27.1.
[줄 2611] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - The positions of the metals in the table apply only in a sea water environment, and where metals are grouped together they have no strong tendency to form couples with each other.
[줄 2612] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Some metals appear twice because they are capable of having both a passive and an active state.
[줄 2613] [96.1%] (73/76) ✅ 유지 - A metal is said to be passive when the surface is exposed to an electrolyte solution and a reaction is expected but the metal shows no sign of Table 27.1 Galvanic series of metals and alloys in sea water Noble end Platinum, gold Silver Titanium Stainless steels, passive Nickel, passive High-duty bronzes Copper Nickel, active Millscale Naval brass Lead, tin Stainless steels, active Iron, steel, cast iron Aluminum alloys Aluminum Zinc Magnesium Ignoble end
[줄 2614] [96.2%] (25/26) ✅ 유지 - It is generally agreed that passivation results from the formation of a current barrier on the metal surface, usually in the form of an oxide film.
[줄 2615] [100.0%] (35/35) ✅ 유지 - This thin protective film forms, and a change in the overall potential of the metal occurs when a critical current density is exceeded at the anodes of the local corrosion cells on the metal surface.
[줄 2616] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - Among the more common bimetallic corrosion cell problems in ship hulls are those formed by the mild steel hull with the bronze or nickel alloy propeller.
[줄 2617] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Also, above-the-waterline problems exist with the attachment of bronze and aluminum alloy fittings.
[줄 2618] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Where aluminum superstructures are introduced, the attachment to the steel hull and the fitting of steel equipment to the superstructure require special attention.
[줄 2619] [90.9%] (20/22) ✅ 유지 - This latter problem is overcome by insulating the two metals and preventing the ingress of water, as illustrated in Figure 27.2.
[줄 2620] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - A further development is the use of explosion-bonded aluminum/steel transition joints, also illustrated.
[줄 2621] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - These joints are free of any crevices, the exposed aluminum-to-steel interface being readily protected by paint.
[줄 2622] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Stress corrosion Corrosion and subsequent failure associated with varying forms of applied stress is not uncommon in marine structures.
[줄 2623] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Internal stresses produced by non-uniform cold working are often more dangerous than applied stresses.
[줄 2624] [90.9%] (10/11) ✅ 유지 - For example, localized corrosion is often evident at cold flanged brackets.
[줄 2625] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - Corrosion/erosion Erosion is essentially a mechanical action but it is associated with electrochemical corrosion in producing two forms of metal deterioration.
[줄 2626] [94.7%] (18/19) ✅ 유지 - Firstly, in what is known as 'impingement attack', the action is mainly electrochemical but it is initiated by erosion.
[줄 2627] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Air bubbles entrained in the flow of water and striking a metal surface may erode away any protective film that may be present locally.
[줄 2628] [91.7%] (11/12) ✅ 유지 - The eroded surface becomes anodic to the surrounding surface and corrosion occurs.
[줄 2629] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - This type of attack can occur in most places where there is water flow, but particularly where features give rise to turbulent flow.
[줄 2630] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Sea water discharges from the hull are a particular case, the effects being worse if warm water is discharged.
[줄 2631] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - Cavitation damage is also associated with a rapidly flowing liquid environment.
[줄 2632] [100.0%] (6/6) ✅ 유지 - At certain regions in the flow
[줄 2633] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - the local pressures drop below that of the absolute vapor pressure.
[줄 2634] [96.2%] (25/26) ✅ 유지 - Vapor cavities, i.e areas of partial vacuum, are formed locally, but when the pressure increases clear of this region the vapor cavities collapse or 'implode'.
[줄 2635] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - This collapse occurs with the release of considerable energy, and if it occurs adjacent to a metal surface damage results.
[줄 2636] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - The damage shows itself as pitting, which is thought to be predominantly due to the effects of the mechanical damage.
[줄 2637] [94.7%] (18/19) ✅ 유지 - However, it is also considered that electrochemical action may play some part in the damage after the initial erosion.
[줄 2638] [87.5%] (7/8) ✅ 유지 - Aluminum house side Aluminum washer Sealing compound Galvd.

[줄 2643] [93.1%] (27/29) ✅ 유지 - Corrosion allowance Plate and section scantlings specified for ships in the rules of classification societies include corrosion additions to the thickness, generally based on a 25-year service life.
[줄 2644] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - The corrosion allowance is based on the concept that corrosion occurs on the exposed surface of the material at a constant rate, no matter how much material lies behind it.
[줄 2645] [92.9%] (26/28) ✅ 유지 - That is, if a plate is 8 or 80 mm thick, corrosion will take place at the same rate, not at a faster rate in the thicker plate.
[줄 2646] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Some shipowners may specify thicker material than is required by the classification society, where there are plans for long-term ownership.
[줄 2647] [95.8%] (23/24) ✅ 유지 - Corrosion control The control of corrosion may be broadly considered in two forms, cathodic protection and the application of protective coatings, i.e paints.
[줄 2648] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Cathodic protection Only where metals are immersed in an electrolyte can the possible onset of corrosion be prevented by cathodic protection.
[줄 2649] [95.2%] (20/21) ✅ 유지 - The fundamental principle of cathodic protection is that the anodic corrosion reactions are suppressed by the application of an opposing current.
[줄 2650] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - This superimposed direct electric current enters the metal at every point, lowering the potential of the anode metal of the local corrosion cells so that they become cathodes.
[줄 2651] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - There are two main types of cathodic protection installation, sacrificial anode systems and impressed current systems.
[줄 2652] [84.4%] (27/32) ✅ 유지 - Sacri fi cial anode systems Sacrificial anodes are metals or alloys attached to the hull that have a more anodic, i.e less noble, potential than steel when immersed in sea water.
[줄 2653] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - These anodes supply the cathodic protection current, but will be consumed in doing so and therefore require replacement for the protection to be maintained.
[줄 2654] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - This system has been used for many years, the fitting of zinc plates in way of bronze propellers and other immersed fittings being common practice.
[줄 2655] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Initially, results with zinc anodes were not always very effective owing to the use of unsuitable zinc alloys.
[줄 2656] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Modern anodes are based on alloys of zinc, aluminum, or magnesium, which have undergone many tests to examine their suitability; high-purity zinc anodes are also used.
[줄 2657] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - The cost, with various other practical considerations, may decide which type is to be fitted.
[줄 2658] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Sacrificial anodes may be fitted within the hull, and are often fitted in ballast tanks.
[줄 2659] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - However, magnesium anodes are not used in the cargo-ballast tanks of oil carriers owing to the 'spark hazard'.
[줄 2660] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Should any part of the anode fall and strike the tank structure when gaseous conditions exist, an explosion could result.
[줄 2661] [91.7%] (22/24) ✅ 유지 - Aluminum anode systems may be employed in tankers provided they are only fitted in locations where the potential energy is less than 28 kgm.
[줄 2662] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Impressed current systems These systems are applicable to the protection of the immersed external hull only.
[줄 2663] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - The principle of the systems is that a voltage difference is maintained between the hull and fitted anodes, which will protect the hull against corrosion, but not overprotect it, thus wasting current.
[줄 2664] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - For normal operating conditions the potential difference is maintained by means of an externally mounted silver/silver chloride reference cell detecting the voltage difference between itself and the hull.
[줄 2665] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - An amplifier controller is used to amplify the micro-range reference cell current, and it compares this with the preset protective potential value that is to be maintained.
[줄 2666] [92.9%] (26/28) ✅ 유지 - Using the amplified DC signal from the controller, a saturable reactor controls a larger current from the ship's electrical system that is supplied to the hull anodes.
[줄 2667] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - An AC current from the electrical system would be rectified before distribution to the anodes.
[줄 2668] [71.4%] (5/7) ✅ 유지 - Figure 27.3 shows such a system.
[줄 2669] [76.0%] (19/25) ✅ 유지 - Originally consumable anodes were employed, but in recent systems nonconsumable relativelynoble metalsareused; these include lead/silverand platinum/palladiumalloys, and platinized titanium anodes are also used.
[줄 2670] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - A similar impressed current system employs a consumable anode in the form of an aluminum wire up to 45 meters long that is trailed behind the ship whilst at sea.
[줄 2671] [100.0%] (6/6) ✅ 유지 - No protection is provided in port.
[줄 2672] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - Although the initial cost is high, these systems are claimed to be more flexible, to have a longer life, to reduce significantly hull maintenance, and to weigh less than the sacrificial anode systems.
[줄 2673] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Care is required in their use in port alongside ships or other unprotected steel structures.
[줄 2674] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Protective coatings Paints intended to protect against corrosion consist of pigment dispersed in a liquid referred to as the 'vehicle'.
[줄 2675] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - When spread out thinly the vehicle changes in time to an adherent dry film.
[줄 2676] [91.7%] (11/12) ✅ 유지 - The drying may take place through one of the following processes: 1.
[줄 2677] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - When the vehicle consists of solid resinous material dissolved in a volatile solvent, the latter evaporates after application of the paint, leaving a dry film.
[줄 2678] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - A liquid like linseed oil as a constituent of the vehicle may produce a dry paint film by reacting chemically with the surrounding air.
[줄 2679] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - A chemical reaction may occur between the constituents of the vehicle after application, to produce a dry paint film.
[줄 2680] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - The reactive ingredients may be separated in two containers and mixed before application.
[줄 2681] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Alternatively, ingredients that only react at higher temperatures may be selected, or the reactants may be diluted with a solvent so that the reaction occurs only slowly in the can.
[줄 2682] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - Corrosion-inhibiting paints for application to steel have the following vehicle types: 1 Bitumen or pitch.
[줄 2683] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Simple solutions of bitumen or pitch are available in solvent naphtha or white spirit.
[줄 2684] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - The bitumen or pitch may also be blended by heat with other materials to form a vehicle.
[줄 2685] [92.9%] (13/14) ✅ 유지 - These consist mainly of vegetable drying oils, such as linseed oil and tung oil.
[줄 2686] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - To accelerate the drying by the natural reaction with oxygen, driers are added.
