[줄 2721] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - The vehicle incorporates natural or artificial resins into drying oils.
[줄 2722] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Some of these resins may react with the oil to give a faster-drying vehicle.
[줄 2723] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Other resins do not react with the oil but heat is applied to dissolve the resin and cause the oil to body.
[줄 2724] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - These vehicles provide a further improvement in the drying time and filmforming properties of drying oils.
[줄 2725] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - The name alkyd arises from the ingredients, alcohols and acids.
[줄 2726] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Alkyds need not be made from oil, as an oil-fatty acid or an oil-free acid may be used.
[줄 2727] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Vehicles of this type show extremely good resistance to severe conditions of exposure.
[줄 2728] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - As any number of important vehicle types come under this general heading, these are dealt with individually.
[줄 2729] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Chemicals that may be produced from petroleum and natural gas are the source of epoxy resins.
[줄 2730] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - These paints have very good adhesion, apart from their excellent chemical resistance.
[줄 2731] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - They may also have good flexibility and toughness where co-reacting resins are introduced.
[줄 2732] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - Epoxy resins are expensive owing to the removal of unwanted side products during their manufacture, and the gloss finish may tend to 'chalk', making it unsuitable for many external decorative finishes.
[줄 2733] [97.1%] (34/35) ✅ 유지 - These paints often consist of a 'two-pack' formulation, a solution of epoxy resin together with a solution of cold curing agent, such as an amine or a polyamide resin, being mixed prior to application.
[줄 2734] [93.5%] (29/31) ✅ 유지 - The mixed paint has a relatively slow curing rate at temperatures below 10  C Epoxy resin paints should not be confused with epoxy-ester paints, which are unsuitable for underwater use.
[줄 2735] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Epoxy-ester paints can be considered as alkyd equivalents, as they are usually made with epoxy resins and oil-fatty acids.
[줄 2736] [100.0%] (4/4) ✅ 유지 - Coal tar/epoxy resin.
[줄 2737] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - This vehicle type is similar to the epoxy resin vehicle except that, as a two-pack product, a grade of coal tar pitch is blended with the resin.
[줄 2738] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - A formulation of this type combines to some extent the chemical resistance of the epoxy resin with the impermeability of coal tar.
[줄 2739] [80.0%] (4/5) ✅ 유지 - Chlorinated rubber and isomerized rubber.
[줄 2740] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - The vehicle in this case consists of a solution of plasticized chlorinated rubber, or isomerized rubber.
[줄 2741] [95.0%] (19/20) ✅ 유지 - Isomerized rubber is produced chemically from natural rubber, and it has the same chemical composition but a different molecular structure.
[줄 2742] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Both these derivatives of natural rubber have a wide range of solubility in organic solvents, and so allow a vehicle of higher solid content.
[줄 2743] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - On drying, the film thickness is greater than would be obtained if natural rubber were used.
[줄 2744] [96.2%] (25/26) ✅ 유지 - High build coatings of this type are available, thickening or thixotropic agents being added to produce a paint that can be applied in much thicker coats.
[줄 2745] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - Coats of this type are particularly resistant to attack from acids and alkalis.
[줄 2746] [93.3%] (28/30) ✅ 유지 - A reaction between isocyanates and hydroxyl-containing compounds produces 'urethane' and this reaction has been adapted to produce polymeric compounds from which paint film, fibers, and adhesives may be obtained.
[줄 2747] [96.6%] (28/29) ✅ 유지 - Paint films so produced have received considerable attention in recent years, and since there is a variety of isocyanate reactions, both one- and two-pack polyurethane paints are available.
[줄 2748] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - These paints have many good properties: toughness, hardness, gloss, abrasion resistance, as well as chemical and weather resistance.
[줄 2749] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - Polyurethanes are not used underwater on steel ships, only on superstructures etc. but they are very popular on yachts, where their good gloss is appreciated.
[줄 2750] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Vinyl resins are obtained by the polymerization of organic compounds containing the vinyl group.
[줄 2751] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - The solids content of these paints is low; therefore, the dry film is thin and more coats are required than for most paints.
[줄 2752] [94.4%] (17/18) ✅ 유지 - As vinyl resin paints have poor adhesion to bare steel surfaces they are generally applied over a pretreatment
[줄 2753] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Vinyl paint systems are among the most effective for the underwater protection of steel.
[줄 2754] [96.6%] (28/29) ✅ 유지 - Paints containing metallic zinc as a pigment in sufficient quantity to ensure electrical conductivity through the dry paint film to the steel are capable of protecting the steel cathodically.
[줄 2755] [95.8%] (23/24) ✅ 유지 - The pigment content of the dry paint film should be greater than 90%, the vehicle being an epoxy resin, chlorinated rubber, or similar medium.
[줄 2756] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Corrosion protection by means of paints It is often assumed that all paint coatings prevent attack on the metal covered simply by excluding the corrosive agency, whether air or water.
[줄 2757] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - This is often the main and sometimes only form of protection; however, there are many paints that afford protection even though they present a porous surface or contain various discontinuities.
[줄 2758] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - For example, certain pigments in paints confer protection on steel even where it is exposed at a discontinuity.
[줄 2759] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - If the reactions at the anode and cathode of the corrosion cell that form positive and negative ions respectively are inhibited, protection is afforded.
[줄 2760] [88.0%] (22/25) ✅ 유지 - Good examples of pigments of this type are red lead and zinc chromate, red lead being an anodic inhibitor and zinc chromate a cathodic inhibitor.
[줄 2761] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - A second mode of protection occurs at gaps where the paint is richly pigmented with a metal anodic to the basis metal.
[줄 2762] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Zinc dust is a commercially available pigment that fulfills this requirement for coating steel in a salt water environment.
[줄 2763] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - The zinc dust is the sacrificial anode with respect to the steel.
[줄 2764] [97.6%] (40/41) ✅ 유지 - Antifouling systems The immersed hull and fittings of a ship at sea, particularly in coastal waters, are subject to algae, barnacle, mussel, and other shellfish growth that can impair its hydrodynamic performance and adversely affect the service of the immersed fittings.
[줄 2765] [92.9%] (26/28) ✅ 유지 - Fittings such as cooling water intake systems are often protected by impressed current antifouling systems, and immersed hulls today are finished with very effective self-polishing antifouling paints.
[줄 2766] [96.4%] (27/28) ✅ 유지 - Impressed current antifouling systems The functional principle of these systems is the establishment of an artificially triggered voltage difference between copper anodes and the integrated steel plate cathodes.
[줄 2767] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - This causes a minor electrical current to flow from the copper anodes, so that they are dissolved to a certain degree.
[줄 2768] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - A control unit makes sure that the anodes add the required minimum amount of copper particles to the sea water, thus ensuring the formation of copper oxide that creates ambient conditions precluding local fouling.
[줄 2769] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - A control unit can be connected to the management system of the vessel.
[줄 2770] [96.9%] (31/32) ✅ 유지 - Using information from the management system, the impressed current antifouling system can determine the amount of copper that needs to be dissolved to give optimum performance with minimum wastage of the anodes.
[줄 2771] [92.0%] (23/25) ✅ 유지 - Antifouling paints Antifouling paints consist of a vehicle with pigments that give body and color together with materials toxic to marine vegetable and animal growth.
[줄 2772] [90.9%] (10/11) ✅ 유지 - Copper is the best known toxin used in traditional antifouling paints.
[줄 2773] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - To prolong the useful life of the paint the toxic compounds must dissolve slowly in sea water.
[줄 2774] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - Once the release rate falls below a level necessary to prevent settlement of marine organisms, the antifouling composition is no longer effective.
[줄 2775] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - On merchant ships the effective period for traditional compositions was about 12 months.
[줄 2776] [90.6%] (29/32) ✅ 유지 - Demands in particular from large tanker owners wishing to reduce very high docking costs led to specially developed antifouling compositions with an effective life up to 24 months in the early 1970s.
[줄 2777] [96.9%] (31/32) ✅ 유지 - Subsequent developments of constant emission organic toxin antifoulings having a leaching rate independent of exposure time saw the paint technologists by chance discover coatings that also tended to become smoother in service.
[줄 2778] [96.8%] (30/31) ✅ 유지 - These so-called self-polishing antifoulings, with a lifetime that is proportional to applied thickness and therefore theoretically unlimited, smooth rather than roughen with time and result in reduced friction drag.
[줄 2779] [90.2%] (46/51) ✅ 유지 - Though more expensive than their traditional counterparts, given the claim that each 10-micron increase in hull roughness can result in a 1% increase in fuel consumption, their selfpolishing characteristic as well as their longer effective life, up to 5 years' protection between dry dockings, made them attractive to the shipowner.
[줄 2780] [85.2%] (23/27) ✅ 유지 - The benefits of the first widely used self-polishing copolymer antifouling paints could be traced to the properties of their prime ingredients, the tributyltin compounds or TBTs.
[줄 2781] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - TBTs were extremely active against a wide range of fouling organisms and they were able to be chemically bonded to the acrylic backbone of the paint system.
[줄 2782] [94.4%] (34/36) ✅ 유지 - When immersed in sea water a specific chemical reaction took place that cleaved the TBT from the paint backbone, resulting in both controlled release of the TBT and controlled disappearance or polishing of the paint film.
[줄 2783] [95.8%] (23/24) ✅ 유지 - Unfortunately, it was found that the small concentrations of TBTs released, particularly in enclosed coastal waters, had a harmful effect on certain marine organisms.
[줄 2784] [89.2%] (33/37) ✅ 유지 - This led to the banning of TBT antifouling paints for pleasure boats and smaller commercial ships in many developed countries and the introduction of regulations limiting the release rate of TBT for antifouling paints on larger ships.
[줄 2785] [76.9%] (30/39) ✅ 유지 - The International Convention on the Control of Harmful Antifouling on Ships, 2001 subsequently required that: 1 Ships shall not apply or reapply organotin compounds that act as biocides in antifouling systems on or after 1 January 2003; and 2.
[줄 2786] [76.9%] (10/13) ✅ 유지 - No ship shall have organotin compounds that act as biocides in antifouling systems.
[줄 2787] [80.0%] (8/10) ✅ 유지 - The final phase-out of TBT paints was in 2008.
[줄 2788] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - In theory, ships could retain the paint if it was sealed under another coating but in practice TBTs are no longer at sea.
[줄 2789] [97.0%] (32/33) ✅ 유지 - Note: Organotin means an organic compound with one or more tin atoms in its molecules used as a pesticide, hitherto considered to decompose safely, now found to be toxic in the food chain.
[줄 2790] [90.0%] (9/10) ✅ 유지 - A biocide is a chemical capable of killing living organisms.
[줄 2791] [92.5%] (37/40) ✅ 유지 - Antifouling paints subsequently applied have generally focused on either the use of copper-based self-polishing antifouling products, which operate in a similar manner to the banned TBT products, or the use of the so-called low-surface-energy coatings.
[줄 2792] [96.6%] (28/29) ✅ 유지 - The latter coatings do not polish or contain booster biocides, instead they offer a very smooth, low-surface-energy surface to which it is difficult for fouling to adhere.
[줄 2793] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - When the vessel is at rest some fouling may occur but once it is underway and reaches a critical speed the fouling is released.
[줄 2794] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - Painting ships To obtain the optimum performance from paints it is important that the metal surfaces are properly prepared before application of paints and subsequently maintained as such throughout the fabrication and erection process.
[줄 2795] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Paints tailored for the service conditions of the structure to which they apply, and recommended as such by the manufacturer, only should be applied.
[줄 2796] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - It is common, especially for ships undergoing a regular dry-docking, for the coating process to be specified and managed by the coating supplier.
[줄 2797] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - Surface preparation Good surface preparation is essential to successful painting, the primary cause of many paint failures being the inadequacy of the initial material preparation.
[줄 2798] [92.9%] (13/14) ✅ 유지 - It is particularly important before painting new steel that any millscale should be removed.
[줄 2799] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - Millscale is a thin layer of iron oxides that forms on the steel surface during hot rolling of the plates and sections.
[줄 2800] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - Not only does the non-uniform millscale set up corrosion cells, as illustrated previously, but it may also come away from the surface removing any paint film applied over it.
[줄 2801] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Any corrosion from storage of the steel outdoors in a stockyard must also be removed.
[줄 2802] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - It is also important to create a good surface for coating.
[줄 2803] [83.3%] (15/18) ✅ 유지 - Swedish standards are often quoted, SA 3 being white metal and SA 2.5 being near white metal.
[줄 2804] [75.0%] (9/12) ✅ 유지 - SA 2.5 is common as a reasonably achieveable standard for shipyards.
[줄 2805] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - The surface is clean and the blasting process also provides a 'key' with very small indentations to which the coating adheres well.
[줄 2806] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - The most common methods employed to prepare steel surfaces for painting are: Blast cleaning Pickling Flame cleaning Preparation by hand High-pressure water blasting.
[줄 2807] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Blast cleaning is the most efficient method for preparing the surface and is in common use in all large shipyards.
[줄 2808] [90.0%] (9/10) ✅ 유지 - The shipyard preparation process has been outlined in Chapter 13.
[줄 2809] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - Smaller shipyards, where the quantity of steel processed does not justify the capital investment in the preparation equipment, usually buy steel already prepared from a steel mill or stockist.
[줄 2810] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Following the blast cleaning it is desirable to brush the surface and apply a coat of priming paint as soon as possible, since the metal is liable to rust rapidly.
[줄 2811] [100.0%] (39/39) ✅ 유지 - There are two main types of blasting equipment available, an impeller wheel plant where the abrasive is thrown at high velocity against the metal surface, and a nozzle type where a jet of abrasive impinges on the metal surface.
[줄 2812] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - The latter type should preferably be fitted with vacuum recovery equipment, rather than allow the spent abrasive and dust to be discharged to atmosphere, as is often the case in ship repair work.
[줄 2813] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Impeller wheel plants that are self-contained and collect the dust and recirculate the clean abrasive are generally fitted within the shipbuilding shops.
[줄 2814] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Steel shot is the preferred blast medium for preparation of steel plates and profiles for new construction.
[줄 2815] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - As the process proceeds the shot is recovered and reused.
[줄 2816] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - The shot breaks down during the blasting and a mix of new and broken shot provides good surface preparation.
[줄 2817] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Dust and other debris is filtered out of the recovery system for disposal.
[줄 2818] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Cast iron and steel grit may be used for the abrasive, also copper slag, but nonmetallic abrasives are also available.
[줄 2819] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Grit has been used in ship repair but is becoming much less popular because of environmental issues associated with disposal of the waste material.
[줄 2820] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - The use of sand is prohibited in most countries because the fine dust produced may cause silicosis.
[줄 2821] [92.6%] (25/27) ✅ 유지 - Pickling involves the immersion of the metal in an acid solution, usually hydrochloric or sulfuric acid, in order to remove the millscale and rust from the surface.
[줄 2822] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - After immersion in these acids the metal will require a thorough hot water rinse.
[줄 2823] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - It is preferable that the treatment is followed by application of a priming coat.
[줄 2824] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Pickling is no longer found in most of the ship construction industry.
[줄 2825] [93.3%] (14/15) ✅ 유지 - Using an oxyacetylene flame the millscale and rust may be removed from a steel surface.
[줄 2826] [96.6%] (28/29) ✅ 유지 - The process does not entirely remove the millscale and rust, but it can be quite useful for cleaning plates under inclement weather conditions, the flame drying out the plate.
[줄 2827] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - Flame, or another heating process, is used as part of an automated preparation line in a shipyard, to preheat the steel, which assists the cleaning and drying of the primer paint coating.
[줄 2828] [94.3%] (33/35) ✅ 유지 - Hand cleaning by various forms of wire brush is often not very satisfactory, and would only be used where the millscale has been loosened by weathering, i.e exposure to atmosphere over a long period.
[줄 2829] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - For ships in service hand cleaning may be used for very small corroded areas.
[줄 2830] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - High-pressure water blasting is superseding grit blasting for ship repair.
[줄 2831] [90.5%] (19/21) ✅ 유지 - It is capable of restoring a steel surface to SA 2.5, provided any corrosion has not been allowed to develop.
[줄 2832] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Disposal of the waste material, in this case mainly water, is a main reason for the adoption of water blasting.
[줄 2833] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Blast cleaning using shot or grit is preferred for best results and economy in shipbuilding, it is essential prior to application of high-performance paint systems used today.
[줄 2834] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Pickling, which also gives good results, can be expensive and less applicable to production schemes; flame cleaning is much less effective; and hand cleaning gives the worst results.
[줄 2835] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - Water blasting is mainly a ship repair process.
[줄 2836] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - Temporary paint protection during building After the steel is blast cleaned it may be several months before it is built into the ship and finally painted.
[줄 2837] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - It is desirable to protect the material against rusting in this period as the final paint will offer the best protection when applied over perfectly clean steel.
[줄 2838] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - The formulation of a prefabrication primer for immediate application after blasting must meet a number of requirements.
[줄 2839] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - It should dry rapidly to permit handling of the plates within a few minutes and working the plates within a day or so.
[줄 2840] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - It should be nontoxic, and it should not produce harmful porosity in welds nor give off obnoxious fumes during welding or cutting.
[줄 2841] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - For some high-speed welding processes it is necessary to remove the primer in way of the welds to avoid porosity.
[줄 2842] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - After cutting and welding, areas of damaged primer are usually strip coated by hand to cover the affected steel and retain the primer protection against corrosion.
[줄 2843] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - The primer must also be compatible with any subsequent paint finishes to be applied.
[줄 2844] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Satisfactory formulations are available, for example a primer consisting of zinc dust in an epoxy resin.
[줄 2845] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Some shipyards where work is entirely undercover and where the steel is used quickly may dispense with primer.
[줄 2846] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Given the sophistication and cost of modern, long-life coatings, their application is critical to performance.
[줄 2847] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - It is common for shipyards to take complete units and blocks, once all the hot work is completed, for final coating in a controlled environment.
[줄 2848] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - So-called 'paint cells' are temperature- and humidity-controlled buildings.
[줄 2849] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - The units are driven into the cells using self-elevating transporters.
[줄 2850] [95.0%] (19/20) ✅ 유지 - The units are then blasted, if no primer has been used or the primer is degraded and unsuitable for overcoating.
[줄 2851] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - Once cleaned the coatings can be applied in near ideal conditions.

[줄 2854] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - These are completed after the hull welding, using localized protection from unsuitable weather conditions.
[줄 2855] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - Paint systems on ships The paint system applied to any part of a ship will be dictated by the environment to which that part of the structure is exposed.
[줄 2856] [96.2%] (25/26) ✅ 유지 - Traditionally, the painting of the external ship structure was divided into three regions: 1 Below the waterline, where the plates are continually immersed in sea water.
[줄 2857] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - The waterline or boot topping region, where immersion is intermittent and a lot of abrasion occurs.
[줄 2858] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - The topsides and superstructure exposed to an atmosphere laden with salt spray, and subject to damage through cargo handling.
[줄 2859] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - However, now that tougher paints are used for the ship's bottom the distinction between regions need not be so well defined, one scheme covering the bottom and waterline regions.
[줄 2860] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Internally, by far the greatest problem is the provision of coatings for various liquid cargo and salt water ballast tanks.
[줄 2861] [90.9%] (20/22) ✅ 유지 - Below the waterline The ship's bottom has priming coats of corrosion-inhibiting paint applied that are followed by an antifouling paint.
[줄 2862] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Paints used for steels immersed in sea water are required to resist alkaline conditions.
[줄 2863] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - The reason for this is that an iron alloy immersed in a sodium chloride solution having the necessary supply of dissolved oxygen gives rise to corrosion cells with caustic soda produced at the cathodes.
[줄 2864] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Further, the paint should have a good electrical resistance so that the flow of corrosion currents between the steel and sea water is limited.
[줄 2865] [95.2%] (20/21) ✅ 유지 - These requirements make the standard nonmarine structural steel primer red lead in linseed oil unsuitable for ship use below the waterline.
[줄 2866] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Suitable corrosion-inhibiting paints for ships' bottoms are pitch or bitumen types, chlorinated rubber, coal tar/epoxy resin, or vinyl resin paints.
[줄 2867] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - The antifouling paints may be applied after the corrosion-inhibiting coatings and should not come into direct contact with the steel hull, since the toxic compounds present may cause corrosion.
[줄 2868] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Waterline or boot topping region Generally, modern practice requires a complete paint system for the hull above the waterline.
[줄 2869] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - This may be based on vinyl and alkyd resins or on polyurethane resin paints.
[줄 2870] [90.9%] (10/11) ✅ 유지 - Superstructures Red lead- or zinc chromate-based primers are commonly used.
[줄 2871] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - White finishing paints are then used extensively for superstructures.
[줄 2872] [96.4%] (27/28) ✅ 유지 - These are usually oleo-resinous or alkyd paints that may be based on 'nonyellowing' oils, linseed oil-based paints that yellow on exposure being avoided on modern ships.
[줄 2873] [96.0%] (24/25) ✅ 유지 - Where aluminum alloy superstructures are fitted, under no circumstance should lead-based paints be applied; zinc chromate paints are generally supplied for application to aluminum.
[줄 2874] [97.1%] (34/35) ✅ 유지 - Cargo and ballast tanks Severe corrosion may occur in a ship's cargo tanks as the combined result of carrying liquid cargoes and sea water ballast, with warm or cold sea water cleaning between voyages.

[줄 2876] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Tankers carrying 'white oil' cargoes suffer more general corrosion than those carrying crude oils, which deposit a film on the tank surface, providing some protection against corrosion.

[줄 2992] [100.0%] (46/46) ✅ 유지 - It is not intended that the IMO would take over the detailed rule making of the classification societies, but the IMO would state what goals have to be achieved, leaving the classification societies, designers, and builders to determine how the required goals can be best met.

[줄 2994] [96.9%] (31/32) ✅ 유지 - The conventions and amendments are ratified by the member country when they are incorporated in that country's national legislation relating to ships registered in that country and which make international voyages.

[줄 3020] [93.9%] (31/33) ✅ 유지 - International Convention on Tonnage Measurement of Ships 1969 An International Conference on Tonnage Measurement was convened by the IMO in 1969 with the intention of producing a universally acceptable system of tonnage measurement.
[줄 3021] [87.5%] (21/24) ✅ 유지 - The International Convention on Tonnage Measurement of Ships 1969 was prepared at this conference and this convention came into force on 8 July 1982.
[줄 3022] [81.2%] (13/16) ✅ 유지 - All ships constructed on or after that datewere measured for tonnage in accordancewith the 1969 Convention.
[줄 3023] [81.0%] (34/42) ✅ 유지 - Ships builtprior to that datewere, if theownerso desired, permitted to retain their existing tonnages for a period of 12 years from that date, i.e all ships were required to be measured in accordance with the 1969 Convention by 18 July 1994.

[줄 3027] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - Net tonnage The net tonnage is determined by the following formulae:
[줄 3028] [28.6%] (10/35) ❌ 제거 - For passenger ships i.e ships carrying 13 passengers or more NT 1⁄4 K 2 V c 1⁄4  4 d 3 D  2 þ K 3 N 1 þ N 2 10 2.

[줄 3032] [69.0%] (20/29) ✅ 유지 - The term K 2 V c 2 is not to be taken as less than 0.25GT, and NT is not to be taken as less than 0.30GT.
[줄 3033] [90.5%] (19/21) ✅ 유지 - It will be noted that vessels with high freeboards, i.e low draft to depth ratios will have low net tonnages.
[줄 3034] [88.2%] (15/17) ✅ 유지 - Squaring this ratio can result in excessively low net tonnages, hence the limiting value of 0.30GT.

[줄 3049] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - Most maritime authorities have authorized various classification societies and perhaps other bodies to act on their behalf to measure ships and issue the International Tonnage Certificate.
[줄 3050] [97.6%] (41/42) ✅ 유지 - The volumes to be included in the calculation of gross and net tonnages are measured irrespective of the fitting of insulation or other linings to the inner side shell or structural boundary plating in metal, i.e the molded dimensions are used.
[줄 3051] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - It is possible for the surveyor to compute tonnages directly form the molded lines of the ship or computer-stored offsets.
[줄 3052] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - This is in contrast to the previous regulations, where the surveyor was required to physically measure spaces to the inside of frames and linings.
[줄 3053] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - Panama and Suez Canal tonnages Tolls for transiting the Suez Canal are based on a net tonnage of the ship determined in accordance with the regulations of the Suez Canal authority.
[줄 3054] [96.6%] (28/29) ✅ 유지 - Whilst the IMO recommended acceptance of the use of the Convention rule for the Suez and Panama Canals in 1981, the Suez Canal Authority has maintained its own system.
[줄 3055] [88.9%] (16/18) ✅ 유지 - The Panama Canal Authority introduced a net tonnage measurement system based on the 1969 Tonnage Convention in 1994.
[줄 3056] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - It has, however, subsequently changed its charging regime from a flat rate for all ships to one based on ship size and type, and has separate locomotive usage rates.
[줄 3057] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - This is considered a more equitable system, since charges are now applied according to the transit needs of each ship.
[줄 3058] [96.0%] (24/25) ✅ 유지 - Further, since 2005 a new measurement and pricing system is being phased in for container ships and other vessels with on-deck container-carrying capacity.
[줄 3059] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - For container vessels the Authority have adopted the TEU as the measurement unit.
[줄 3060] [92.1%] (35/38) ✅ 유지 - For other vessels with ondeck container-carrying capacity the Authority will continue to apply the universal tonnage requirement to the underdeck spaces and will charge a per-TEU fee for the actual number of containers carried on deck.
[줄 3061] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - Both the Suez and Panama Canal Authorities have recognized a number of classification societies to undertake measurement and issue of tonnage certificates on their behalf.
[줄 3062] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Compensated gross tonnage For many years the gross tonnage was used as a measure for comparing the output of various shipbuilding countries.
[줄 3063] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - Gross tonnage was never intended to be used for statistical purposes and, although it may have served this purpose, it can give very misleading impressions.
[줄 3064] [87.1%] (27/31) ✅ 유지 - For example, the building of a 65,000 gross tonnage passenger liner may involve considerably more man-hours and capital than the construction of a 150,000 gross tonnage oil tanker.
[줄 3065] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - A system of compensated gross tonnage was introduced and adopted as a means of overcoming this problem.
[줄 3066] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - Factors were developed for each ship type and the gross tonnage of the vessel then multiplied by the appropriate factor to give the compensated gross tonnage.
[줄 3067] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - Compensated gross tonnage factors were developed by the
[줄 3068] [88.9%] (16/18) ✅ 유지 - OECD in cooperation with the Association of West European Shipbuilders and the Shipbuilders Association of Japan in 1968.
[줄 3069] [77.8%] (7/9) ✅ 유지 - In 2007 a revised system for CGT was developed.
[줄 3070] [89.6%] (43/48) ✅ 유지 - This replaced fixed factors for ship type and size by a formula, CGT 1⁄4 A  GT B, where A is a factor to account for the type of ship, B is a factor to account for ship size, and GT is the gross tonnage of the vessel.

[줄 3072] [84.6%] (11/13) ✅ 유지 - Further reading International Conference on Tonnage Measurement of Ships, 1969, IMO publication, 1969.

[줄 3075] [89.5%] (17/19) ✅ 유지 - Freeboard computation Basic freeboards are given in the rules that are dependent on the length and type of vessel.
[줄 3076] [87.5%] (7/8) ✅ 유지 - Ships are divided into types 'A' and 'B'.
[줄 3077] [97.2%] (35/36) ✅ 유지 - Type 'A' ships are those that are designed to carry only liquid cargoes in bulk, and in which the cargo tanks have only small access openings closed by watertight gasketed covers of steel or equivalent material.
[줄 3078] [87.5%] (7/8) ✅ 유지 - These vessels benefit from the minimum assignable freeboard.
[줄 3079] [94.7%] (18/19) ✅ 유지 - All ships that do not come within the provisions regarding Type 'A' ships are considered as Type 'B' ships.
[줄 3080] [87.1%] (27/31) ✅ 유지 - As a considerable variety of ships will come within the Type 'B' category, a reduction or increase from the basic table Type 'B' freeboard is made in the following cases: 1.
[줄 3081] [86.8%] (33/38) ✅ 유지 - Vessels having hatchways fitted with portable beams and covers on exposed freeboard or raised quarter decks, and within 25% of the ship's length from the FP on exposed superstructure decks, are to have the basic freeboard increased.
[줄 3082] [92.5%] (37/40) ✅ 유지 - Vessels having steel weathertight covers fitted with gaskets and clamping devices, improved measures for the protection of the crew, better freeing arrangements, and satisfactory subdivision characteristics may obtain a reduction in the basic freeboard given for a Type 'B' ship.
[줄 3083] [90.5%] (19/21) ✅ 유지 - This reduction may be increased up to the total difference between the values for Type 'A' and Type 'B' basic freeboards.
[줄 3084] [86.8%] (33/38) ✅ 유지 - The Type 'B' ship, which is effectively adopting a Type 'A' basic freeboard, is referred to as a Type 'B-100' and its final calculated freeboard will be almost the same as that for a Type 'A' ship.
[줄 3085] [87.5%] (28/32) ✅ 유지 - Other Type 'B' vessels that comply with not such severe subdivision requirements can be assigned a basic freeboard reduced by up to 60% of the difference between 'B' and 'A' basic values.

[줄 3088] [88.2%] (30/34) ✅ 유지 - This is particularly the case with bulk carriers, since these vessels can often be designed to obtain the 'B-60' freeboards, and where this is impossible some reduction in freeboard may still be possible.

[줄 3094] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - After flooding the final waterline is to be below the lower edge of any opening through which progressive flooding may take place.

[줄 3109] [66.7%] (26/39) ✅ 유지 - Where the effective length of superstructure is 1.0 L, the freeboard may be reduced by 350 mm at 24 m length of ship, 860 mm at 85 m length, and 1070 mm at 122 m length and above.

[줄 3111] [87.0%] (20/23) ✅ 유지 - Where the total effective length of superstructures and trunks is less than 1.0 L the deduction is a percentage of the above.
[줄 3112] [95.8%] (23/24) ✅ 유지 - These percentages are given in tabular form in the rules, and the associated notes give corrections for size of forecastles with Type 'B' ships.
[줄 3113] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - The area under the actual sheer curve is compared with the area under a standard parabolic sheer curve, the aft ordinate of which is given by 25
[줄 3114] [80.0%] (8/10) ✅ 유지 - mm and the forward ordinate by 2 S A mm.
[줄 3115] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - Where a poop or forecastle is of greater than standard height, an addition to the sheer of the freeboard deck may be made.
[줄 3116] [96.8%] (30/31) ✅ 유지 - The correction for deficiency or excess of sheer is the difference between the actual sheer and the standard sheer multiplied by, where S is the total mean enclosed length of superstructure.
[줄 3117] [92.9%] (13/14) ✅ 유지 - Where the sheer is less than standard the correction is added to the freeboard.
[줄 3118] [77.4%] (24/31) ✅ 유지 - If the sheer is in excess of standard a deduction may be made from the freeboard if the superstructure covers 0.1 L abaft and 0.1 L forward of amidships.
[줄 3119] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - No deduction for excess sheer may be made if no superstructure covers amidships.
[줄 3120] [85.0%] (17/20) ✅ 유지 - Where superstructure covers less than 0.1 L abaft and forward of amidships the deduction is obtained by linear interpolation.
[줄 3121] [81.2%] (13/16) ✅ 유지 - The maximum deduction for excess sheer is limited to 125 mm per 100 m of length.
[줄 3122] [92.0%] (23/25) ✅ 유지 - If the above corrections are made to the basic freeboard, the final calculated freeboard will correspond to the maximum geometric summer draft for the vessel.
[줄 3123] [93.8%] (30/32) ✅ 유지 - The final freeboard may, however, be increased if the bow height is insufficient, or the owners request the assignment of freeboards corresponding to a draft that is less than the maximum possible.
[줄 3124] [96.8%] (30/31) ✅ 유지 - Bow height is defined as the vertical distance at the forward perpendicular between the waterline corresponding to the assigned summer freeboard and the top of the exposed deck at the side.
[줄 3125] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - This height should not be less than the values quoted in the Convention.
[줄 3126] [85.7%] (18/21) ✅ 유지 - The minimum freeboard in the summer zone is the freeboard described above; however, it may not be less than 50 mm.
[줄 3127] [87.0%] (20/23) ✅ 유지 - In the tropical and winter zones the minimum freeboard is obtained by deducting and adding respectively 1/48th of the summer molded draft.
[줄 3128] [84.6%] (11/13) ✅ 유지 - The tropical freeboard is, however, also limited to a minimum of 50 mm.
[줄 3129] [80.0%] (20/25) ✅ 유지 - The freeboard for a ship of not more than 100 m length in the winter North Atlantic zone is the winter freeboard plus 50 mm.
[줄 3130] [83.3%] (10/12) ✅ 유지 - For other ships, the winter North Atlantic freeboard is the winter freeboard.
[줄 3131] [87.5%] (35/40) ✅ 유지 - The minimum freeboard in fresh water is obtained by deducting from the summer or tropical freeboard the quantity: Displacement in SW 4  TPC mm where TPC is the tonnes per cm immersion at the waterline, and displacement is in tonnes.
[줄 3132] [96.8%] (30/31) ✅ 유지 - Timber freeboards If a vessel is carrying timber on the exposed decks it is considered that the deck cargo affords additional buoyancy and a greater degree of protection against the sea.
[줄 3133] [93.3%] (28/30) ✅ 유지 - Ships thus arranged are granted a smaller freeboard than would be assigned to a Type 'B' vessel, provided they comply with the additional conditions of assignment for timber-carrying vessels.
[줄 3134] [84.2%] (16/19) ✅ 유지 - No reduction of freeboard may be made in ships that already have Type 'A' or reduced Type 'B' freeboards.
[줄 3135] [93.3%] (28/30) ✅ 유지 - The freeboards are computed as described above, but have a different superstructure correction, this being modified by the use of different percentage deductions given in the rules for timber freeboards.
[줄 3136] [80.0%] (16/20) ✅ 유지 - Winter timber freeboard is obtained by adding to the summer timber freeboard 1/36th of the molded summer timber draft.
[줄 3137] [82.4%] (28/34) ✅ 유지 - Winter North Atlantic timber freeboard is the same as for normal freeboards, and the tropical timber freeboard is obtained by deducting from the summer timber freeboard 1/48th of the molded summer timber draft.
[줄 3138] [81.8%] (9/11) ✅ 유지 - The fresh water timber freeboard is determined as for normal freeboards.

[줄 3154] [91.3%] (21/23) ✅ 유지 - The product of the maximum stress thus calculated and the factor 4.25 should not exceed the minimum ultimate strength of the material.
[줄 3155] [84.6%] (11/13) ✅ 유지 - The deflection is limited to 0.0028 times the span under these loads.

[줄 3207] [71.2%] (57/80) ✅ 유지 - The minimum freeing port area on each side of the ship where sheer in way of the well is standard or greater than standard, is given, in square meters, by A 1⁄4 0.7 þ 0.035 l where l is the length of bulwark in the well and is less than 20 m, and A 1⁄4 0.07 l where l is greater than 20 m In no case need l be greater than 0.7 L.

[줄 3231] [97.2%] (35/36) ✅ 유지 - Ships built in accordance with Lloyd's Register rules or equivalent standards are assigned a class in the Register Book, and continue to be classed so long as they are maintained in accordance with the rules.
[줄 3232] [81.0%] (17/21) ✅ 유지 - Lloyd ' s register classi fi cation symbols All ships classed by Lloyd's Register are assigned one or more character symbols.
[줄 3233] [81.8%] (9/11) ✅ 유지 - The majority of ships are assigned the characters 100A1 or 100A1.
[줄 3234] [93.3%] (14/15) ✅ 유지 - The character figure 100 is assigned to all ships considered suitable for sea-going service.
[줄 3235] [96.4%] (27/28) ✅ 유지 - The character letter A is assigned to all ships that are built in accordance with or accepted into class as complying with the society's rules and regulations.
[줄 3236] [91.7%] (22/24) ✅ 유지 - The character figure 1 is assigned to ships carrying on board anchor and/or mooring equipment complying with the society's rules and regulations.

[줄 3238] [94.1%] (32/34) ✅ 유지 - The Maltese cross mark is assigned to new ships constructed under the society's special survey, i.e a surveyor has been in attendance during the construction period to inspect the materials and workmanship.
[줄 3239] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - There may be appended to the character symbols, when considered necessary by the society or requested by the owner, a number of class notations.
[줄 3240] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - These class notations may consist of one or a combination of the following: type notation, cargo notation, special duties notation, special features notation, service restriction notation.
[줄 3241] [88.0%] (22/25) ✅ 유지 - Type notation indicates that the ship has been constructed in compliance with particular rules applying to that type of ship, e.g 100A1 'Bulk carrier'.
[줄 3242] [89.5%] (17/19) ✅ 유지 - Cargo notation indicates the ship has been designed to carry one or more specific cargoes, e.g 'Sulfuric acid'.
[줄 3243] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - This does not preclude it from carrying other cargoes for which it might be suitable.
[줄 3244] [92.0%] (23/25) ✅ 유지 - Special duties notation indicates that the ship has been designed for special duties other than those implied by type or cargo notation, e.g 'research'.
[줄 3245] [88.9%] (16/18) ✅ 유지 - Special features notation indicates the ship incorporates special features that significantly affect the design, e.g 'movable decks'.
[줄 3246] [93.8%] (30/32) ✅ 유지 - Service restriction notation indicates the ship has been classed on the understanding it is operated only in a specified area and/or under specified conditions, e.g 'Great Lakes and St Lawrence'.

[줄 3251] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Where additional strengthening is fitted for navigation in ice conditions an appropriate notation may be assigned.
[줄 3252] [83.8%] (62/74) ✅ 유지 - 32 Structural fi re protection Chapter Outline Requirements 371 ' A ', ' B ', and ' C ' class divisions 372 Openings in fi re protection divisions 373 Protection of special category spaces 375 Fire protection arrangements in high-speed craft 375 Further reading 375 Some useful websites 376 Of the requirements of the International Conventions for the Safety of Life at Sea, those having a particular influence on ship construction are the requirements relating to structural fire protection.
[줄 3253] [93.3%] (28/30) ✅ 유지 - Varying requirements for vessels engaged in international voyages are given for passenger ships carrying more than 36 passengers, passenger ships carrying not more than 36 passengers, cargo ships, and tankers.
[줄 3254] [97.7%] (42/43) ✅ 유지 - Requirements Ships carrying more than 36 passengers are required to have accommodation spaces and main divisional bulkheads and decks that are generally of incombustible material in association with either an automatic fire detection and alarm system or an automatic sprinkler and alarm system.
[줄 3255] [89.8%] (44/49) ✅ 유지 - The hull, superstructure, and deckhouses are subdivided by 'A' class divisions into main vertical zones, the length of which on any one deck should not exceed 40 m Main horizontal zones of 'A' class divisions are fitted to provide a barrier between sprinklered and nonsprinklered zones of the ship.
[줄 3256] [91.4%] (32/35) ✅ 유지 - Bulkheads within the main vertical zones are required to be 'A', 'B', or 'C' class divisions depending on the fire risk of the adjoining spaces and whether adjoining spaces are within sprinkler or nonsprinkler zones.
[줄 3257] [92.3%] (24/26) ✅ 유지 - Passenger vessels carrying not more than 36 passengers are required to have the hull, superstructure, and deckhouses subdivided into main vertical zones by 'A' class divisions.
[줄 3258] [95.7%] (45/47) ✅ 유지 - The accommodation and service spaces are to be protected either by all enclosure bulkheads within the space being of at least 'B' class divisions or only the corridor bulkheads being of at least 'B' class divisions, where an approved automatic fire detection and alarm system is installed.
[줄 3259] [100.0%] (3/3) ✅ 유지 - All rights reserved.
[줄 3260] [94.4%] (34/36) ✅ 유지 - Cargo ships exceeding 500 gross tonnage are generally to be constructed of steel or equivalent material and to be fitted with one of the following methods of fire protection in accommodation and service spaces: 'Method Ic'.
[줄 3261] [96.0%] (48/50) ✅ 유지 - All internal divisional bulkheads constructed of noncombustible 'B' or 'C' class divisions and no installation of an automatic sprinkler, fire detection, and alarm system in the accommodation and service spaces, except smoke detection and manually operated alarm points, which are to be installed in all corridors, stairways, and escape routes.
[줄 3262] [100.0%] (40/40) ✅ 유지 - An approved automatic sprinkler, fire detection, and fire alarm system is installed in all spaces in which a fire might be expected to originate, and in general there is no restriction on the type of divisions used for internal bulkheads.
[줄 3263] [96.8%] (60/62) ✅ 유지 - A fixed fire detection and fire alarm system is installed in all spaces in which a fire might be expected to originate, and in general there is no restriction on the type of divisions used for internal bulkheads except that in no case must the area of any accommodation space bounded by an 'A' or 'B' class division exceed 50 square meters.
[줄 3264] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Crowns of casings of main machinery spaces are to be of steel construction and insulated.
[줄 3265] [91.7%] (22/24) ✅ 유지 - Bulkheads and decks separating adjacent spaces are required to have appropriate A, B, or C ratings depending on the fire risk of adjoining spaces.
[줄 3266] [95.0%] (38/40) ✅ 유지 - Cargo spaces of ships of 2000 gross tonnage or more are to be protected by a fixed gas fireextinguishing system or its equivalent unless they carry bulk or other cargoes considered by the authorities to be a low fire risk.
[줄 3267] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Cargo ships carrying dangerous goods are subject to special fire protection precautions.
[줄 3268] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - In the construction of tankers, particular attention is paid to the exterior boundaries of superstructures and deckhouses that face the cargo oil tanks.
[줄 3269] [97.9%] (46/47) ✅ 유지 - Accommodation boundaries facing the cargo area are insulated to A60 standard, no doors are allowed in such boundaries giving access to the accommodation, and any windows are to be of non-opening type and fitted with steel covers if in the first tier on the main deck.
[줄 3270] [91.7%] (22/24) ✅ 유지 - Bulkheads and decks separating adjacent spaces of varying fire risk are required to have appropriate A, B, and C ratings within the accommodation space.
[줄 3271] [90.6%] (29/32) ✅ 유지 - For new tankers of 20,000 tons deadweight and upwards the cargo tanks' deck area and cargo tanks are protected by a fixed deck foam system and a fixed inert gas system.
[줄 3272] [90.5%] (19/21) ✅ 유지 - Tankers of less than 2000 tons deadweight are provided with a fixed deck foam system in way of the cargo tanks.
[줄 3273] [94.7%] (36/38) ✅ 유지 - ' A ', ' B ', and ' C ' class divisions 'A' class divisions are constructed of steel or equivalent material and should be capable of preventing the passage of smoke and flame to the end of a one-hour standard fire test.
[줄 3274] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - A plain stiffened steel bulkhead or deck has what is known as an A-O rating.
[줄 3275] [90.9%] (40/44) ✅ 유지 - By adding insulation in the form of approved incombustible materials to the steel an increased time is taken for the average temperature of the unexposed side to rise to 139  C above the original temperature or not more than 180  C at any one
[줄 3276] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - point above the original temperature during the standard fire test.
[줄 3277] [69.2%] (18/26) ✅ 유지 - The 'A' class division rating is related to this time as follows: Class Time A-60 60 A-30 30 A-15 15 A-0 0
[줄 3278] [81.2%] (13/16) ✅ 유지 - Figure 32.1 shows typical steel divisions with typical proprietary non-asbestos fiberreinforced silicate board insulation.
[줄 3279] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - 'B' class divisions are those that are constructed as to be capable of preventing the passage of flame to the end of half an hour of the standard fire test.
[줄 3280] [78.3%] (18/23) ✅ 유지 - Various patent board materials are commonly used where 'B' class divisions are required and there are two ratings B-0 and B-15.
[줄 3281] [87.6%] (78/89) ✅ 유지 - These relate to the insulation value such that the average temperature of the unexposed side does not rise more than 139  C above the original temperature and at any one point more than 225  C above the original temperature when the material is subjected to the standard fire test within the following times: Class Time B-15 15 B-0 0 'C class divisions are constructed of approved incombustible materials but do not need to meet any specified requirements relative to passage of smoke and flame nor temperature rise.
[줄 3282] [91.5%] (54/59) ✅ 유지 - The standard fire test referred to is a test in which a specimen of the division with a surface area of not less than 4.65 square meters and height or length of 2.44 m is exposed in a test furnace to a series of time–temperature relationships, defined by a smooth curve drawn through the following points:
[줄 3283] [62.5%] (5/8) ✅ 유지 - At end of first 5 minutes 538  C
[줄 3284] [62.5%] (5/8) ✅ 유지 - At end of first 10 minutes 704  C
[줄 3285] [62.5%] (5/8) ✅ 유지 - At end of first 30 minutes 843  C
[줄 3286] [79.3%] (23/29) ✅ 유지 - At end of first 60 minutes 927  C Some typical examples of fire divisions are given in Table 32.1 for a passenger ship carrying more than 36 passengers.
[줄 3287] [96.8%] (30/31) ✅ 유지 - Openings in fi re protection divisions Generally, openings in fire divisions are to be fitted with permanently attached means of closing that have the same fire-resisting rating as the division.
[줄 3288] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - arrangements are made to ensure that the fire resistance of a division is not impaired where it is pierced for the passage of pipes, vent trunks, electrical cables, etc.
[줄 3289] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Greatest care is necessary in the case of openings in the main fire zone divisions.
[줄 3290] [93.8%] (30/32) ✅ 유지 - Door openings in the main fire zone bulkheads and stairway enclosures are fitted with fire doors of equivalent fire integrity and are self-closing against an inclination of 3.5  opposing closure.
[줄 3291] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - Such doors are capable of closure from a control station either simultaneously or in groups, and also individually from a position adjacent to the door.

[줄 3298] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - This usually takes the form of a steel flap in the trunk, which is held open by a weighted hinge secured by an external fusible link.

[줄 3300] [100.0%] (42/42) ✅ 유지 - Protection of special category spaces A special category space is an enclosed space above or below the bulkhead deck used for the carriage of motor vehicles with fuel for their own propulsion in their own tanks and to which passengers have access.
[줄 3301] [78.9%] (15/19) ✅ 유지 - Obvious examples are the garage spaces in ro-ro passenger ferries and vehicle decks in ro-ro cargo ships.
[줄 3302] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Such spaces cannot have the normal main vertical fire zoning without interfering with the working of the ship.
[줄 3303] [100.0%] (37/37) ✅ 유지 - Equivalent protection is provided in such spaces by ensuring that the horizontal and vertical boundaries of the space are treated as main fire zone divisions and an efficient fixed fire-extinguishing system is fitted within the space.
[줄 3304] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - This takes the form of a fixed-pressure water-spraying system, generally in association with an automatic fire detection system.
[줄 3305] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - Special scupper arrangements are provided to clear the deck of the water deposited by the system in the event of a fire to avoid a drastic reduction in stability.
[줄 3306] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - Fire protection arrangements in high-speed craft The IMO High-Speed Craft Code recognizes the use of lightweight construction materials such as aluminum alloy and fiber-reinforced plastics that have a lesser fire rating than steel.
[줄 3307] [95.0%] (19/20) ✅ 유지 - Consequently, that Code has applied a new approach to fire insulation to that taken by SOLAS for conventional steel ships.
[줄 3308] [97.6%] (40/41) ✅ 유지 - The HSC Code has introduced the concept of a 'fire-restricting material', which may be a combustible material or combination of combustible materials provided it can comply with a prescribed fire test limiting heat release, smoke production, and spread of flame.
[줄 3309] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - Also introduced is the concept of a 'fire-resisting division' to prevent flame spread from one compartment to another within a prescribed time, which is related to a passenger evacuation time for the craft.
[줄 3310] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - A fire-resisting division can be constructed from noncombustible material, fire-resisting material, or a combination of both.
[줄 3311] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Further reading International Code of Safety for High Speed Craft .
[줄 3312] [75.0%] (3/4) ✅ 유지 - IMO publication, 2000 edition.
[줄 3313] [66.7%] (2/3) ✅ 유지 - SOLAS Consolidated Edition.

[줄 3317] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Part Five Ship Structure Introduction Ships are the largest, mobile man-made structures in the world.
[줄 3318] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - The largest ships are comparable with major buildings, but have additionally to withstand enormous forces from wind and waves.
[줄 3319] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - Their structural arrangements are therefore of great importance.
[줄 3320] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Because in most cases ships have to earn by carrying cargo, their structure not only has to be strong, it must also be as light as possible.
[줄 3321] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - The structure of a ship is based on flat and curved steel plate panels, with primary and secondary stiffening.
[줄 3322] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - The complete hull structure has to fulfill several important requirements.
[줄 3323] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - These include: Maintaining watertight integrity Separating internal spaces, for example cargo, fuel oil, ballast water Resisting forces on the ship, in particular from waves.
[줄 3324] [92.9%] (26/28) ✅ 유지 - The structure also has to conform to the hull shape dictated by hydrodynamics, i.e the performance in terms of speed and seakeeping specified by the hull designer.
[줄 3325] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Both the forces on the ship and the capability of the structure have some uncertainty, which must be allowed for in the design.
[줄 3326] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - The structure may suffer from changes in material properties over the life of the ship.
[줄 3327] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Some causes of structural failure are hard to predict, for example fatigue and corrosion.
[줄 3328] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - The quality of workmanship can also vary considerably.
[줄 3329] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Basic structural arrangements The structure of a ship is based primarily on panels, both flat and curved.
[줄 3330] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - These are the building blocks of the structure and also provide a convenient breakdown of the structure into units during ship construction.
[줄 3331] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - The basic components of the panels are steel plates and steel profiles.
[줄 3332] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - The plates form the panels and the profiles are used to provide stiffening to prevent the plates deforming when subjected to forces.
[줄 3333] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - There is a specific terminology for the structural components.
[줄 3334] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Plating forms the main structural elements of the ship, which are: Hull bottom plating, inner and outer bottom Hull side plating
[줄 3335] [100.0%] (7/7) ✅ 유지 - Hull deck plating Internal bulkheads Internal decks.
[줄 3336] [94.1%] (16/17) ✅ 유지 - Stiffening for the various panels includes: Longitudinals that run along the bottom plating and provide significant strength.
[줄 3337] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - There may be a keel in the form of a longitudinal center-line girder.
[줄 3338] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Deck girders, also longitudinal, which again contribute to the longitudinal strength of the ship.
[줄 3339] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Stringers, running longitudinally on the side plating, and where required along the inner side plating for a double-hull ship.
[줄 3340] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - Frames, which run vertically up the side plating.
[줄 3341] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Floors, which are deep transverse frames on the bottom plating.
[줄 3342] [100.0%] (7/7) ✅ 유지 - Deck beams, which support the deck transversely.
[줄 3343] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - Note Throughout this part of the book a number of requirements relating to the spacing and scantlings of various structural members are given.
[줄 3344] [95.1%] (39/41) ✅ 유지 - These are intended only as examples, which were taken from Lloyd's Register rules at the time of writing and were introduced only to give the student an idea of the variation in dimensions and scantlings found within the ship structure.
[줄 3345] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Other classification society requirements may differ, but basically the overall structure would have the same characteristics.
[줄 3346] [94.4%] (34/36) ✅ 유지 - It should be borne in mind that owner's additional requirements and the nature of a particular trade can result in ships having greater scantlings and additional strengthening to the minimum indicated in the following chapters.

[줄 3359] [93.5%] (43/46) ✅ 유지 - Classi fi cation of ships operating in ice Classification societies such as Lloyd's Register and a number of administrations whose waters experience icing have for many years had regulations defining and categorizing ice conditions and specifying design and standard requirements for ships operating in ice.
[줄 3360] [96.0%] (24/25) ✅ 유지 - Lloyd's Register have assigned special features notations to many existing ships for operation in first-year ice and for operation in multi-year ice.
[줄 3361] [96.0%] (24/25) ✅ 유지 - Firstyear ice notations are for additional strengthening where waters ice up in winter only and multi-year ice for service in Arctic and Antarctic waters.
[줄 3362] [95.5%] (64/67) ✅ 유지 - The increasing maritime trading within Arctic waters in the past decade and the desire to ship oil, gas, and other commodities from there all year round appears to have resulted in the class societies adopting to some extent the ice strengthening requirements of the 'Finnish–Swedish Ice Class Rules 1985' developed for vessels trading in winter and for which the keel was laid after 1 November 1986.
[줄 3363] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - These requirements were intended primarily for vessels operating in the Northern Baltic in winter are given for four different ice classes:
[줄 3364] [85.0%] (34/40) ✅ 유지 - Ice Class 1AA Ice Class 1A Ice Class 1B Ice Class 1C The hull scantling requirements determined under these rules are based on certain assumptions concerning the nature of the ice load the ship's structure may be subjected to.
[줄 3365] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - These assumptions have been determined from full-scale observations made in the Northern Baltic.
[줄 3366] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - This increased trading in Arctic waters has also created particular interest in the establishment of universal requirements for ships operating in ice.
[줄 3367] [87.5%] (28/32) ✅ 유지 - Both the IMO and IACS have been involved in this work, with the IMO producing guidelines in December 2002 for shipsoperatingin Arctic ice-covered waters forwhich they prescribe seven 'Polar Class' descriptions.
[줄 3368] [93.9%] (31/33) ✅ 유지 - These range from PC 1 for year-round operation in all Arctic ice covered waters to PC 7 for summer/autumn operation in thin first-year ice that may include old ice inclusions.
[줄 3369] [92.0%] (23/25) ✅ 유지 - Subsequently, the IACS set up a working group to develop Unified Requirements for Polar Ships that would cover: a Polar class descriptions and applications b.
[줄 3370] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - Structural requirements for Polar class ships c Machinery requirements for Polar class ships.
[줄 3371] [95.1%] (39/41) ✅ 유지 - It was intended that with the completion of these Uniform Requirements for Polar Ships and their adoption by the IACS Council, the IACS member societies will have one year in which to implement these common standards for ships operating in ice.

[줄 3452] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - The production of all steels used for shipbuilding purposes starts with the smelting of iron ore and the making of pig-iron.
[줄 3453] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Normally the iron ore is smelted in a blast furnace, which is a large, slightly conical structure lined with a refractory material.
[줄 3454] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - To provide the heat for smelting, coke is used and limestone is also added.
[줄 3455] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - This makes the slag formed by the incombustible impurities in the iron ore fluid, so that it can be drawn off.
[줄 3456] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - Air necessary for combustion is blown in through a ring of holes near the bottom, and the coke, ore, and limestone are charged into the top of the furnace in rotation.
[줄 3457] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - Molten metal may be drawn off at intervals from a hole or spout at the bottom of the furnace and run into molds formed in a bed of sand or into metal molds.
[줄 3458] [88.2%] (15/17) ✅ 유지 - The resultant pig-iron contains 92–97% iron, the remainder being carbon, silicon, manganese, sulfur, and phosphorus.
[줄 3459] [94.1%] (16/17) ✅ 유지 - In the subsequent manufacture of steels the pigiron is refined; in other words the impurities are reduced.
[줄 3460] [100.0%] (3/3) ✅ 유지 - All rights reserved.
[줄 3461] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - Propulsive characteristics and hull form Preliminary general arrangement Principal structural details.
[줄 3462] [93.5%] (29/31) ✅ 유지 - Each item of information may be considered in more detail, together with any restraints placed on these items by the ship's service or other factors outside the designer's control.
[줄 3463] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - The dimensions of most ships are primarily influenced by the cargo-carrying capacity of the vessel.
[줄 3464] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - In the case of the passenger vessel, dimensions are influenced by the height and length of superstructure containing the accommodation.
[줄 3465] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Length, where not specified as a maximum, should be a minimum consistent with the required speed and hull form.
[줄 3466] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Increase of length produces higher longitudinal bending stresses requiring additional strengthening and a greater displacement for the same cargo weight.
[줄 3467] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Breadth may be such as to provide adequate transverse stability.
[줄 3468] [93.5%] (43/46) ✅ 유지 - A minimum depth is controlled by the draft plus statutory freeboard, but an increase in depth will result in a reduction of the longitudinal bending stresses, providing an increase in strength, or allowing a reduction in scantlings i.e plate thickness/size of stiffening members etc..
[줄 3469] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - Increased depth is therefore preferred to increased length.
[줄 3470] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Draft is often limited by area of operation, but if it can be increased to give a greater depth this can be an advantage.
[줄 3471] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Many vessels are required to make passages through various canals and straits and pass under bridges within enclosed waters, and this will place a limitation on their dimensions.
[줄 3472] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - For example, locks in the Panama Canal and St Lawrence Seaway limit length, breadth, and draft.
[줄 3473] [89.2%] (33/37) ✅ 유지 - At the time of writing, the Malacca Straits main shipping channel is about 25 meters deep and the Suez Canal could accommodate ships with a beam of up to 75 meters and maximum draft of 16 metres.
[줄 3474] [96.8%] (30/31) ✅ 유지 - A maximum air draft on container ships of around 40 meters is very close to clear the heights of the Gerard Desmond Bridge, Long Beach, California and Bayonne Bridge, New York.
[줄 3475] [89.5%] (17/19) ✅ 유지 - Newer bridges over the Suez Canal at 65 meters and over the Bosporus at 62 meters provide greater clearance.
[줄 3476] [87.5%] (7/8) ✅ 유지 - Displacement is made up of lightweight plus deadweight.
[줄 3477] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - The lightweight is the weight of vessel as built and ready for sea.
[줄 3478] [93.8%] (30/32) ✅ 유지 - Deadweight is the difference between the lightweight and loaded displacement, i.e it is the weight of cargo plus weights of fuel, stores, water ballast, fresh water, crew and passengers, and baggage.
[줄 3479] [91.3%] (21/23) ✅ 유지 - When carrying high-density cargoes e.g ore it is desirable to keep the lightweight as small as possible, consistent with adequate strength.
[줄 3480] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - Since only cargo weight of the total deadweight is earning capital, other items should be kept to a minimum as long as the vessel fulfills its commitments.
[줄 3481] [95.8%] (23/24) ✅ 유지 - In determining the dimensions, statical stability is kept in mind in order to ensure that this is sufficient in all possible conditions of loading.
[줄 3482] [100.0%] (7/7) ✅ 유지 - Beam and depth are the main influences.
[줄 3483] [88.2%] (15/17) ✅ 유지 - Statutory freeboard and sheer are important together with the weight distribution in arranging the vessel's layout.
[줄 3484] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Adequate propulsive performance will ensure that the vessel attains the required speeds.
[줄 3485] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - The hull form is such that economically it offers a minimum resistance to motion so that a minimum power with economically lightest machinery is installed without losing the specified cargo capacity.
[줄 3486] [87.9%] (29/33) ✅ 유지 - Manufacture of steels Steels may be broadly considered as alloys of iron and carbon, the carbon percentage varying from about 0.1% in mild steels to about 1.8% in some hardened steels.
[줄 3487] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - These may be produced by one of four different processes: the open hearth process, the Bessemer converter process, the electric furnace process, or an oxygen process.
[줄 3488] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Processes may be either an acid or basic process according to the chemical nature of the slag produced.
[줄 3489] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Acid processes are used to refine pig-iron low in phosphorus and sulfur that are rich in silicon and therefore produce an acid slag.
[줄 3490] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - The furnace lining is constructed of an acid material so that it will prevent a reaction with the slag.
[줄 3491] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - A basic process is used to refine pig-iron that is rich in phosphorus and low in silicon.
[줄 3492] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Phosphorus can be removed only by introducing a large amount of lime, which produces a basic slag.
[줄 3493] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - The furnace lining must then be of a basic refractory to prevent a reaction with the slag.
[줄 3494] [96.6%] (28/29) ✅ 유지 - About 85% of all steel produced in Britain is of the basic type, and with modern techniques is almost as good as the acid steels produced with superior ores.
[줄 3495] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Only the open hearth, electric furnace, and oxygen processes are described here as the Bessemer converter process is not used for shipbuilding steels.
[줄 3496] [91.3%] (21/23) ✅ 유지 - Open hearth process The open hearth furnace is capable of producing large quantities of steel, handling 150–300 tonnes in a single melt.
[줄 3497] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - It consists of a shallow bath, roofed in, and set above two brick-lined heating chambers.
[줄 3498] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - At the ends are openings for heated air and fuel to be introduced into the furnace.
[줄 3499] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Also, these permit the escape of the burned gas, which is used for heating the air and fuel.
[줄 3500] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - Every 20 minutes or so the flow of air and fuel is reversed.
[줄 3501] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - In this process a mixture of pig-iron and steel scrap is melted in the furnace, carbon and the impurities being oxidized.
[줄 3502] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Oxidization is produced by the oxygen present in the iron oxide of the pig-iron.
[줄 3503] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Subsequently carbon, manganese, and other elements are added to eliminate iron oxides and give the required chemical composition.
[줄 3504] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Electric furnaces Electric furnaces are generally of two types: the arc furnace and the high-frequency induction furnace.
[줄 3505] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - The former is used for refining a charge to give the required composition, whereas the latter may only be used for melting down a charge whose composition is similar to that finally required.
[줄 3506] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - For this reason only the arc furnace is considered in any detail.
[줄 3507] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - In an arc furnace melting is produced by striking an arc between electrodes suspended from the roof of the furnace and the charge itself in the hearth of the furnace.
[줄 3508] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - A charge consists of pig-iron and steel scrap, and the process enables consistent results to be obtained and the final composition of the steel can be accurately controlled.
[줄 3509] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Electric furnace processes are often used for the production of high-grade alloy steels.
[줄 3510] [96.6%] (28/29) ✅ 유지 - Oxygen process This is a modern steelmaking process by which a molten charge of pig-iron and steel scrap with alloying elements is contained in a basic lined converter.
[줄 3511] [95.2%] (20/21) ✅ 유지 - A jet of highpurity gaseous oxygen is then directed onto the surface of the liquid metal in order to refine it.
[줄 3512] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Steel from the open hearth or electric furnace is tapped into large ladles and poured into ingot molds.
[줄 3513] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - It is allowed to cool in these molds until it becomes reasonably solidified, permitting it to be transferred to 'soaking pits' where the ingot is reheated to the required temperature for rolling.
[줄 3514] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Chemical additions to steels Additions of chemical elements to steels during the above processes serve several purposes.
[줄 3515] [96.2%] (25/26) ✅ 유지 - They may be used to deoxidize the metal, to remove impurities and bring them out into the slag, and finally to bring about the desired composition.
[줄 3516] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - The amount of deoxidizing elements added determines whether the steels are 'rimmed steels' or 'killed steels'.
[줄 3517] [94.1%] (16/17) ✅ 유지 - Rimmed steels are produced when only small additions of deoxidizing material are added to the molten metal.
[줄 3518] [77.8%] (14/18) ✅ 유지 - Only those steels having less than 0.2% carbon and less than 0.6% manganese can be rimmed.
[줄 3519] [96.4%] (27/28) ✅ 유지 - Owing to the absence of deoxidizing material, the oxygen in the steel combines with the carbon and other gases present and a large volume of gas is liberated.
[줄 3520] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - So long as the metal is molten, the gas passes upwards through the molten metal.
[줄 3521] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - When solidification takes place in ingot form, initially from the sides and bottom and then across the top, the gases can no longer leave the metal.
[줄 3522] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - In the central portion of the ingot a large quantity of gas is trapped, with the result that the core of the rimmed ingot is a mass of blow holes.
[줄 3523] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - Normally the hot rolling of the ingot into thin sheet is sufficient to weld the surfaces of the blow holes together, but this material is unsuitable for thicker plate.
[줄 3524] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - The term 'killed' steel indicates that the metal has solidified in the ingot mold with little or no evolution of gas.
[줄 3525] [94.1%] (16/17) ✅ 유지 - This has been prevented by the addition of sufficient quantities of deoxidizing material, normally silicon or aluminum.
[줄 3526] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Steel of this type has a high degree of chemical homogeneity, and killed steels are superior to rimmed steels.
[줄 3527] [91.3%] (21/23) ✅ 유지 - Where the process of deoxidation is only partially carried out by restricting the amount of deoxidizing material, a 'semi-killed' steel is produced.
[줄 3528] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - In the ingot mold the steel gradually solidifies from the sides and base, as mentioned previously.
[줄 3529] [97.7%] (42/43) ✅ 유지 - The melting points of impurities like sulfides and phosphides in the steel are lower than that of the pure metal and these will tend to separate out and collect towards the center and top of the ingot, which is the last to solidify.
[줄 3530] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - This forms what is known as the 'segregate' in the way of the noticeable contraction at the top of the ingot.
[줄 3531] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Owing to the high concentration of impurities at this point, this portion of the ingot is often discarded prior to rolling plate and sections.
[줄 3532] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Heat treatment of steels The properties of steels may be altered greatly by the heat treatment to which the steel is subsequently subjected.
[줄 3533] [94.4%] (17/18) ✅ 유지 - These heat treatments bring about a change in the mechanical properties principally by modifying the steel's structure.
[줄 3534] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - Those heat treatments that concern shipbuilding materials are described.
[줄 3535] [90.3%] (28/31) ✅ 유지 - Annealing This consists of heating the steel at a slow rate to a temperature of say 850–950  C, and then cooling it in the furnace at a very slow rate.
[줄 3536] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - The objects of annealing are to relieve any internal stresses, to soften the steel, or to bring the steel to a condition suitable for a subsequent heat treatment.
[줄 3537] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - Normalizing This is carried out by heating the steel slowly to a temperature similar to that for annealing and allowing it to cool in air.
[줄 3538] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - The resulting faster cooling rate produces a harder, stronger steel than annealing, and also refines the grain size.
[줄 3539] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Steel is heated to temperatures similar to that for annealing and normalizing, and then quenched in water or oil.
[줄 3540] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - The fast cooling rate produces a very hard structure with a higher tensile strength.
[줄 3541] [93.5%] (29/31) ✅ 유지 - Tempering Quenched steels may be further heated to a temperature somewhat between atmospheric and 680  C, and some alloy steels are then cooled fairly rapidly by quenching in oil or water.
[줄 3542] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - The object of this treatment is to relieve the severe internal stresses produced by the original hardening process and to make the material less brittle but retain the higher tensile stress.
[줄 3543] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Stress relieving To relieve internal stresses the temperature of the steel may be raised so that no structural change of the material occurs and then it may be slowly cooled.
[줄 3544] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Steel sections A range of steel sections are rolled hot from ingots.
[줄 3545] [84.6%] (11/13) ✅ 유지 - The more common types associated with shipbuilding are shown in Figure 5.1.
[줄 3546] [95.0%] (19/20) ✅ 유지 - It is preferable to limit the sections required for shipbuilding to those readily available, i.e the standard types; otherwise
[줄 3547] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - a steel mill is required to set up rolls for a small amount of material, which is not very economic.
[줄 3548] [82.6%] (19/23) ✅ 유지 - Shipbuilding steels Steel for hull construction purposes is usually mild steel containing 0.15–0.23% carbon and a reasonably high manganese content.
[줄 3549] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Both sulfur and phosphorus in the mild steel are kept to a minimum.
[줄 3550] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Higher concentrations of both are detrimental to the welding properties of the steel, and cracks can develop during the rolling process if the sulfur content is high.
[줄 3551] [96.6%] (28/29) ✅ 유지 - Steel for a ship classed with Lloyd's Register is produced by an approved manufacturer, and inspection and prescribed tests are carried out at the steel mill before dispatch.
[줄 3552] [94.4%] (17/18) ✅ 유지 - All certified materials are marked with the society's brand and other particulars as required by the rules.
[줄 3553] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - Ship classification societies originally had varying specifications for steel.
[줄 3554] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - However, in 1959, the major societies agreed to standardize their requirements in order to reduce the required grades of steel to a minimum.
[줄 3555] [95.2%] (20/21) ✅ 유지 - There are now five different qualities of steel employed in merchant ship construction and now often referred to as IACS steels.
[줄 3556] [80.8%] (21/26) ✅ 유지 - These are graded A, B, C, D, and E, Grade A being an ordinary mild steel to Lloyd's Register requirements and generally used in shipbuilding.
[줄 3557] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - Grade B is a better quality mild steel than Grade A and specified where thicker plates are required in the more critical regions.
[줄 3558] [78.9%] (15/19) ✅ 유지 - Grades C, D, and E possess increasing notch-tough characteristics, Grade C being to American Bureau of Shipping requirements.
[줄 3559] [80.0%] (24/30) ✅ 유지 - Lloyd's Register requirements for Grades A, B, D, and E steels may be found in Chapter 3 of Lloyd's Rules for the Manufacture, Testing and Certification of Materials.
