[줄 3561] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - High tensile steels Steels having a higher strength than that of mild steel are employed in the more highly stressed regions of large tankers, container ships, and bulk carriers.
[줄 3562] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - Use of higher strength steels allows reductions in thickness of deck, bottom shell, and framing where fitted in the midships portion of larger vessels; it does, however, lead to larger deflections.
[줄 3563] [96.6%] (28/29) ✅ 유지 - The weldability of higher tensile steels is an important consideration in their application in ship structures and the question of reduced fatigue life with these steels has been suggested.
[줄 3564] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Also, the effects of corrosion with lesser thicknesses of plate and section may require more vigilant inspection.
[줄 3565] [94.7%] (18/19) ✅ 유지 - Higher tensile steels used for hull construction purposes are manufactured and tested in accordance with Lloyd's Register requirements.
[줄 3566] [94.6%] (35/37) ✅ 유지 - Full specifications of the methods of manufacture, chemical composition, heat treatment, and mechanical properties required for the higher tensile steels are given in Chapter 3 of Lloyd's Rules for the Manufacture, Testing and Certification of Materials.
[줄 3567] [87.0%] (20/23) ✅ 유지 - The higher strength steels are available at three strength levels, 32, 36, and 40, when supplied in the as-rolled or normalized condition.
[줄 3568] [76.9%] (20/26) ✅ 유지 - Provision is also made for material with six higher strength levels, 42, 46, 50, 55, 62, and 69, when supplied in the quenched and tempered condition.
[줄 3569] [95.2%] (20/21) ✅ 유지 - Each strength level is subdivided into four grades, AH, DH, EH, and FH, depending on the required level of notch toughness.
[줄 3570] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - Corrosion-resistant steels Steels with alloying elements that give them good corrosion resistance and colloquially referred to as stainless steels are not commonly used in ship structures, primarily because of their higher initial and fabrication costs.
[줄 3571] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Only in the fabrication of cargo tanks containing highly corrosive cargoes might such steels be found.
[줄 3572] [96.2%] (25/26) ✅ 유지 - For oil tankers the inner surfaces, particularly the deckhead and bottom, are generally protected by high-cost corrosion-resistant coatings that require vigilant inspection and maintenance.
[줄 3573] [92.3%] (48/52) ✅ 유지 - A recent development in the manufacture of an alloyed shipbuilding steel with claimed improved corrosion resistance properties and its approval by Lloyd's Register for use in certain cargo tanks of a 105,000 dwt tanker indicate that in the future the need to coat oil cargo tanks might be dispensed with.
[줄 3574] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - Steel sandwich panels As an alternative to conventional shipyard-fabricated stiffened steel plate structures, proprietary manufactured steel sandwich panels have become available and used on ships where their lighter weight was important.
[줄 3575] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - Such panels consist of a steel core in
[줄 3576] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - the form of a honeycomb with flanges to which the external steel sheets are resistance or laser welded.
[줄 3577] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - Early use of these bought-in steel sandwich panels was primarily for nonhull structures in naval construction, where their light weight was important.
[줄 3578] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Such panels have also been used for the superstructures of passenger ships, where lightness can allow additional decks and hence increased passenger accommodation.
[줄 3579] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Also, when fabricated using stainless steel their corrosion resistance and low maintenance properties have been utilized.
[줄 3580] [94.7%] (18/19) ✅ 유지 - A proprietary steel sandwich plate system has been developed that consists of an elastomer core between steel face plates.
[줄 3581] [90.9%] (20/22) ✅ 유지 - Elastomers are a specific class of polyurethane that has a high tolerance to mechanical stress, i.e it rapidly recovers from deformation.
[줄 3582] [84.6%] (11/13) ✅ 유지 - The SPS elastomer also has a high resistance to most common chemical species.
[줄 3583] [97.3%] (36/37) ✅ 유지 - Initial application of SPS in shipbuilding has been in passenger ship superstructures, where the absence of stiffening has increased the space available and provided factory-finished surfaces with built-in vibration damping, acoustic insulation, and fire protection.
[줄 3584] [72.7%] (8/11) ✅ 유지 - SPS structures have been approved with an A 60 fireresistance rating.
[줄 3585] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - The main use of this system has been for repair of ships, especially decks.
[줄 3586] [93.3%] (14/15) ✅ 유지 - A single steel panel is used to secure the elastomer core to the existing deck.
[줄 3587] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - This creates a sandwich panel that is structurally acceptable.
[줄 3588] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - The major benefit is in the reduced time required to complete a major steelwork repair, compared to removing and replacing existing, corroded structure.
[줄 3589] [94.1%] (32/34) ✅ 유지 - SPS structures can be fabricated using joining technologies presently used in the shipbuilding industry, but the design of all joints must take into account the structural and material characteristics of the metal–elastomer composite.
[줄 3590] [96.6%] (28/29) ✅ 유지 - The manufacturer envisages the use of SPS panels throughout the hull and superstructure of ships, providing a simpler construction with greater carrying capacity and less corrosion, maintenance, and inspection.
[줄 3591] [92.9%] (26/28) ✅ 유지 - In association with the manufacturer, Lloyd's Register in early 2006 published provisional rules for the use of this sandwich plate system for new construction and ship repair.
[줄 3592] [90.9%] (20/22) ✅ 유지 - The rules cover construction procedures, scantling determination for primary supporting structures, framing arrangements, and methods of scantling determination for steel sandwich panels.
[줄 3593] [84.2%] (16/19) ✅ 유지 - The Norwegian classification society, Det Norske Veritas, have developed proposals for ship hulls using a lightweight concrete/steel sandwich.
[줄 3594] [96.8%] (30/31) ✅ 유지 - They envisaged a steel/concrete/steel composite structure for the cargo hold area of some 600 mm width for the side shell but somewhat greater width for the double bottom area.
[줄 3595] [97.7%] (43/44) ✅ 유지 - This sandwich would be much narrower than for a comparable steelonly double-skin bulk carrier, thus increasing the potential carrying capacity, although water ballast may have to be carried in some designated holds as the double skin would not be available for this purpose.
[줄 3596] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - DNV consider the other advantages of the concrete/steel sandwich to be reduced stress concentrations with less cracking in critical areas, considerable elimination of corrosion, and elimination of local buckling.

[줄 3600] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - Steel castings Molten steel produced by the open hearth, electric furnace, or oxygen process is poured into a carefully constructed mold and allowed to solidify to the shape required.
[줄 3601] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - After removal from the mold, a heat treatment is required, for example annealing, or normalizing and tempering to reduce brittleness.
[줄 3602] [94.1%] (16/17) ✅ 유지 - Stern frames, rudder frames, spectacle frames for bossings, and other structural components may be produced as castings.
[줄 3603] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - Steel forgings Forging is simply a method of shaping a metal by heating it to a temperature where it becomes more or less plastic and then hammering or squeezing it to the required form.
[줄 3604] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Forgings are manufactured from killed steel made by the open hearth, electric furnace, or oxygen process, the steel being in the form of ingots cast in chill molds.
[줄 3605] [96.2%] (25/26) ✅ 유지 - Adequate top and bottom discards are made to ensure no harmful segregations in the finished forgings and the sound ingot is gradually and uniformly hot worked.
[줄 3606] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Where possible the working of the metal is such that metal flow is in the most favorable direction with regard to the mode of stressing in service.
[줄 3607] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Subsequent heat treatment is required, preferably annealing or normalizing and tempering to remove effects of working and non-uniform cooling.

[줄 3613] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Aluminum alloy There are three advantages that aluminum alloys have over mild steel in the construction of ships.
[줄 3614] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - Firstly, aluminum is lighter than mild steel, and with an aluminum structure it has been suggested that up to 60% of the weight of a steel structure may be saved.
[줄 3615] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - This is in fact the principal advantage as far as merchant ships are concerned, the other two advantages of aluminum being a high resistance to corrosion and its nonmagnetic properties.
[줄 3616] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - The nonmagnetic properties can have advantages in warships and locally in the way of the magnetic compass, but they are generally of little importance in merchant vessels.
[줄 3617] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Good corrosion properties can be utilized, but correct maintenance procedures and careful insulation from the adjoining steel structure are necessary.
[줄 3618] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - A major disadvantage of the use of aluminum alloys is their higher initial and fabrication costs.
[줄 3619] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - The higher costs must be offset by an increased earning capacity of the vessel, resulting from a reduced lightship weight or increased passenger accommodation on the same ship dimensions.
[줄 3620] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - Experience with large passenger liners on the North Atlantic service has indicated that maintenance costs of aluminum alloy structures can be higher for this type of ship and service.
[줄 3621] [93.1%] (27/29) ✅ 유지 - Although aluminum was first used for small craft in 1891 and for experimental naval vessels in 1894, it has not been a significant material for ships until comparatively recently.
[줄 3622] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - A significant number of larger ships have been fitted with superstructures of aluminum alloy and, apart from the resulting reduction in displacement, benefits have been obtained in improving the transverse stability.
[줄 3623] [100.0%] (7/7) ✅ 유지 - Since the reduced weight of Ship Construction.
[줄 3624] [100.0%] (3/3) ✅ 유지 - All rights reserved.
[줄 3625] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - superstructure is at a position above the ship's center of gravity, this ensures a lower center of gravity than that obtained with a comparable steel structure.
[줄 3626] [97.6%] (41/42) ✅ 유지 - For example, on the Queen Elizabeth 2 with a limited beam to transit the Panama Canal, the top five decks constructed of aluminum alloy enabled the ship to support one more deck than would have been possible with an all-steel construction.

[줄 3628] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - Such ships are moderate- and high-speed passenger liners having a low deadweight.

[줄 3631] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Smaller naval vessels have often had aluminum superstructures on a steel hull as a weight saving measure.
[줄 3632] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - A difficulty is the joining of the two metals, in such a way as to avoid a corrosion cell being set up.
[줄 3633] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Either bolted connections with washers to separate the two metals, or an explosively bonded steel/aluminum transition piece can be used.
[줄 3634] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - In the explosively bonded material the interface between the metals remains corrosion free.

[줄 3653] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - Aluminum alloys Pure aluminum has a low tensile strength and is of little use for structural purposes; therefore, the pure metal is alloyed with small percentages of other materials to give greater tensile strengths.

[줄 3656] [95.2%] (20/21) ✅ 유지 - Cold working of the nonheat-treated plate has the effect of strengthening the material and this can be employed to advantage.
[줄 3657] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - However, at the same time the plate becomes less ductile, and if cold working is considerable the material may crack; this places a limit on the amount of cold forming possible in ship building.

[줄 3746] [88.9%] (32/36) ✅ 유지 - 7 Testing of materials Chapter Outline Classi fi cation society tests for hull materials 63 Metals are tested to ensure that their strength, ductility, and toughness are suitable for the function they are required to perform.
[줄 3747] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Material properties are important to the capability of the structure.
[줄 3748] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - The properties outlined below are appropriate in determining the suitability of a material for ship construction.
[줄 3749] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - The strength of the material is its ability to resist deformation.
[줄 3750] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Yield stress and ultimate tensile strength measure the ability to resist forces on the structure.
[줄 3751] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Hardness of a material describes its ability to resist abrasion.
[줄 3752] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Hardness is important, for example, in bulk carriers where the cargo handling produces abrasive action on the cargo hold structures.
[줄 3753] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - Hardness is usually measured on a scale, based on test results.
[줄 3754] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Ductility is the ability of a material to be deformed before it fails.
[줄 3755] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Brittleness is the opposite of ductility and describes a material that fails under stress because it cannot deform.
[줄 3756] [100.0%] (7/7) ✅ 유지 - Softer metals, such as aluminum, are ductile.
[줄 3757] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Hard materials such as cast iron are strong but brittle.
[줄 3758] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Toughness is the ability of a material to absorb energy.
[줄 3759] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - In comparing the strengths of various metals, stresses and strains are often referred to and require to be defined.
[줄 3760] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - Stress is a measure of the ability of a material to transmit a load, and the intensity of stress in the material, which is the load per unit area, is often stated.
[줄 3761] [90.0%] (54/60) ✅ 유지 - The load per unit area is simply obtained by dividing the applied load by the cross-sectional area of the material, e.g if a tensile load of P kg is applied to a rod having a cross-sectional area of A mm 2, then the tensile stress in the material of the rod is P / A kg/mm 2.
[줄 3762] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Total strain is defined as the total deformation that a body undergoes when subjected to an applied load.
[줄 3763] [86.0%] (37/43) ✅ 유지 - The strain is the deformation per unit length or unit volume, e.g if the tensile load P applied to the rod of original length l produces an elongation, or extension, of the rod of amount d l, then the tensile Ship Construction.
[줄 3764] [100.0%] (3/3) ✅ 유지 - All rights reserved.
[줄 3765] [88.5%] (23/26) ✅ 유지 - strain to which the material of the rod is subjected is given by the extension per unit length, i.e Extension Original length or d l
[줄 3766] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - It can be shown that the load on the rod may be increased uniformly and the resulting extension will also increase uniformly until a certain load is reached.
[줄 3767] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - This indicates that the load is proportional to extension, and hence stress and strain are proportional since the cross-sectional area and original length of the rod remain constant.
[줄 3768] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - For most metals this direct proportionality holds until what is known as the 'elastic limit' is reached.
[줄 3769] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - The metal behaves elastically to this point, the rod for example returning to its original length if the load is removed before the 'elastic limit' is reached.
[줄 3770] [94.7%] (36/38) ✅ 유지 - If a mild steel bar is placed in a testing machine and the extensions are recorded for uniformly increasing loads, a graph of load against extension, or stress against strain, may be plotted as in Figure 7.1.
[줄 3771] [94.7%] (18/19) ✅ 유지 - This shows the straight-line relationship i.e direct proportionality between stress and strain up to the elastic limit.
[줄 3772] [92.9%] (52/56) ✅ 유지 - Since stress is directly proportional to strain, the stress is equal to a constant, which is in fact the slope of the straight-line part of the graph, and is given by: A constant 1⁄4 stress O strain This constant is referred to as the modulus of elasticity for the metal and is denoted E.

[줄 3777] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - The yield stress for a metal corresponds to the stress at the 'yield point'; that is, the point at which the metal no longer behaves elastically.
[줄 3778] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Ultimate tensile stress is the maximum load to which the metal is subjected, divided by the original cross-sectional area.
[줄 3779] [94.7%] (36/38) ✅ 유지 - Beyond the yield point the metal behaves plastically, which means that the metal deforms at a greater, unproportional, rate when the yield stress is exceeded, and will not return to its original dimensions on removal of the load.
[줄 3780] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - It becomes deformed or is often said to be permanently 'set'.
[줄 3781] [100.0%] (41/41) ✅ 유지 - Many metals do not have a clearly defined yield point, for example aluminum, having a stress–strain curve over its lower range that is a straight line becoming gradually curved without any sharp transformation on yielding, as shown by mild steel.
[줄 3782] [94.9%] (37/39) ✅ 유지 - A 'proof stress' is quoted for the material and this may be obtained by setting off on the base some percentage of the strain, say 0.2%, and drawing a line parallel to the straight portion of the curve.
[줄 3783] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - The intersection of this line with the actual stress–strain curve marks the proof stress.
[줄 3784] [97.6%] (40/41) ✅ 유지 - It is worth noting at this stage that the ship's structure is designed for working stresses that are within the elastic range and much lower than the ultimate tensile strength of the material to allow a reasonable factor of safety.

[줄 3790] [100.0%] (35/35) ✅ 유지 - The basic principle of this test has already been described, a specimen of given dimensions being subject to an axial pull and a minimum specified yield stress, ultimate tensile stress, and elongation must be obtained.
[줄 3791] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - In order to make comparisons between the elongation of tensile test pieces of the same material the test pieces must have the same proportions of sectional area and gage length.
[줄 3792] [89.2%] (33/37) ✅ 유지 - Therefore, a standard gage length equal to 5.65 times the square root of the cross-sectional area, which is equivalent to a gage length of five times the diameter, is adopted by the major classification societies.
[줄 3793] [85.2%] (23/27) ✅ 유지 - There are several forms of impact test, but the Charpy V-notch test or Charpy U-notch test is commonly specified and therefore described in this text.
[줄 3794] [100.0%] (4/4) ✅ 유지 - The object of the

[줄 3798] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - This specimen is placed on an anvil and the pendulum is allowed to swing so that the striker hits the specimen opposite the notch and fractures it.
[줄 3799] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Energy absorbed in fracturing the specimen is automatically recorded by the machine.
[줄 3800] [100.0%] (39/39) ✅ 유지 - Basically, making allowances for friction, the energy absorbed in fracturing the specimen is the difference between the potential energy the pendulum possesses before being released, and that which it attains in swinging past the vertical after fracturing the specimen.
[줄 3801] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - A specified average impact energy for the specimens tested must be obtained at the specified test temperature, fracture energy being dependent on temperature, as will be illustrated in Chapter 8.
[줄 3802] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Aluminum alloy plate and section material is subject to specified tensile tests.
[줄 3803] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Bar material for aluminum alloy rivets is subject to a tensile test and also a dump test.
[줄 3804] [91.3%] (21/23) ✅ 유지 - The latter test requires compression of the bar until its diameter is increased to 1.6 times the original diameter without cracking occurring.
[줄 3805] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - Selected manufactured rivets are also subjected to the same dump test.

[줄 3810] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - The stresses experienced by the ship floating in still water and when at sea may conveniently be considered separately.
[줄 3811] [100.0%] (35/35) ✅ 유지 - Vertical shear and longitudinal bending in still water If a homogeneous body of uniform cross-section and weight is floating in still water, at any section the weight and buoyancy forces are equal and opposite.
[줄 3812] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Therefore, there is no resultant force at a section and the body will not be stressed or deformed.
[줄 3813] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - A ship floating in still water has an unevenly distributed weight owing to both cargo distribution and structural distribution.
[줄 3814] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - The buoyancy distribution is also non-uniform since the underwater sectional area is not constant along the length.
[줄 3815] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Total weight and total buoyancy are of course balanced, but at each section there will be a resultant force or load, either an excess of buoyancy or excess of load.
[줄 3816] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Since the vessel remains intact there are vertical upward and downward forces tending to distort the vessel Ship Construction.

[줄 3819] [95.2%] (20/21) ✅ 유지 - The final building specification and design is prepared by the successful tendering shipbuilder in cooperation with the owner's technical staff.
[줄 3820] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - The latter may oversee construction of the vessel and approve the builder's drawings and calculations.
[줄 3821] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - Other shipowners may retain a firm of consultants or approach a firm who may assist with preliminary design studies and will prepare the tender specifications and in some cases call tenders on behalf of the owner.
[줄 3822] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Often the consultants will also assist the owners in evaluating the tenders and oversee the construction on their behalf.
[줄 3823] [97.4%] (38/39) ✅ 유지 - Ship contracts The successful tendering shipbuilder will prepare a building specification for approval by the owner or the owner's representative that will form an integral part of the contract between the two parties and thus have legal status.
[줄 3824] [98.5%] (64/65) ✅ 유지 - This technical specification will normally include the following information: Brief description and essential qualities and characteristics of the ship Principal dimensions Deadweight, cargo and tank capacities, etc Speed and power requirements Stability requirements Quality and standard of workmanship Survey and certificates Accommodation details Trial conditions Equipment and fittings Machinery details, including the electrical installation, will normally be produced as a separate section of the specification.
[줄 3825] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - Most shipbuilding contracts are based on one of a number of standard forms of contract that have been established to obtain some uniformity in the contract relationship between builders and purchasers.
[줄 3826] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - There are a number of 'standard' contract forms, all very similar in structure and content.

[줄 3835] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - which are referred to as vertical shearing forces, since they tend to shear the vertical material in the hull.
[줄 3836] [94.4%] (34/36) ✅ 유지 - The ship shown in Figure 8.1 will be loaded in a similar manner to the beam shown below it, and will tend to bend in a similar manner owing to the variation in vertical loading.
[줄 3837] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - It can be seen that the upper fibers of the beam will be in tension, as will the material forming the deck of the ship with this loading.
[줄 3838] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Conversely, the lower fibers of the beam, and likewise the material forming the bottom of the ship, will be in compression.
[줄 3839] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - A vessel bending in this manner is said to be 'hogging' and if it takes up the reverse form with excess weight amidships is said to be 'sagging'.
[줄 3840] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - When sagging the deck will be in compression and the bottom shell in tension.
[줄 3841] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - Lying in still water the vessel is subjected to bending moments either hogging and sagging depending on the relative weight and buoyancy forces, and it will also be subjected to vertical shear forces.
[줄 3842] [100.0%] (39/39) ✅ 유지 - Bending moments in a seaway When a ship is in a seaway the waves with their troughs and crests produce a greater variation in the buoyant forces and therefore can increase the bending moment, vertical shear force, and stresses.
[줄 3843] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Classically the extreme effects can be illustrated with the vessel balanced on a wave of length equal to that of the ship.
[줄 3844] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - If the crest of the wave is amidships the buoyancy forces will tend to 'hog' the vessel; if the trough is amidships the buoyancy forces will tend to 'sag' the ship.
[줄 3845] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - In a seaway the overall effect is an increase of bending moment from that in still water when the greater buoyancy variation is taken into account.
[줄 3846] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Longitudinal shear forces When the vessel hogs and sags in still water and at sea, shear forces similar to the vertical shear forces will be present in the longitudinal plane.
[줄 3847] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Vertical and longitudinal shear stresses are complementary and exist in conjunction with a change of bending moment between adjacent sections of the hull girder.
[줄 3848] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - The magnitude of the longitudinal shear force is greatest at the neutral axis and decreases towards the top and bottom of the girder.
[줄 3849] [77.6%] (45/58) ✅ 유지 - Bending stresses From classic bending theory the bending stress at any point in a beam is given by: s 1⁄4 M I  y where M 1⁄4 applied bending moment, y 1⁄4 distance of point considered from neutral axis, and I 1⁄4 second moment of area of cross-section of beam about the neutral axis.
[줄 3850] [100.0%] (4/4) ✅ 유지 - Crest Crest Crest Crest
[줄 3851] [84.6%] (11/13) ✅ 유지 - Trough Trough SAGGING HOGGING Longitudinal shear forces Figure 8.2 Wave bending moments.
[줄 3852] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - When the beam bends it is seen that the extreme fibers are, say in the case of hogging, in tension at the top and in compression at the bottom.
[줄 3853] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Somewhere between the two there is a position where the fibers are neither in tension nor compression.
[줄 3854] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - This position is called the neutral axis, and at the furthest fibers from the neutral axis the greatest stress occurs for plane bending.
[줄 3855] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - It should be noted that the neutral axis always contains the center of gravity of the cross-section.
[줄 3856] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - In the equation the second moment of area of the section is a divisor; therefore, the greater the value of the second moment of area, the less the bending stress will be.
[줄 3857] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - This second moment of area of section varies as the depth squared and therefore a small increase in depth of section can be very beneficial in reducing the bending stress.
[줄 3858] [87.5%] (35/40) ✅ 유지 - Occasionally reference is made to the sectional modulus of a beam; this is simply the ratio between the second moment of area and the distance of the point considered from the neutral axis, i.e I / y 1⁄4 Z.
[줄 3859] [58.3%] (7/12) ❌ 제거 - The bending stress is then given by s 1⁄4 M / Z.
[줄 3860] [100.0%] (45/45) ✅ 유지 - The ship as a beam It was seen earlier that the ship bends like a beam, and in fact the hull can be considered as a box-shaped girder for which the position of the neutral axis and second moment of area may be calculated.
[줄 3861] [100.0%] (35/35) ✅ 유지 - The deck and bottom shell form the flanges of the hull girder, and are far more important to longitudinal strength than the sides that form the web of the girder and carry the shear forces.
[줄 3862] [87.5%] (14/16) ✅ 유지 - The box-shaped hull girder and a conventional I girder are compared in Figure 8.3.
[줄 3863] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - In a ship the neutral axis is generally nearer the bottom, since the bottom shell will be heavier than the deck, having to resist water pressure as well as the bending stresses.
[줄 3864] [100.0%] (42/42) ✅ 유지 - In calculating the second moment of an area of the cross-section all longitudinal material is of greatest importance and the further the material is from the neutral axis, the greater will be its second moment of area about the neutral axis.
[줄 3865] [97.1%] (33/34) ✅ 유지 - However, at greater distances from the neutral axis, the sectional modulus will be reduced and correspondingly higher stress may occur in extreme hull girder plates such as the deck stringer, sheer strake, and bilge.
[줄 3866] [90.0%] (9/10) ✅ 유지 - These strakes of plating are generally heavier than other plating.
[줄 3867] [90.0%] (27/30) ✅ 유지 - Bending stresses are greater over the middle portion of the length and it is owing to this variation that Lloyd's give maximum scantlings over 40% of the length amidships.
[줄 3868] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - Other scantlings may taper towards the ends of the ship, apart from locally highly stressed regions where other forms of loading are encountered.
[줄 3869] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Strength deck The deck forming the uppermost flange of the main hull girder is often referred to as the strength deck.
[줄 3870] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - This is to some extent a misleading term since all continuous decks are in fact strength decks if properly constructed.
[줄 3871] [97.7%] (43/44) ✅ 유지 - Along the length of the ship the top flange of the hull girder, i.e the strength deck, may step from deck to deck where large superstructures are fitted or there is a natural break, for instance in way of a raised quarter deck.
[줄 3872] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Larger superstructures tend to deform with the main hull and stresses of
[줄 3873] [92.0%] (23/25) ✅ 유지 - Flange Web Web Web I SECTION GIRDER BOX GIRDER SHIP HULL GIRDER Flange Flange Flange Flange Flange Figure 8.3 Box girder and I girder.
[줄 3874] [100.0%] (7/7) ✅ 유지 - appreciable magnitude will occur in the structure.
[줄 3875] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Early vessels fitted with large superstructures of light construction demonstrated this to their cost.
[줄 3876] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Attempts to avoid fracture have been made by fitting expansion joints, which made the light structure discontinuous.
[줄 3877] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - These were not entirely successful and the expansion joint may itself form a stress concentration at the strength deck, which one would wish to avoid.
[줄 3878] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - In modern construction the superstructure is usually made continuous and of such strength that its sectional modulus is equivalent to that which the strength deck would have if no superstructure were fitted.
[줄 3879] [96.0%] (24/25) ✅ 유지 - Transverse stresses When a ship experiences transverse forces these tend to change the shape of the vessel's cross-sections and thereby introduce transverse stresses.
[줄 3880] [96.8%] (30/31) ✅ 유지 - These forces may be produced by hydrostatic loads and impact of seas or cargo and structural weights, both directly and as the result of reactions due to change of ship motion.
[줄 3881] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - Racking When a ship is rolling, the deck tends to move laterally relative to the bottom structure, and the shell on one side to move vertically relative to the other side.
[줄 3882] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - This type of deformation is referred to as 'racking'.
[줄 3883] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - Transverse bulkheads primarily resist such transverse deformation, the side frames' contribution being insignificant provided the transverse bulkheads are at their usual regular spacings.
[줄 3884] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - Where transverse bulkheads are widely spaced, deep web frames and beams may be introduced to compensate.
[줄 3885] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - When any body is subject to a twisting moment, which is commonly referred to as torque, that body is said to be in 'torsion'.
[줄 3886] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - A ship heading obliquely to a wave will be subjected to righting moments of opposite direction at its ends, twisting the hull and putting it in 'torsion'.
[줄 3887] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - In most ships these torsional moments and stresses are negligible but in ships with extremely wide and long deck openings they are significant.
[줄 3888] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - A particular example is the larger container ship, where at the topsides a heavy torsion box girder structure including the upper deck is provided to accommodate the torsional stresses.
[줄 3889] [95.0%] (38/40) ✅ 유지 - Local stresses Panting Panting refers to a tendency for the shell plating to work 'in' and 'out' in a bellowslike fashion, and is caused by the fluctuating pressures on the hull at the ends when the ship is amongst waves.
[줄 3890] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - These forces are most severe when the vessel is running into
[줄 3891] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - waves and is pitching heavily, the large pressures occurring over a short time cycle.
[줄 3892] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - Strengthening to resist panting both forward and aft is covered in Chapter 17.
[줄 3893] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Pounding Severe local stresses occur in way of the bottom shell and framing forward when a vessel is driven into head seas.
[줄 3894] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - These pounding stresses, as they are known, are likely to be most severe in a lightly ballasted condition, and occur over an area of the bottom shell aft of the collision bulkhead.
[줄 3895] [92.9%] (13/14) ✅ 유지 - Additional stiffening is required in this region; this is dealt with in Chapter 16.
[줄 3896] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Other local stresses Ship structural members are often subjected to high stresses in localized areas, and great care is required to ensure that these areas are correctly designed.
[줄 3897] [91.7%] (33/36) ✅ 유지 - This is particularly the case where various load-carrying members of the ship intersect, examples being where longitudinals meet at transverse bulkheads and at intersections Crest Crest Container ship section Torsion box Figure 8.4 Torsion.
[줄 3898] [100.0%] (5/5) ✅ 유지 - of longitudinal and transverse bulkheads.
[줄 3899] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - Another highly stressed area occurs where there is a discontinuity of the hull girder at ends of deck house structures, also at hatch and other opening corners, and where there are sudden breaks in the bulwarks.
[줄 3900] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - Brittle fracture With the large-scale introduction of welding in ship construction, much consideration has been given to the correct selection of materials and structural design to prevent the possibility of brittle fracture occurring.
[줄 3901] [96.2%] (25/26) ✅ 유지 - During the Second World War the incidence of this phenomenon was high amongst tonnage hastily constructed, whilst little was known about the mechanics of brittle fracture.
[줄 3902] [100.0%] (43/43) ✅ 유지 - Although instances of brittle fracture were recorded in riveted ships, the consequences were more disastrous in the welded vessels because of the continuity of metal provided by the welded joint as opposed to the riveted lap, which tended to limit the propagating crack.
[줄 3903] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Brittle fracture occurs when an otherwise elastic material fractures without any apparent sign or little evidence of material deformation prior to failure.
[줄 3904] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - Fracture occurs instantaneously with little warning and the vessel's overall structure need not be subject to a high stress at the time.
[줄 3905] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Mild steel used extensively in ship construction is particularly prone to brittle fracture given the conditions necessary to trigger it off.
[줄 3906] [97.7%] (42/43) ✅ 유지 - The subject is too complex to be dealt with in detail in this text, but it is known that the following factors influence the possibility of brittle fracture and are taken into consideration in the design and material selection of modern ships: 1.
[줄 3907] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - A sharp notch is present in the structure from which the fracture initiates.
[줄 3908] [100.0%] (5/5) ✅ 유지 - A tensile stress is present.
[줄 3909] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - There is a temperature above which brittle fracture will not occur.
[줄 3910] [100.0%] (7/7) ✅ 유지 - The metallurgical properties of the steel plate.
[줄 3911] [100.0%] (5/5) ✅ 유지 - Thick plate is more prone.
[줄 3912] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - A brittle fracture is distinguishable from a ductile failure by the lack of deformation at the edge of the tear, and its bright granular appearance.
[줄 3913] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - A ductile failure has a dull gray appearance.
[줄 3914] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - The brittle fracture is also distinguished by the apparent chevron marking, which aids location of the fracture initiation point since these tend to point in that direction.
[줄 3915] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Factors that are known to exist where a brittle fracture may occur must be considered if this is to be avoided.
[줄 3916] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Firstly, the design of individual items of ship structure must be such that sharp notches where cracks may be initiated are avoided.
[줄 3917] [100.0%] (35/35) ✅ 유지 - With welded structures as large as a ship the complete elimination of crack initiation is not entirely possible owing to the existence of small faults in the welds, a complete weld examination not being practicable.
[줄 3918] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Steel specified for the hull construction should therefore have good 'notch ductility' at the service temperatures, particularly where thick plate is used.
[줄 3919] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Provision of steel having good 'notch ductility' properties has the effect of making it difficult for a crack to propagate.
[줄 3920] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Notch ductility is a measure of the relative toughness of the steel, which has already been seen to be determined by an impact test.
[줄 3921] [100.0%] (7/7) ✅ 유지 - Steels specified for ship construction have elements
[줄 3922] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - added, and may also be subjected to a controlled heat treatment, which will enhance the notch toughness properties.
[줄 3923] [88.9%] (16/18) ✅ 유지 - Figure 8.5 illustrates the improved notch ductility of a manganese/carbon steel against a plain carbon steel.
[줄 3924] [94.6%] (35/37) ✅ 유지 - Grade D and Grade E steels, which have higher notch ductility, are employed where thick plate is used and in way of higher stressed regions, as will be seen when the ship structural details are considered later.
[줄 3925] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - In association with the problem of brittle fracture it was not uncommon at one time to hear reference to the term 'crack arrester'.
[줄 3926] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - The term related to the now outdated practice of introducing riveted seams in cargo ships to subdivide the vessel into welded substructures so that any possible crack propagation was limited to the substructure.
[줄 3927] [88.9%] (16/18) ✅ 유지 - In particular, such a 'crack arrester' was usually specified in the sheerstrake/stringer plate area of larger ships.
[줄 3928] [93.3%] (14/15) ✅ 유지 - Today strakes of higher notch toughness steel are required to be fitted in such areas.
[줄 3929] [84.8%] (39/46) ✅ 유지 - Lloyd's Register, for example, require the mild steel sheerstrake and stringer plate at the strength deck over the midship portion of vessels of more than 250 meters length to be Grade D if less than 15 mm thick and Grade E if of greater thickness.
[줄 3930] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Fatigue failures Unlike brittle fracture, fatigue fracture occurs very slowly and can in fact take years to propagate.
[줄 3931] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - The greatest danger with fatigue fractures is that they occur at low stresses that are applied to a structure repeatedly over a period of time.
[줄 3932] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - A fatigue crack, once initiated, may grow unnoticed until the load-bearing member is reduced to a cross-sectional area that is insufficient to carry the applied load.
[줄 3933] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - Fatigue failures are associated with sharp notches or discontinuities in structures, and are especially prevalent at 'hard spots', i.e regions of high rigidity in ship structures.
[줄 3934] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - With the growth in size of oil tankers, bulk carriers, and container ships there has been increasing use of higher yield strength steels in their hull structures.
[줄 3935] [96.8%] (30/31) ✅ 유지 - The classification societies have subsequently placed special emphasis on analysis of the fatigue performance of these larger structures, usually over a 25-year life cycle, as part of their approval process.

[줄 3984] [85.7%] (6/7) ✅ 유지 - For the shipbuilder the advantages are: 1.

[줄 3992] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - The smoother hull with the elimination of overlapping plate joints leads to reduced skin friction resistance, which can reduce fuel costs.
[줄 3993] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Other than some blacksmith work involving solid-phase welding, the welding processes employed in shipbuilding are of the fusion welding type.
[줄 3994] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - Fusion welding is achieved by means of a heat source that is intense enough to melt the edges of the material to be joined as it is traversed along the joint.
[줄 3995] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Gas welding, arc welding, laser welding, and resistance welding all provide heat sources of sufficient intensity to achieve fusion welds.
[줄 3996] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - Gas welding A gas flame was probably the first form of heat source to be used for fusion welding, and a variety of fuel gases with oxygen have been used to produce a high-temperature flame.
[줄 3997] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - The most commonly used gas in use is acetylene, which gives an intense concentrated flame when burnt in oxygen.
[줄 3998] [100.0%] (40/40) ✅ 유지 - An oxyacetylene flame has two distinct regions: an inner cone, in which the oxygen for combustion is supplied via the torch; and a surrounding envelope, in which some or all the oxygen for combustion is drawn from the surrounding air.
[줄 3999] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - By varying the ratio of oxygen to acetylene in the gas mixture supplied by the torch, it is possible to vary the efficiency of the combustion and alter the nature of the flame.
[줄 4000] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - If the oxygen supply is slightly greater than the supply of acetylene by volume, what is known as an 'oxidizing' flame is obtained.
[줄 4001] [90.9%] (30/33) ✅ 유지 - This type of flame may be used for welding materials of high thermal conductivity, e.g copper, but not steels, as the steel may be decarburized and the weld pool depleted of silicon.
[줄 4002] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - With equal amounts of acetylene and oxygen a 'neutral' flame is obtained, and this would normally be used for welding steels and most other metals.
[줄 4003] [95.8%] (23/24) ✅ 유지 - Where the acetylene supply exceeds the oxygen by volume a 'carburizing' flame is obtained, the excess acetylene decomposing and producing submicroscopic particles of carbon.
[줄 4004] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - These readily go into solution in the molten steel, and can produce metallurgical problems in service.
[줄 4005] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - The outer envelope of the oxyacetylene flame by consuming the surrounding oxygen to some extent protects the molten weld metal pool from the surrounding air.
[줄 4006] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - If unprotected the oxygen may diffuse into the molten metal and produce porosity

[줄 4020] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - Electric arc welding The basic principle of electric arc welding is that a wire or electrode is connected to a source of electrical supply with a return lead to the plates to be welded.
[줄 4021] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - If the electrode is brought into contact with the plates an electric current flows in the circuit.
[줄 4022] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - By removing the electrode a short distance from the plate, so that the electric current is able to jump the gap, a high-temperature electrical arc is created.
[줄 4023] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - This will melt the plate edges and the end of the electrode if this is of the consumable type.
[줄 4024] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Electrical power sources vary, DC generators or rectifiers with variable or constant voltage characteristics being available, as well as AC transformers with variable voltage characteristics for single or multiple operation.
[줄 4025] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - The latter are most commonly used in shipbuilding.

[줄 4075] [97.4%] (38/39) ✅ 유지 - Gas-shielded arc welding processes The application of bare wire welding with gas shielding was developed in the 1960s, and was quickly adopted for the welding of lighter steel structures in shipyards, as well as for welding aluminum alloys.

[줄 4077] [91.3%] (21/23) ✅ 유지 - Tungsten inert gas welding In the TIG welding process the arc is drawn between a water-cooled nonconsumable tungsten electrode and the plate.
[줄 4078] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - An inert gas shield is provided to protect the weld metal from the atmosphere, and filler metal may be added to the weld pool as required.

[줄 4080] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Normally in Britain the inert gas shield used for welding aluminum and steel is argon.
[줄 4081] [96.4%] (27/28) ✅ 유지 - Only plate thicknesses of less than 6 mm would normally be welded by this process, and in particular aluminum sheet, a skilled operator being required for manual work.
[줄 4082] [86.7%] (13/15) ✅ 유지 - This may also be referred to as TAGS welding, i.e tungsten arc gasshielded welding.
[줄 4083] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - Metal inert gas welding This is in effect an extension of TIG welding, the electrode in this process becoming a consumable metal wire.
[줄 4084] [93.1%] (27/29) ✅ 유지 - Basically the process is as illustrated in Figure 9.6, a wire feed motor supplying wire via guide rollers through a contact tube in the torch to the arc.
[줄 4085] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - An inert gas is supplied to the torch to shield the arc, and electrical connections are made to the contact tube and workpiece.
[줄 4086] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - Welding is almost always done with a DC source and electrode positive for regular metal transfer, and when welding aluminum to remove the oxide film by the action of the arc cathode.
[줄 4087] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - Although the process may be fully automatic, semi-automatic processes as illustrated with hand gun are now in greater use, and are particularly suitable in many cases for application to shipyard work.

[줄 4094] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Initially aluminum accounted for most of the MIG welding, with argon being used as the inert shielding gas.
[줄 4095] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - Much of the welding undertaken on aluminum deckhouses, and liquid methane gas tanks of specialized carriers, has made use of this process.
[줄 4096] [97.3%] (36/37) ✅ 유지 - Generally larger wire sizes and heavier currents have been employed in this work, metal transfer in the arc being by means of a spray transfer, i.e metal droplets being projected at high speed across the arc.
[줄 4097] [100.0%] (35/35) ✅ 유지 - At low currents metal transfer in the arc is rather difficult and very little fusion of the plate results, which has made the welding of light aluminum plate rather difficult with the MIG/argon process.
[줄 4098] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - The introduction of the 'pulsed arc' process has to some extent overcome this problem and made positional welding easier.
[줄 4099] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Here a low-level current is used with high-level pulses of current that detach the metal from the electrode and accelerate it across the arc to give good penetration.
[줄 4100] [97.8%] (45/46) ✅ 유지 - Early work on the welding of mild steel with the metal inert gas process made use of argon as a shielding gas, but as this gas is rather expensive, and satisfactory welding could only be accomplished in the downhand position, an alternative shielding gas was sought.
[줄 4101] [93.3%] (28/30) ✅ 유지 - Research in this direction was concentrated on the use of CO 2 as the shielding gas, and the MIG/CO 2 process is now widely used for welding mild steel.
[줄 4102] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Using higher current values with thicker steel plate a fine spray transfer of the metal from the electrode across the arc is achieved, with a deep penetration.
[줄 4103] [87.5%] (21/24) ✅ 유지 - Wire diameters in excess of 1.6 mm are used, and currents above about 350 amps are required to obtain this form of transfer.
[줄 4104] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - Much of the higher current work is undertaken with automatic machines, but some semi-automatic torches are available to operate in this range in the hands of skilled welders.
[줄 4105] [75.0%] (3/4) ✅ 유지 - Welding is downhand only.
[줄 4106] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - On thinner plating where lower currents would be employed, a different mode of transfer of metal in the arc is achieved with the MIG/CO 2 process.
[줄 4107] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - This form of welding is referred to as the dip transfer process.
[줄 4108] [85.7%] (6/7) ✅ 유지 - The sequence of metal transfer is : 1.
[줄 4109] [100.0%] (3/3) ✅ 유지 - Establish the arc.
[줄 4110] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Wire fed into arc until it makes contact with plate.
[줄 4111] [100.0%] (8/8) ✅ 유지 - Resistance heating of wire in contact with plate.
[줄 4112] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Pinch effect, detaching heated portion of wire as droplet of molten metal.
[줄 4113] [100.0%] (4/4) ✅ 유지 - Re-establish the arc.
[줄 4114] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - To prevent a rapid rise of current and 'blast off' of the end of the wire when it shortcircuits on the plate, variable inductance is introduced in the electrical circuit.
[줄 4115] [83.3%] (20/24) ✅ 유지 - Smaller wire diameters, 0.8 and 1.2 mm, are used where the dip transfer method is employed on lighter plate at low currents.
[줄 4116] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - The process is suitable for welding light mild steel plate in all positions.
[줄 4117] [95.0%] (19/20) ✅ 유지 - It may be used in shipbuilding as a semi-automatic process, particularly for welding deckhouses and other light steel assemblies.
[줄 4118] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - The pulsed MIG/argon process, developed for positional welding of light aluminum plate, may be used for positional welding of light steel plate but is likely to prove more expensive.
[줄 4119] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Use of the MIG semi-automatic processes can considerably increase weld output and lower costs.
[줄 4120] [95.0%] (19/20) ✅ 유지 - This form of welding may also be collectively referred to as MAGS welding, i.e metal arc gas-shielded welding.
[줄 4121] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - Plasma welding This is very similar to TIG welding as the arc is formed between a pointed tungsten electrode and the plate.
[줄 4122] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - But, with the tungsten electrode positioned within the body of the torch, the plasma arc is separated from the shielding gas envelope.
[줄 4123] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Plasma is forced through a fine-bore copper nozzle that constricts the arc.
[줄 4124] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - By varying the bore diameter and plasma gas flow rate, three different operating modes can be achieved:
[줄 4125] [93.3%] (14/15) ✅ 유지 - Microplasmathe arc is operated at very low welding currents and used for welding thin sheets.
[줄 4126] [75.0%] (9/12) ✅ 유지 - Medium currentthe arc is operated at currents from 15 to 200 amps.
[줄 4127] [95.8%] (23/24) ✅ 유지 - Plasma welding is an alternative to conventional TIG welding, but with the advantage of achieving deeper penetration and having greater tolerance to surface contamination.
[줄 4128] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Because of the bulkiness of the torch, it is more suited to mechanized welding than hand welding.
[줄 4129] [91.3%] (21/23) ✅ 유지 - Keyhole plasmathe arc is operated at currents above 100 amps and by increasing the plasma flow a very powerful plasma beam is created.
[줄 4130] [91.7%] (22/24) ✅ 유지 - This can penetrate thicknesses up to 10 mm, but when using a single-pass technique is normally limited to a thickness of 6 mm.
[줄 4131] [92.9%] (13/14) ✅ 유지 - This operating mode is normally used for welding sheet metal in the downhand position.
[줄 4132] [78.9%] (15/19) ✅ 유지 - Nozzle Shielding gas Plate Plasma gas Tungsten electrode Cooling water Power source +ve –ve Figure 9.7 Plasma welding.
[줄 4133] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Other welding processes There are some welding processes that cannot strictly be classified as gas or arc welding processes and these are considered separately.
[줄 4134] [95.6%] (43/45) ✅ 유지 - Electro-slag welding The electro-slag welding process is used for welding heavy casting structure components such as stern frames and was also used at an earlier stage to make vertical welds in heavier side shell when fabricated hull units where joined at the berth.
[줄 4135] [90.0%] (18/20) ✅ 유지 - With the development of the electro-gas welding process, electro-slag welding is no longer used for the latter purpose.
[줄 4136] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - To start the weld an arc is struck, but welding is achieved by resistance path heating through the flux, the initial arcing having been discouraged once welding is started.
[줄 4137] [91.2%] (31/34) ✅ 유지 - In Figure 9.8 the basic electro-slag process is illustrated; the current passes into the weld pool through the wire, and the copper water-cooled shoes retain the molten pool of weld metal.
[줄 4138] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - These may be mechanized so that they move up the plate as the weld is completed, flux being fed into the weld manually by the operator.
[줄 4139] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - A square edge preparation is used on the plates, and it is found that the final weld metal has a high plate dilution.
[줄 4140] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - 'Run-on' and 'run-off' plates are required for stopping and starting the weld, and it is desirable that the weld should be continuous.
[줄 4141] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - If a stoppage occurs it will be impossible to avoid a major slag inclusion in the weld, and it may then be necessary to cut out the original metal and start again.
[줄 4142] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - If very good weld properties are required with a fine grain structure
[줄 4143] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - it is necessary to carry out a local normalizing treatment.
[줄 4144] [87.5%] (14/16) ✅ 유지 - Electro-gas welding Of greater interest to the shipbuilder is a further development, electro-gas welding.
[줄 4145] [90.0%] (18/20) ✅ 유지 - This is in fact an arc welding process that combines features of gasshielded welding with those of electro-slag welding.
[줄 4146] [96.8%] (30/31) ✅ 유지 - Water-cooled copper shoes similar to those for the electro-slag welding process are used, but a flux-cored wire rather than a bare wire is fed into the weld pool.
[줄 4147] [95.7%] (45/47) ✅ 유지 - Fusion is obtained by means of an arc established between the surface of the weld pool and the wire, and the CO 2 or CO 2 with argon mixture gas shield is supplied from separate nozzles or holes located centrally near the top of the copper shoes.
[줄 4148] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - The system is mechanized utilizing an automatic vertical-up welding machine fed by a power source and having a closed-loop cooling circuit and a level sensor that automatically adjusts the vertical travel speed.
[줄 4149] [94.6%] (53/56) ✅ 유지 - The process is more suitable for welding plates in the thickness range of 13–50 mm with square or vee edge preparations and is therefore used for shipbuilding purposes in the welding of vertical butts when erecting side shell panels or for the vertical shell butt joints when joining building blocks on the berth or dock.
[줄 4150] [93.5%] (29/31) ✅ 유지 - For this purpose the use of a single- or double-vee butt with the electro-gas process is preferable since this permits completion of the weld manually if any breakdown occurs.
[줄 4151] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - A square butt with appreciable gap would be almost impossible to bridge manually.
[줄 4152] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - Laser welding Laser welding is being used in the shipbuilding industry and shows much promise as a welding process that offers low heat input and therefore minimum distortion of welded plates and stiffeners.
[줄 4153] [86.7%] (13/15) ✅ 유지 - For shipbuilding welding applications the laser source is either CO 2 or Nd:YAG crystals.
[줄 4154] [87.5%] (56/64) ✅ 유지 - Because of the wide range of applied powers and power densities available from Wire fed into pool Weld pool Slag ELECTRO-SLAG WELDING Molten metal Cooling water Weld direction IN OUT Copper shoe Completed weld Wire guide nozzle Water-cooled copper shoe Weld ELECTRO-GAS WELDING CO 2 Wire feed Arc Electrode wire CO 2 Figure 9.8 Electro-gas and electro-slag welding.
[줄 4155] [87.5%] (7/8) ✅ 유지 - Nd:YAG lasers, different welding methods are possible.
[줄 4156] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - If the laser is in pulsed mode and the surface temperature is below boiling point, heat transfer is predominantly by conduction and a conduction limited weld is produced.
[줄 4157] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - If the applied power is higher, boiling begins in the weld pool and a deep penetration weld can be formed.
[줄 4158] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - After the pulse, the material flows back into the cavity and solidifies.
[줄 4159] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Both these methods can be used to produce spot welds or 'stake' welds.
[줄 4160] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Laser 'stake welding' has been used in shipbuilding, stiffening members being welded to plate panels from the plate side only.
[줄 4161] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - A seam weld is produced by a sequence of overlapping deep penetration 'spot' welds or by the formation of a continuous molten weld pool.
[줄 4162] [91.7%] (11/12) ✅ 유지 - Pulsed laser welding is normally used at thicknesses below about 3 mm.
[줄 4163] [75.0%] (15/20) ✅ 유지 - Higher power continuous-wave Nd:YAG lasers are capable of keyholetype welding materials from 0.8 to 15 mm thickness.
[줄 4164] [93.3%] (14/15) ✅ 유지 - Nd:YAG lasers can be used on a wide range of steels and aluminum alloys.
[줄 4165] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - Also, because of the possibility of using fiber-optic beam delivery, Nd:YAG lasers are often used in conjunction with articulated arm robots for welding fabricated units of complex shape.
[줄 4166] [93.5%] (29/31) ✅ 유지 - Since the beam can burn the skin or severely damage the eyes, Nd:YAG lasers require enclosures within the fabrication shop that are fully opaque to the Nd:YAG laser wavelength.
[줄 4167] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - Hybrid laser–arc welding is also used in the shipbuilding industry, this being a combination of laser and arc welding that produces deep penetration welds with good tolerance to poor joint fit-up.
[줄 4168] [91.7%] (11/12) ✅ 유지 - The Nd:YAG laser is combined with a metal arc welding gas.
[줄 4169] [96.3%] (26/27) ✅ 유지 - Thermit welding This is a very useful method of welding that may be used to weld together large steel sections, for example parts of a stern frame.
[줄 4170] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - It is in fact often used to repair castings or forgings of this nature.
[줄 4171] [75.0%] (9/12) ✅ 유지 - Thermit welding is basically a fusion process, the required heat beingevolvedfroma mixtureofpowderedaluminumandironoxide.
[줄 4172] [89.5%] (17/19) ✅ 유지 - Theendsofthepart to be welded are initially built into a sand or graphite mold, whilst the mixture is poured intoarefractorylinedcrucible.
[줄 4173] [87.5%] (7/8) ✅ 유지 - Ignitionofthismixtureisobtainedwiththeaidofahighly inflammable powder consisting mostly of barium peroxide.
[줄 4174] [92.6%] (25/27) ✅ 유지 - During the subsequent reaction within the crucible the oxygen leaves the iron oxide and combines with the aluminum producing aluminum oxide, or slag, and superheated thermit steel.
[줄 4175] [80.0%] (16/20) ✅ 유지 - This steel isrun intothe mold, where itpreheats and eventually fuses and mixeswith the ends of the parts to be joined.
[줄 4176] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - On cooling a continuous joint is formed and the mold is removed.
[줄 4177] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - Friction stir welding 1 Friction stir welding is a relatively new materials joining process that has been used in the shipbuilding industry and is likely to be more widely used.
[줄 4178] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Friction stir welding is a solid-state process that offers advantages over fusion welding for certain applications.
[줄 4179] [91.9%] (34/37) ✅ 유지 - In producing butt joints it uses a nonconsumable rotating tool, the profiled pin of which is plunged into the butted joint of two plates 1 Friction stir welding was invented and patented by TWI Ltd. Cambridge, UK.
[줄 4180] [100.0%] (6/6) ✅ 유지 - and then moves along the joint.
[줄 4181] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - The plate material is softened in both plates and forced around the rotating profiled pin, resulting in a solid-state bond between the two plates.
[줄 4182] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - To contain the softened material in the line of the joint, a backing bar is used and the tool shoulder under pressure retains material at the upper surface.
[줄 4183] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Both plates and the backing bar require substantial clamping because of the forces involved.
[줄 4184] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Plates of different thickness may be butt welded by inclining the rotating tool.
[줄 4185] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - The process is currently used for welding aluminum alloy plates and such plates to aluminum alloy extrusions or castings.
[줄 4186] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - Dissimilar aluminum alloys may be joined by the process.
[줄 4187] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - A suitable material for a rotating tool to permit friction stir welding of steel has yet to be developed.
[줄 4188] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - Typical applications of friction stir welding are the construction of aluminum alloy deck panels for high-speed craft from extruded sections and aluminum alloy honeycomb panels for passenger ship cabin bulkheads.

[줄 4191] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - Cutting processes Steel plates and sections were mostly cut to shape in shipyards using a gas cutting technique, but the introduction of competitive plasma-arc cutting machines has led to their widespread use in shipyards today.
[줄 4192] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Gas cutting Gas cutting is achieved by what is basically a chemical/thermal reaction occurring with iron and iron alloys only.
[줄 4193] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Iron or its alloys may be heated to a temperature at which the iron will rapidly oxidize in an atmosphere of high purity oxygen.
[줄 4194] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - The principle of the process as applied to the cutting of steel plates and sections in shipbuilding is as follows.
[줄 4195] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Over a small area the metal is preheated to a given temperature, and a confined stream of oxygen is then blown onto this area.
[줄 4196] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - The iron is then oxidized in a narrow band, and the molten oxide and metal are removed by the kinetic energy of the oxygen stream.
[줄 4197] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - A narrow parallel sided gap is then left between the cut edges.
[줄 4198] [100.0%] (46/46) ✅ 유지 - Throughout the cutting operation the preheat flame is left on to heat the top of the cut since most of the heat produced by the reaction at the cutting front is not instantaneous, and tends to be liberated at the lower level of the cut only.
[줄 4199] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Alloying elements in small amounts are dissolved in the slag and removed when cutting steel.
[줄 4200] [93.3%] (14/15) ✅ 유지 - However, if they are present in large quantities, alloying elements, especially chromium, will retard andevenpreventcutting.
[줄 4201] [94.4%] (17/18) ✅ 유지 - Thereasonforthisisthattheyeitherdecreasethefluidityofthe slag or produce a tenacious oxide film over the surface which prevents further oxidation of the iron.
[줄 4202] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - This may be overcome by introducing an iron rich powder into the cutting area, a process often referred to as 'powder cutting'.
[줄 4203] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - When cutting stainless steels which have a high chromium content 'powder cutting' would be employed.
[줄 4204] [96.9%] (31/32) ✅ 유지 - Generally acetylene is used with oxygen to provide the preheat flame but other gases can be used: propane for example or hydrogen which is used for underwater work because of its compressibility.
[줄 4205] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Apart from the torch, the equipment is similar to that for gas welding.
[줄 4206] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - The torch has valves for controlling the volume of acetylene and oxygen provided for the preheat flame, and it has a separate valve for controlling the oxygen jet.
[줄 4207] [94.7%] (18/19) ✅ 유지 - The oxyacetylene cutting process has been highly automated for use in shipyards; these developments are considered in Chapter 13.
[줄 4208] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Hand burning with an oxyacetylene flame is used extensively for small jobbing work, and during the fabrication and erection of units.
[줄 4209] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Plasma-arc cutting Plasma in this sense is a mass of ionized gas which will conduct electricity.
[줄 4210] [100.0%] (36/36) ✅ 유지 - An electrode is connected to the negative terminal of a DC supply and a gas shield is supplied for the arc from a nozzle which has a bore less than the natural diameter of the arc.
[줄 4211] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - As a result a constricted arc is obtained which has a temperature considerably higher than that of an open arc.
[줄 4212] [95.0%] (19/20) ✅ 유지 - The arc is established between the electrode and workpiece when the ionized conducting gas comes into contact with the work.

[줄 4217] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - The hull form of a ship may be defined by a number of dimensions and terms that are often referred to during and after building the vessel.
[줄 4218] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - An explanation of the principal terms is given below: After Perpendicular :
[줄 4219] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - A perpendicular drawn to the waterline at the point where the after side of the rudder post meets the summer load line.
[줄 4220] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Where no rudder post is fitted it is taken as the center line of the rudder stock.
[줄 4221] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Forward Perpendicular : A perpendicular drawn to the waterline at the point where the fore-side of the stem meets the summer load line.
[줄 4222] [100.0%] (3/3) ✅ 유지 - Length Between Perpendiculars :
[줄 4223] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - The length between the forward and aft perpendiculars measured along the summer load line.
[줄 4224] [100.0%] (10/10) ✅ 유지 - Amidships : A point midway between the after and forward perpendiculars.
[줄 4225] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - Length Overall : Length of vessel taken over all extremities.
[줄 4226] [81.2%] (13/16) ✅ 유지 - Lloyd's Length : Used for obtaining scantlings if the vessel is classed with Lloyd's Register.
[줄 4227] [93.9%] (31/33) ✅ 유지 - It is the same as length between perpendiculars except that it must not be less than 96% and need not be more than 97% of the extreme length on the summer load line.
[줄 4228] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - If the ship has an unusual stem or stern arrangement the length is given special consideration.
[줄 4229] [100.0%] (48/48) ✅ 유지 - Register Length : The length of ship measured from the fore-side of the head of the stem to the aft side of the head of the stern post or, in the case of a ship not having a stern post, to the fore-side of the rudder stock.
[줄 4230] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - If the ship does not have a stern post or a rudder stock, the after terminal is taken to the aftermost part of the transom or stern of the ship.
[줄 4231] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - This length is the official length in the register of ships maintained by the flag state and appears on official documents relating to ownership and other matters concerning the business of the ship.
[줄 4232] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Another important length measurement is what might be referred to as the IMO Length.
[줄 4233] [93.3%] (28/30) ✅ 유지 - This length is found in various international conventions such as the Load Line, Tonnage, SOLAS and MARPOL conventions, and determines the application of requirements of those conventions to a ship.
[줄 4234] [88.2%] (15/17) ✅ 유지 - It is defined as 96% of the total length on a waterline at 85% of Ship Construction.

[줄 4236] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - This gas is ionized in the first place by a subsidiary electrical discharge between the electrode and the nozzle.
[줄 4237] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - Plates are cut by the high-temperature concentrated arc melting the material locally.
[줄 4238] [100.0%] (13/13) ✅ 유지 - The plasma-arc process may be used for cutting all electrically conductive materials.
[줄 4239] [76.2%] (16/21) ✅ 유지 - Cutting units are available with cutting currents of 20–1000 amps to cut plates with thicknesses of 0.6–150 mm.
[줄 4240] [100.0%] (37/37) ✅ 유지 - The plasma carrier gas may be compressed air, nitrogen, oxygen, or argon/hydrogen to cut mild or high alloy steels, and aluminum alloys, the more expensive argon/hydrogen mixture being required to cut the greater thickness sections.
[줄 4241] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - A water-injection plasma-arc cutting system is available for cutting materials up to 75 mm thick using nitrogen as the carrier gas.
[줄 4242] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - A higher cutting speed is possible and pollution minimized with the use of water and an exhaust system around the torch.
[줄 4243] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Water cutting tables were often used with plasma-arc cutting, but more recent systems have dispensed with underwater cutting.
[줄 4244] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Cutting in water absorbed the dust and particulate matter and reduced the plasma noise and ultraviolet radiation of earlier plasma cutters.
[줄 4245] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - Gouging Both gas and arc welding processes may be modified to produce means of gouging out shallow depressions in plates to form edge preparations for welding purposes where precision is not important.
[줄 4246] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Gouging is particularly useful in shipbuilding for cleaning out the backs of welds to expose clean metal prior to depositing a weld back run.
[줄 4247] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - The alternative to gouging for this task is mechanical chipping, which is slow and arduous.
[줄 4248] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Usually, where gouging is applied for this purpose, what is known as 'arc-air' gouging is used.
[줄 4249] [95.8%] (23/24) ✅ 유지 - A tubular electrode is employed, the electrode metal conducting the current and maintaining an arc of sufficient intensity to heat the workpiece to incandescence.
[줄 4250] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - Whilst the arc is maintained, a stream of oxygen is discharged from the bore of the electrode that ignites the incandescent electrode metal and the combustible elements of the workpiece.
[줄 4251] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - At the same time the kinetic energy of the excess oxygen removes the products of combustion, and produces a cut.
[줄 4252] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Held at an angle to the plate, the electrode will gouge out the unwanted material.
[줄 4253] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - A gas cutting torch may be provided with special nozzles that allow gouging to be accomplished when the torch is held at an acute angle to the plate.
[줄 4254] [90.0%] (18/20) ✅ 유지 - Laser cutting Profilecuttingandplaningathighspeedscanbeachievedwithaconcentratedlaserbeam and has increasingly been employed in a mechanized or robotic form in the shipbuilding industry in recentyears.
[줄 4255] [76.2%] (16/21) ✅ 유지 - Ina laserbeam the light isof onewavelength,travels inthe same direction, and is coherent, i.e all the waves are in phase.
[줄 4256] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - Such a beam can be focused to give high energy densities.
[줄 4257] [92.3%] (12/13) ✅ 유지 - For welding and cutting the beam is generated in a CO 2 laser.
[줄 4258] [96.0%] (24/25) ✅ 유지 - This consists of a tube filled with a mixture of CO 2, nitrogen, and helium that is made to fluoresce by a high-voltage discharge.
[줄 4259] [79.2%] (19/24) ✅ 유지 - The tube emits infrared radiation with a wavelength of about 1.6 m m and is capable of delivering outputs up to 20 kW.
[줄 4260] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - Laser cutting relies on keyholing to penetrate the thickness, and the molten metal is blown out of the hole by a gas jet.
[줄 4261] [96.6%] (28/29) ✅ 유지 - A nozzle is fitted concentric with the output from a CO 2 laser so that a gas jet can be directed at the work coaxial with the laser beam.
[줄 4262] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - The jet can be an inert gas, nitrogen, or in the case of steel, oxygen.
[줄 4263] [94.4%] (17/18) ✅ 유지 - With oxygen there is an exothermic reaction with the steel, giving additional heat as in oxy-fuel cutting.
[줄 4264] [95.7%] (22/23) ✅ 유지 - The thermal keyholing gives a narrow straight-sided cut compared with the normal cut obtained by other processes relying on a chemical reaction.
[줄 4265] [95.2%] (40/42) ✅ 유지 - Water jet cutting The cutting tool employed in this process is a concentrated water jet, with or without abrasive, which is released from a nozzle at 21⁄2 times the speed of sound and at a pressure level of several thousand bar.
[줄 4266] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - Water jet cutting can be used on a range of materials such as timber, plastics, rubber, etc. as well as steels and aluminum alloys.
[줄 4267] [75.0%] (18/24) ✅ 유지 - Mild steel from 0.25 to 150 mm in thickness and aluminum alloys from 0.5 to 250 mm in thickness can be cut.
[줄 4268] [100.0%] (19/19) ✅ 유지 - Being a cold cutting process the heat-affected zone, mechanical stresses, and distortion are left at the cut surface.
[줄 4269] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - Water jet cutting is slower than most thermal cutting processes and is not a portable machine tool.
[줄 4270] [86.7%] (13/15) ✅ 유지 - Further reading ESAB advances in welding and cutting technology, The Naval Architect, July/August 2003.
[줄 4271] [83.3%] (10/12) ✅ 유지 - Exploiting friction-stir welding of aluminium, The Naval Architect, July/August 2004.

[줄 4279] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - The strongest welded joint that may be produced in two plates subsequently subjected to a tensile pull is the butt joint.
[줄 4280] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - A butt joint is one where the two joined plates are in the same plane, and in any welded structure it is desirable that butt joints should be used wherever possible.
[줄 4281] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - In mild steel the weld metal tends to have a higher yield strength than the plate material.
[줄 4282] [100.0%] (29/29) ✅ 유지 - Under tension it is found that initial yielding usually occurs adjacent to a butt weld in the plate when the yield strength of the plate material is reached locally.
[줄 4283] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Since a good butt weld in tension has a strength equivalent to that of the mild steel plate, it is not considered as a line of structural weakness.
[줄 4284] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - Lapped joints, where fillet welds are used to connect the plates, should be avoided in strength members of a welded structure.
[줄 4285] [100.0%] (31/31) ✅ 유지 - As the fillet welds are in shear when the plates are in tension, the strength of the joint is very much less than that of the plate material or butt joint.
[줄 4286] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Fillet welds are unavoidable where sections or plates are connected at an angle to an adjacent plate, but often there is not the same problem as the loading is different.
[줄 4287] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - The fatigue strength of fillet welds is also inferior to that of a butt weld.
[줄 4288] [95.0%] (38/40) ✅ 유지 - Welding practice In making a butt weld with manual arc welding, where the plate thickness exceeds, say, 5–6 mm it will become necessary to make more than one welding pass to deposit sufficient weld metal to close the joint.

[줄 4294] [100.0%] (32/32) ✅ 유지 - In ship work unless a permanent backing bar is used, or a 'one-sided' welding technique or process is used, a back run of weld is required to ensure complete weld penetration.
[줄 4295] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - This is made on the reverse side of the joint after cleaning out the slag, etc. by chipping or gouging.
[줄 4296] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Permanent backing bars may conveniently be introduced where it is desired to weld from one side only during erection at the berth.
[줄 4297] [100.0%] (34/34) ✅ 유지 - A good example is the use of a cut-down channel bar used as a deck beam, the upper flange providing the backing bar for a deck panel butt weld, made by machine above.
[줄 4298] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - Tack welds are used throughout the construction to hold plates and sections in place after alignment and prior to completion of the full butt or fillet weld.
[줄 4299] [100.0%] (27/27) ✅ 유지 - These are short light runs of weld metal, which may be welded over, or cut out in more critical joints during the final welding of the joint.
[줄 4300] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Fillet welds may be continuous or intermittent depending on the structural effectiveness of the member to be welded.
[줄 4301] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - Where fillets are intermittent they may be either staggered or chain welded, the member may also be scalloped to give the same result when continuously welded.
[줄 4302] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - On thicker plates it becomes necessary to bevel the edges of plates that are to be butted together in order to achieve complete penetration of the weld metal.
[줄 4303] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - This operation may be carried out whilst profiling or trimming the plate edges, which must be aligned correctly.
[줄 4304] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Most edge preparations are made by gas or plasma heads having three nozzles out of phase that can be set at different angles to give the required bevels.
[줄 4305] [100.0%] (18/18) ✅ 유지 - Alternatively, the edge preparation may be obtained by mechanical machining methods using either a planing or milling tool.
[줄 4306] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - For very high quality welds in thick plate, particularly of the higher tensile types of steel, mechanical machining may well be specified.
[줄 4307] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - It is worth noting that there is little to choose between the two as far as metallurgical damage goes, but mechanical methods provide a better finish.
[줄 4308] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - Plates of varying thickness may be butt welded together at different locations, a good example being where heavy insert plates are fitted.
[줄 4309] [96.8%] (30/31) ✅ 유지 - Insert plates are preferred to doubling plates in welded construction, and the heavy plate is chamfered to the thickness of the adjacent thinner plate before the butt edge preparation is made.
[줄 4310] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - To ease the assembly of welded units it is common practice to make use of what is known as an 'egg box' construction.
