[줄 4326] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Welding distortion During the welding process the metal is heated, which causes expansion and the metal then contracts on cooling.
[줄 4327] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - The initial rapid heating causes the welded area to expand locally.
[줄 4328] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - The slower cooling of the weld causes the plate to move as the weld contracts.
[줄 4329] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - The result is a distortion of the part, and this is a major cause of extra work during assembly of units and construction of the ship.
[줄 4330] [100.0%] (17/17) ✅ 유지 - The need to adjust distorted parts so that they fit correctly can take considerable time and effort.
[줄 4331] [100.0%] (9/9) ✅ 유지 - In-plane distortion is basically shrinkage of the plate.
[줄 4332] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - For repeatable processes, which are usual in shipbuilding, the shrinkage can be measured and sufficient data built up to allow the shrinkage to be predicted.
[줄 4333] [100.0%] (30/30) ✅ 유지 - Computer-aided design systems can now include an allowance for shrinkage, so that the part as modeled in the system can then be adjusted during the generation of cutting information.
[줄 4334] [93.8%] (15/16) ✅ 유지 - The plates are cut oversized and the shrinkage after welding brings it to the correct size.
[줄 4335] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - More recently, work has been carried out to model shrinkage of more complex parts, for example structural webs with face flats.
[줄 4336] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - Again, these parts can then have their dimensions adjusted prior to cutting so that the effect of shrinkage is to bring them to the correct shape.
[줄 4337] [90.9%] (10/11) ✅ 유지 - Out-ofplane distortion is much more difficult to predict and manage.
[줄 4338] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - The cause is the same as in-plane shrinkage, but the distortion is often associated with fillet welds used to attach stiffeners to plates.
[줄 4339] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - The fillet welds, as they shrink, pull the plate out of plane, resulting in the typical appearance of a welded hull with indentations between the frames.
[줄 4340] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - The effect is much more noticeable for thin plate structures, for smaller ships, and for superstructures.
[줄 4341] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Restraining the plate during assembly and welding is one commonly used solution.
[줄 4342] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - The causes of distortion are complex and also include any residual stresses in the steel plate as a result of the steel mill rolling and cooling.
[줄 4343] [100.0%] (23/23) ✅ 유지 - Some of the stress may be relieved by rolling the plate prior to production, but distortion remains a significant problem for many shipbuilders.
[줄 4344] [96.7%] (29/30) ✅ 유지 - Welding sequences In order to minimize distortion in manual welding the 'backstep' and 'wandering' methods of welding are often used, the length of each step being the amount of weld
[줄 4345] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - metal laid down by an electrode to suit the required cross-section of weld.
[줄 4346] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - To reduce distortion and limit the residual stresses in the structure it is important that a correct welding sequence should be utilized throughout the construction.
[줄 4347] [100.0%] (16/16) ✅ 유지 - This applies both during the fabrication of units and at erection and joining on the berth.
[줄 4348] [100.0%] (25/25) ✅ 유지 - Of the more important welds in the construction of the ship the sequences involving welding of butts and seams in plating panels may be considered.

[줄 4355] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - Welding the seam first would cause high restraint across the plate strake and when the butt was finished a crack might occur.
[줄 4356] [100.0%] (24/24) ✅ 유지 - General practice when welding shell panels is to start by welding the central butts and then adjacent seams, working outwards both transversely and longitudinally.
[줄 4357] [100.0%] (28/28) ✅ 유지 - Ships' structural panels have various forms of stiffener attached to the plate panels, these generally being welded to the panel after completing the welding of the panel plates.
[줄 4358] [96.2%] (25/26) ✅ 유지 - These stiffening members are left unwelded across the butts and seams of the plates until these are completed, if they are attached at some intermediate stage.
[줄 4359] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Erection welding sequences generally follow the principles laid down for plating panels.
[줄 4360] [100.0%] (22/22) ✅ 유지 - In welded ships the lower side plating seams should not be welded before the upper seams, particularly the deck and gunwale seams.
[줄 4361] [100.0%] (33/33) ✅ 유지 - If this sequence of welding the side shell were adopted the upper portion of the hull structure would tend to be shortened, causing the hull to rise from the blocks at the ends.
[줄 4362] [100.0%] (26/26) ✅ 유지 - Where in modern construction the side shell and deck plating are erected in blocks and a suitable welding sequence is employed, this problem does not arise.
[줄 4363] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - In repair work correct welding sequences are also important, particularly where new material is fitted into the existing relatively rigid structure.
[줄 4364] [100.0%] (14/14) ✅ 유지 - Again, the procedure follows the general pattern for butts and seams in plate panels.
[줄 4365] [94.9%] (37/39) ✅ 유지 - If a new shell plate is to be welded in place the seams and butts in the surrounding structure are cut back 300–375 mm from the opening, likewise the connection of the stiffening in way of the opening.
[줄 4366] [93.8%] (30/32) ✅ 유지 - The inserted plate panel is then welded to within 300–375 mm of the free edges, the butts are completed, and then the seams after welding any longitudinal stiffening across the butts.
[줄 4367] [100.0%] (11/11) ✅ 유지 - Finally, the vertical framing is welded in way of the seams.
[줄 4368] [100.0%] (20/20) ✅ 유지 - Testing welds For economic reasons much of the weld testing carried out in shipbuilding is done visually by trained inspectors.
[줄 4369] [95.5%] (21/22) ✅ 유지 - Spot checks at convenient intervals are made on the more important welds in merchant ship construction, generally using radiographic or ultrasonic equipment.
[줄 4370] [96.0%] (24/25) ✅ 유지 - Welding materials are subjected to comprehensive tests before they are approved by Lloyd's Register or the other classification societies for use in ship work.
[줄 4371] [100.0%] (15/15) ✅ 유지 - Operatives are required to undergo periodical welder approval tests to ascertain their standard of workmanship.
[줄 4372] [100.0%] (12/12) ✅ 유지 - Weld faults Various faults may be observed in butt and fillet welds.
[줄 4373] [100.0%] (21/21) ✅ 유지 - These may be due to a number of factors: bad design, incorrect welding procedure, use of wrong materials, and bad workmanship.
[줄 4374] [75.0%] (6/8) ✅ 유지 - Different faults are illustrated in Figure 10.5.
[줄 4375] [96.8%] (30/31) ✅ 유지 - The judgment of the seriousness of the fault rests with the weld inspector and surveyor, and where the weld is considered to be unacceptable it will be cut out and rewelded.
